hetuhi kehi vira Tadāha sabbaññuvaro mahesī ānanandabhaddaṃ madhurassarenaYe pubba buddhesu katādhikārā aladdhamokkha jinasāsanesu Teneva sambodhimukhena dhīrā ajjhāsayenāpi mahābalenaPaññāya teje sutikkhapaññā sabaññubhavaṃ anupāpuṇanti Ahampi pubbabuddhesu buddhattamabhipatthayiṃManasāyeva hutvāna dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā Atha buddhāpadānāni suṇātha suddhamānasāTiṃsapāramisampuṇṇā dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā Sambodhiṃ buddhaseṭṭhānaṃ sasaṅghe lokatāyakeDasaṅguli namassitvā sirasā abivādayiṃ Yāvatā buddhakhettesu ratanā vijjantasaṅkhiyāĀkāsaṭṭhā ca bhummaṭṭhā manasā sabbamāhariṃ Ādito paṭhāya imā canasso gāthāyo  potthakesu santi  Catutthagāthāya dutiyadedhāce pañcamagāthāya paṭhamandho ca syāmapotthake na santi  Dhīrā se  Sabba se Tenidha se  Abhivādaye se  Māhare  se  Tattha rūpiyabhumiyaṃ pāsādaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃNekabhummaṃ ratanamayaṃ ubbiddhaṃ nabhamuggataṃ Vicittathambhaṃ sukataṃ suvibhatta ṃmahārahaṃKanakāmayasaṅghāṭaṃ toraṇacchattamaṇḍitaṃ Paṭhamā veḷuriyā bhumi vimalābbhasamā subhāNalīni jalajākiṇaṇavarakañcanabhumiyā Pavāḷaṃsā pavāḷavaṇaṇā kāci lohitakā subhāIndagopakavaṇṇāhā bhumi obhāsati disā Suvibhattā gharamukhā niyyuhā sīhapañajarāCaturo vedikā jālagandhāvela manoramā Nīlā pītā lobhitā odātā suddhakāḷakāKūṭāgāravarūpetā satatratanabhusitā  Olokamayā padumā vāḷa  vihagasobhitāNakkhattatārakākiṇṇā candasuriyehi maṇḍitā Hemajālena sañachannā soṇṇa  kiṅkiṇikāyutāVātavegena kujanti soṇṇamālā manoramā Mañjeṭṭhakaṃ lohitakaṃ pitakaṃ haripiñjaraṃNānāraṅgehi suppitaṃ ussitaddhajamāliniṃ Nānā bahu nekasatā phaḷikā rajatāmayāMaṇimayā lohitaṅkā masāragallamayā tathāKākādavakaniñcittā saṇhakāsikasatthatā Kambalā dukulā cinā patatuṇṇā paṇḍupāvurāVividhattharaṇaṃ sabbaṃ manasā paññapesahaṃ Tāsu tāsveva bhumisu ratanakuṭalaṅkatāMaṇiverācanā ukkā dhārayantā sutiṭṭhare Sobhanti esikāthambhā subhā kañcanatoraṇāJamebānadā sāramayā atho rajatamayāpi ca Kenā sandhi suvibhattā kavāṭaggaḷacittitāUbhato puṇṇaghaṭānekā padumuppalaṃyutā Atite sababbuddhe ca sasaṃghe lokanāyakePakativaṇaṇarūpena nimminitvā sasāvake Māpaye  se  Kekabhumiṃ   Saṅghātaṃ ma  Kontacchattehi maṇḍitaṃ ma Nalina ma  Pavāḷaṃsa   Gandhavelā   Vibhusitā   Olokayamayā se Candasurehi ma se  Vivittattharaṇaṃ  Paññapemahaṃ se   Nekāsanti a muse  Tena dvārena pavisitvā sabbe buddhā sasāvakāSabbasovaṇṇaye pīṭhe nisinnā ariyamaṇḍalā Ye ca etarahi atthi buddhā loke anuttarāAtitā vatatamānā ca bhavanaṃ sabbe samāruhuṃ Paccekakhuddhe nekasate sayambhu aparājiteAtite vattamāne ca bhavanaṃ sabbe samāruhuṃ Kapparukkhā bahu atthi ye dibbā ye ca mānusāSabbaṃ dussaṃ samāhatvā acchādemi ticivarā Khajjaṃ bhojjaṃ sāyaniyaṃ sampannaṃ pānabhojanaṃMaṇimaye pubhe patte sampuretvā adāsasahaṃ Dibbacakkhusamā hutvā maṭṭhacivarasaṃyutā Madhunā sakkharā ceva telena madhuphāṇitā Tappitā paramannena sabbe te ariyamaṇḍalā Ratanāgabbhaṃ pavisitvā kesariva guhāsayā Mahārahamhi sayane sīhaseyyamakappayuṃSampajānā samuḍhāya sayane pallaṅkamābhujuṃGocaraṃ sabbabuddhānaṃ jhānaratisamappitā Aññe dhammāni desenti aññe kiḷanti indhiyāAññe abhiññā appenti abhiññāvasibhāvitāVikubbanā vikubbanti aññe nekasahassiyo Buddhāpi buddhe pucchanti visayaṃ sabbaññumālayaṃGambhiraṃ nipuṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ paññāya vinikhujjhare Sāvakā buddhe pucchanti buddhā pucchanti sāvakeAññamaññaṃ ca pucchanti aññoññaṃ byākaronti te Buddhā paccekabuddhā ca sāvakā paricārakāEvaṃ sakāya ratiyā pāsāde bhiramanti te Chattā tiṭṭhantu ratanā kañcanāvelapantikāMuttājālaparikkhittā sabbe dhārentu matthake Bhavantu ceḷavitānā soṇṇatārakacitatināVicittamālyavitānā sabbe dhārentu matthake Vitatā mālyadāmehi gandhadāmehi sobhitāDussadāmehi parikiṇṇā ratanadāmavibhusitā Atite ma  Samāhariṃ mu a  Cattamānā ma  Samāhariṃ mu a  Acchādesiṃ  Sabbanta se ma  Maṭhā se ma a  Anekasatasahassiyo se aññeneka sahassiyo  se Evaṃ ratisurammānā  se  Suvaṇṇajālābhi saṃyuttaṃ rajatajālamaṇihi ca  Muttajālaparikkhittaṃ chattaṃ   Dhārenti se  Vicittā malya    soṇṇamayeaṭṭhakathā  Pupphābhikiṇṇā sucittā surabhigandhudhupitā Gandhapañcaṅgulikatā hemacchadanachāditā Catuddisā pokkharañño padumuppalasanthatāSovaṇṇarūpā khāyantu padumareṇurajaggatā Pupphanatu pādapā sabbe pāsādasasa samantatoSayaṃ ca pupphā ñcitvā gantvā bhavanamokiruṃ Sikhino tattha naccantu dibbahaṃsā pakujareKaravikā ca gāyantu dijasaṃghā samantato Bheriyo sabbā vajjantu viṇā sabbā ravantu tāSabbā saṃgini vattantu pāsādassa samantato  Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi cakkavāḷe tato pareMahantā jotisampannā acchiddā ratanāmāya Niṭṭhantu soṇṇapalalaṅkā diparukkhā jalantu teBhavantu ekapajjotā dasasahassiparamparā Gaṇikā lāsikā ceva naccantu accharāgaṇāNānāraṅgā padissantu pāsādassa samantato Dumagge pabbatagge vā sinerugirimuddhaniUssāpemi dhajaṃ sabbaṃ vicittaṃ pañcavaṇṇikaṃ Narā nāgā ca gandhabbā sabbe devā apentu teNamassantā pañajalikā pāsādaṃ parivārayuṃ Yaṃ kiñci kusalaṃ kammaṃ kattabbaṃ kiriyaṃ mamaKāyena vācā manasā tidase sukataṃ kataṃ Ye sattā saññino atthi ye ca sattā asaññinoKataṃ puññaphalaṃ mayhaṃ sabbe bhāgi bhavantu te Yesaṃ kataṃ suviditaṃ dinnaṃ puññaphalaṃ mayāYe ca tasmiṃ na jānanti devā gananvā nivedayuṃ Sababalokambhi ye sattā jivantāhārahetukāManuññaṃ bhojanaṃ sabbaṃ labhantu mama tejasā Manasā dānaṃ māya dinnaṃ manasā pāsādamāvahiṃ Pujitā sabbasambuddhā paccekā jinasāvakā Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagañachahaṃ Ave bhave pajānāmi devatte atha mānuseAññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi manasā patthanāphalaṃ Bhusitā se  Gulaṅkitā se  Chadanamālikā se  Gandhā   Motaruṃ se  Rasantuma  Sabbe    Cetasā  se  Māpayiṃ se  Devānaṃ adhiko homi bhavāmi manujādhipoRūpalakkhaṇasampanno paññāya asamo bhave Bhojanaṃ vividhaṃ seṭhaṃ ratanañca anappakaṃNānāvidhāni vatthāni nabhā khippaṃ upenti maṃ Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi dibbā bhakkhā upenati maṃ Pathavyāpabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi ratanā sabba upenati maṃ  Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabba gandhā upenati maṃ Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabba yānā upenati maṃ Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbā mālā upenati maṃ Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi alaṅkārā upenati maṃ Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbā kaññāupenati maṃ Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi upenati madhusakkharā Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vaneYaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabba khajjā upenati maṃ Adhane addhikajane yācake ca pathāvinoDadāmahaṃ dānavaraṃ sambodhivarapattiyā Nādento pabbataṃ selaṃ gajjento bahalaṃ giriṃSadevalokaṃ hāsento buddho loke bhavāmahaṃ Disā dasavidhā loke yāyato natthi antakaṃTasmiñca disābhāgambhi buddhakkhettā asaṅkhiyā Pabhā pakittinā mayhaṃ yamakā raṃsivāhanāEtthantare raṃsijālaṃ āloko vipulo bhave Etatake lokadhātumbhi sabbe passantu maṃ janāSabbe ca sumanā hontu sabbe maṃ anuvattare Sabbe maṃ anuvattanti yāva brahmanivesanaṃ  Vissaṭṭha madhunādena amataṃ bherimāhaniṃEthentare janā sabbe suṇantu madhuraṃ giraṃ Dhammameghe pavassanne sabbe hontu anāsavāYettha pacchimakā sattā sotāpannā bhavantu te Datvā dātabbakaṃ dānaṃ sīlaṃ puretvasesatoNekkhamme pāramiṃ gantvā patto sambodhimuttamaṃ  Paṇḍite paripucchitvā katvā viriyamuttamaṃKhantiyā pāramiṃ gantvā patto sambodhimuttamaṃ Katvā daḷhamadhiṭṭhānaṃ puretvā saccapāramiṃMettāya pāramiṃ gantvā patetā sambodhimuttamaṃ Lābhālābhe sukhe sukkhe sammāne cāvamānaneSabbattha samako hutvā patto sambodhimuttamaṃ Vividhāni ca ma se  Puthavyā   Me   Yammekataṃ   Gacchento ma Sadevakaṃ hāsayanto ma se  Khette ma  Visiṭṭha   Māhane  se  Patvā  Saccamadhiṭana   Saccapārami puriya ma se  Ca vimānane ma   potthekesu dissati  Addhacandakatihi anakariko bhāgo marammapotthakesu cevaseluttarārāmapotthake ca dissati  Kosajjaṃ bhayato disvā viriyañcāpi khematoĀraddhaviriyā hotha esā buddhānusāsanī Vivādaṃ bhayato disvā avivādañca khematoSamaggā sakhilā hotha esā buddhānusāsani Pamādaṃ bhayato disvā appamādaṃ ca khematoBhavethaṭṭhaṅgikaṃ maggaṃ esā buddhānusāsani Samāgatā bahu buddhā arahantā ca sabbasoSambuddhe arahante ca vandamānā namassatha Evaṃ acintiyā buddhā buddhadhammā acintiyāAcintiyesu pasannānaṃ vipāko hoti acintiyoItthaṃ sudaṃ bhagavā attano buddacariyaṃ sambhāvayamāna beddhāpadāniyaṃ nāmadhammapariyāyaṃ abhāsitthāni Buddhāpadānaṃ samantaṃ   Pacceka buddhāpadānaṃAtha paccekkhuddhāpadānaṃ suṇātha Tathāgataṃ jevane vasantaṃ apucchi vedehamuni nataṅgoPaccekabuddhā kira nāma honti bhavanti te hetuhi kehi vīra Tadāha sabbaññuvaro mahesī ānandabhaddaṃ madhurassarenaYe pubbabuddhesu katādhikārā aladdhamokkhā jinasāsanesu Teneva saṃvegamukhena dhīrā vināpi buddhehi sutikkhapaññāĀrammaṇenāpi paritatakena pacekabodhiṃ anupāpuṇanti Sabbamhi lokamhi mamaṃ ṭhapetvā paccekabuddhehi samova natthiTesaṃ imaṃ vaṇaṇapadesamattaṃ vakkhāmahaṃ sādhu mahāmuninaṃ Sayameva buddhānaṃ mahāisīnaṃ sādhuni vākyāni madhuṃva khuddaṃAnuttaraṃ bhesajaṃ patthayanatā suṇātha sabbesu pasannacittā Paccekabuddhānaṃ samāgatānaṃ paramparavyākaraṇāni yāniĀdīnavo yañca virāgavatthu yathā ca bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu Akosajjaṃ ca se  Buddhacaritaṃ ma  Sabbabuddhesu  mase Mahesinaṃ ma  Madhuñca  madhuva ma  Sahagatānaṃ ma   Saṃrāgavatthusu virāgasaññi rattambhi lokambhi virattacittāHitvā papañce vijiya endināni tatheva bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu Sabbesu bhutesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ aviheṭhayaṃ aññatarampi tesaṃMettena cittena hitānukampi eko vare khaggavisāṇakappo Sabbesu bhutesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ aviheṭhayaṃ aññatarampi tesaṃNamettena cittena hitānukampi eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Saṃsaggajātassa bhavanti senahā senahanvayaṃ dukkhamidaṃ pahotiĀdinaṃ senahajaṃ pekkhamāno eko vare khaggavisāṇakappo Mitte subhajje anukampamāno hāpeti atthaṃ paṭibaddhacittoEtaṃ bhayaṃ panthave pakkhemāno eko vare khaggavisāṇakappo Vaṃso visālova yathā visanettā puttesu dāresu ca yā apekkhāVaṃsakaḷirova asajjamāno eko care khagagavisāṇakappo Migo araññambhi yathā abaddho ye nicchakaṃ gacchati gocarāyaViññu naro seritaṃ pekkhamāno eko vare khaggavisāṇakappo Āmantanā hoti sabāyamajjhe va ca ṭhāne gamane cārikāyaAnabhijjhitaṃ seritaṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Khiḍḍhā rati hoti sahāyamajjhe puttesu pemaṃ vipulañca hoti Piyavippayogaṃ vijigucchamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Cātuddiso appaṭigho ca hoti santussamāno itaritarenaParissayānaṃ sabhitā achambhi eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Sarāgavatthūsu  ma se  Papañcaṃ   Jita endanāni   Tattheva  ayaṃ gāthā marammapotthake ca suttanipāte ca na vajjati Vāse mu a  Piyababiyogaṃ ma  Dussaṅgahā pabbajitāpi eke atho gahaṭṭhā gharamāvasantāApposukko paraputtesu hutvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Oropayitvā gibhibyañajanāni saṃsinapatto yatā koviḷāroChenvāna viro gigibandhanāni eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Sace labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ saddhiṃvaraṃ sādhuvihāri dhiraṃAbhibhuyya sabbāni parisasyāni careyya tenattamano satimā No ce labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ saddhiṃvaraṃ sādhuvihāri dhiraṃRājāva raṭṭhaṃ vijitaṃ pahāya eko care mātaṅga raññeva nāgo Addhā pasaṃsāma sabhāyasampadaṃ seṭṭhā samā sevitabbā sabhāyāEte aladdhā anavajjabhoja eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Disvā suvaṇaṇasasa pabhassarāni kammāraputtena suniṭṭhitāniSaṃghaṭṭamānāni duve bhujasmiṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Evaṃ dutiyena sabhā mamassa vācābhilāpo abhisajjanā caEtaṃ bhayaṃ āyatiṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo  Kāmā hi citrā madhurā manoramā virūparūpena mathetti cittaṃĀdinavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Īti ca gaṇḍo ca upadadavo ca rogo ca sallañca bhañcametaṃEtaṃ bhayaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo Sitañca aṇhañca khudaṃ pipāsaṃ vātātape ḍaṃsasiriṃsape caSabbāni petāni abhibbhavitvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo tappayanti mahodadhiṃ Tathevā yaṃ sāriputetā sake tisu visāradoPaññāya pāramiṃ gananvā tappayissati pāṇino Himavantaṃ upādāya sāgarañca mahosadadhiṃEtthantare yaṃ pulinaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ Tampi sakkā asesena saṅkhātuṃ gaṇanā yathāNa tveva sāriputtassa paññāya nto bhavissati Sabbesu the  Devakāyā mu a  Parivārenti taṃ   Taṃ   Phasulā  Pacchime bhavasampatte ma the  Koṭiṃ ma the Appameyya ma  Bhāgirasi ma   Sāke tisu ma the a  Lakkhe ṭhapiyamānambhi khiye gaṅgāya vālukāNa tveva sāriputtassa paññāya nto bhavissati Mahāsamudde ūmiyo gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyāTatheva sāriputtasasa paññāyanto na hessati Ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃPaññāya pāramiṃ gantvā hessati agagasāvako Pavattinaṃ dhammacakkaṃ sakyaputtena tādināAnuvantessani sammā vassento dhamamavuṭṭhiyota Sabbametaṃ sabbaṃ vyādhito parimuttiyā Asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto nibbāṇaṃ amataṃ padaṃAbbokiṇṇaṃ pañcasataṃ pabbajiṃ isipabbajaṃ Jaṭibhārena bharito ajinuttaranivāsanoAbhiññāpāramiṃ gantvā brahmalokaṃ agacchahaṃ  Natthi bāhirake suddhi ṭhapetvā jinasāsanaṃVe keci buddhimā sattā sujjhanti jinasāsane Attakāramayaṃ etaṃ nayidaṃ itihitihaṃ Adaṅkhataṃ gavesanto kutitthaṃ sañcariṃ ahaṃ Anuvattisasti sadadhammaṃ ma the  Vassanto ma the  se Dhanaṃ ma the  Avyakiṇṇaṃ   Nivāsaha ma  se Bāhiyake the  Atthakāmaṃ mamaṃ  se  Itihaṃ tadā  se  Yathā sāratthiko poso kadaliṃ chetvāna phālayeNa tattha sāraṃ vindeyya sārena ritatako hi so Tatheva titthiyā loke nānādiṭṭhi bahujjanāAsaṅkhatena rittāse sārena kadali yathā Pacchīmabhave sampatte brahmabandhu ahosahaṃMahābhogaṃ chaḍḍhayitvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ sappaññaṃ muniṃ mone samāhitaṃSantacittaṃ mahānāgaṃ suphullaṃ padumaṃ yathā Disvā me cittamuppajji sudannaṃ suddhamānasaṃUsabhaṃ pavaraṃ viraṃ arahā yaṃ bhavissati Pāsādiko iriyati abhirūpo susaṃvutoUttame damathe danto amatadassi bhavissati Yannunāhaṃ uttamatthaṃ puccheyyaṃ tuṭṭhamānasaṃSo me puṭṭhā kathessati paṭipucchāma haṃ tadā Piṇḍapātaṃ carantassa pacchato agamāsahaṃOkāsaṃ paṭimānetto pucchituṃ amataṃ padaṃ Vithantare anuppatataṃ upagantvāna pucchahaṃKathaṃ gottosi tvaṃ vīra kassa sissosi mārisa So me puṭṭhā viyākāsi asambhitova kesarīBuddho loke samuppanto tasasa sissombhi āvuso  Kidisaṃ te mahāvīra anujāta mahāyasa Buddhassa sāsanaṃ dhammaṃ Sādhu me kathayassu bho Rittāva   Pacchime bhava ma the  Koṭiyo sataṃ  Sadā   Tamaddasāhaṃ ma the tamaddasāmi se  Vitatimuppajji ma the Anomadassi ma  Piṇḍacāraṃ   Vithintare ma the  Ajambhitova the Mahāyaso   So me puṭṭhā kathi sabbaṃ gambhiraṃ nipuṇaṃ padaṃTaṇhāsallassa bhantāraṃ sabbadukkhāpanudanaṃ Ye dhammā hetuppabhavā tesaṃ hetuṃ tathāgato āhaTesañca yo nirodho evaṃvādi mahāsamaṇo Sohaṃ vissajjite pañeha paṭhamaṃ phalamajjhagaṃVirajo vimalo āsiṃ sutvāna jinasāsanaṃ Sutvāna munino vākyaṃ passitvā dhammamuttamaṃPariyogāḷhasaddhammo ima gāthaṃ abhāsahaṃ Eso va dhammo yadi tāvadeva paccabyathā padamasokaṃAdiṭṭhaṃ abbhathītaṃ bahukehi kappanahutehi Svāhaṃ dhammaṃ gavesanto kutitthe sañcariṃ ahaṃSo me attho anuppatto kālo me nappamajjituṃ Tosikohaṃ assajinā patvāna acalaṃ padaṃSahāyakaṃ gavesanto assamaṃ agamāsabhaṃ Duratova mamaṃ disvā sahāyo me susikkhitoIriyāpathasampanno idaṃ vacanamabravi Pasannamukhanettosi munibhāvova dissatiAmatādhigato kacci nibbāṇaṃ accutaṃ padaṃ Subhānurūpo āyāsi āneñajakārito viyaDantova dantadamathe upasantosi brāhmaṇa Amataṃ mayā adhigataṃ sokasallapanudanaṃ Tvampi taṃ adhigacchāhi gacchāma buddhasantikaṃ Sādhuti so paṭissutvā sahāyo me susikkhitoHatthena hatthaṃ gaṇhitvā upāgami tava ntikaṃ Kathaṃ ma  Dukkha  ma the  Bahuhi ma  Ariyāpathaṃ mama disvā ma the Dannovuttamadamathe mu a  Salla visodhanaṃ the sallavinodāṃ  se Adhigacchasi ma  se  Sādhuni paṭisuṇitvā ma the se  Upagamma ma Santhusantikaṃ   Ubhopi pabbajissāma sakyaputta tavantike Tava sāsanamāgamama viharāma anāsavā Kolito iddhiyā seṭṭho ahaṃ paññāya pāragoUbhova ekato hutvā sāsanaṃ sobhayāmase  Apariyositasaṅkappo kutitthe sañcariṃ ahaṃTava dassanamāgamma saṅkappo purito mama Paṭhaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya pupphanti samaye dumāDibbagandhā sampavanti nosenti sabbapāṇinaṃ Tathevāhaṃ mahāvīra sakyaputta mahāyasaSāsane te patiṭṭhāya samayesāmi pupphituṃ Vimuttipupphaṃ esanto bhavasaṃsāramocanaṃVimuttipupphalābhena tosemi sabbapāṇinaṃ Yāvatā buddhakhettambhi ṭhapetvāna mahāmuniṃPaññāya sadiso natthi tava puttassa cakkhuma Suvinitā ca te sissā parisā ca susikkhitāUttame damathe dantā parivārenti taṃ sadā Jhāyī jhānaratā dhīrā santacittā samāhitāMunī moneyyasampannā parivārenti taṃ sadā Appicchā nipakā dhīrā appāhārā ālolupāVivekābhiratā dhīrā parivārenti taṃ sadā Āraññakā dhutadharā jhāyino lukhacīvarāVivekābhirātā dhīrā parivārenti taṃ sadā Paṭipannā phalaṭṭhā ca sekhā phalasamaṅginoĀsiṃsakā uttamatthaṃ parivārenti taṃ sadā Sotāpannā ca vimalā sakadāgāmino ca yeAnāgāmi ca arahā parivārenti taṃ sadā Satipaṭṭhanakusalā bojjhaṅgabhāvanāratāSāvakā te bahu sabbe parivārenti taṃ sadā Sakya puttassa santike the  Evaṃ sabbattha  Āsisakā ma the  Iddhipādesu kusalā samādhibhāvanāratāSammappadhānamanuyuttā parivārenti taṃ sadā Tevijjā chaḷabhiññā ca iddhiyā pāramiṃ gatāPaññāya pāramiṃ pattā parivārenti taṃ sadā Edisā te mahāvira tava sissā susikkhitāDurāsadā uggatejā parivārenti taṃ sadā Tehi sissehi parivuto saññatehi tapassihiMigarājāvasambhito uḷurājava sobhasi Paṭhaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya ruhanti dharaṇirūhāVepullataṃ pāpuṇanti phalañca adadyanti te  Paṭhavisadiso tvaṃsi sakyaputta mahāyasaSāsane te patiṭaya labhanti amataṃ phalaṃ Sindhu sarasasati ceva tadiyo candabhāgikā Gaṅgā ca yamunā ceva sarakhu ca atho mahi Etāsaṃ sandamānānaṃ sāgaro sampaṭicchatiJahanti purimaṃ nāmaṃ sāgarotveva ñāyati Tathevime catubbaṇṇā pabbajitvā tavantikeJahanti purimaṃ nāma buddhaputtāni ñāyare Yathāpi cando vimalo gacchaṃ ākāsadhātuyāSabbe tāragaṇe loke ābhāya atirocati Tathe tvaṃ mahāvīra parivuto devamānuseEte sabbe atikkamma jalasī sabbadā tuvaṃ Gambhire uṭṭhitā ūmi na velaṃ ativattare Sabbāva velaṃ phusanti saṃvuṇṇā vikiranti tā Tatheva titthiyā loke nānādiṭṭhi bahujjanāDhammaṃ vaditukāmā te nātivattanti taṃ muniṃ Sace ca taṃ pāpuṇanti paṭivādehi cakkhumaTavantikaṃ upāgantvā sañcuṇṇāva bhavanti te Yathāpi udake jātā kumudā mandālakā bahuUpalimpanti toyena kadadama kalalena ca Tatheva bahukā sattā loke jātā virūhareAṭṭitā rāgadosena kadadame kumudaṃ yathā Yathāpi padumaṃ jalajaṃ jalamajjhe virūhatiNa so limpati toyena pariyuddho hi kesarī Iddhipāde ca ma  Cambhito the  Bhāgiyo   Catuvaṇṇā ma   Ativattanima  se  Sabbā velaṃ ma  the  Vāditukāmā ma the dhāritukāma  se Parivārehi se  Maddālikā  Kassamaṃ ma the  Taṃ the  Parisuddhaṃ the  Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra goke jato mahāmuniNo palimpasi lokena toyena padumaṃ yathā Yathāpi ramamake mase bahu pupphanti vārijāNātikkamanti taṃ māsaṃ samayo pupphanāya so  Tatheva tvaṃ sakyaputta pupphito te vimutatiyāSāsanaṃ nātivattanti padumaṃ vārijaṃ yathā Supupphito sālarājā dibbaṃ gandhaṃ pavāyatiAññasālehi parivuto sālarājāva sobhani Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra buddhañāṇena vibabhantā migaraññā yathā migā Ye keci gaṇino loke satthāroti pavuccareParamparāgataṃ dhammaṃ desenti parisāya te Na he vaṃ tvaṃ mahāvīra dhammaṃ desesi pāṇinaṃSāmaṃ saccāni bujjhitvā kevalaṃ Mahāmoggallānattherāpadānaṃ Anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabhoVihāsi himavantamhi devasaṅghapurakkhato Varuṇo nāma nāmena nāgarājā ahaṃ tadāKāmarūpī vikubbāmi mahodadhinivāsahaṃ Saṅgaṇiyaṃ gaṇaṃ hitvā turiyaṃ paṭṭhapesahaṃSambuddhaṃ parivāretvā vādesuṃ accharā tadā Vajjamānesu turiyesu devā turiyāni vajjayuṃ Ubhinnaṃ saddaṃ sutvāna budedhāpi sampabujjhatha Nimantiyitvā sambuddhaṃ sakaṃ a Sambuddho the  Tappemi the ma  imā devā gāthāyo  se  potthakesu navijjanti  Yo so saṅghaṃ apūjesi buddhañca lokanāyakaṃTena cittappasādena devalokaṃ gamissati Santasattatikkhantuṃ ca devarajjaṃ yantaṃ yojetva haṃ tadā Sahassavaṭṭiṃ pādāsiṃ buddhassa lokabandhunoSattāhaṃ pajjalitvāna dīpā vupasamiṃsu me Tena cittappasādena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ vimānamupapajjahaṃ Uppannassa devattaṃ vyamhaṃ āsi sunimmitaṃ Samantato pajjalati dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  Samantā yojanasataṃ virocesiṃ ahaṃ tadāSabbe deve atibhomi dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Hoti laṅkataṃ ma the laṅkato se  Tadākiṇṇaṃ  se  Bhuttāca pītvā  bhutvāvasitvā ca se  Punapi devataṃ ma the  Paribbajiṃ  se  Anukampi  Yojiyahaṃ ma the  Padipa vupasammisu   Thambho āsi sunimamito ma  se Virocemi   Tiṃsa kappāni devindo devarajjamakārayiṃNa maṃ kevatimaññanti dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Aṭṭhavisatikkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃDivārattiñca passāmi samantā yojanaṃ tadā Sahassalokaṃ ñāṇena passāmi santhusāsaneDibbacakkhuṃ anuppatto dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Sumedho nāma sambuddho tiṃsakappasahassinoTassa dīpo mayā dinno vippasanne cetasā Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anuruddho thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Anuruddhattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ  Puṇṇattherāpadānaṃ Ajjhayako mattadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāraguPurakkhatomahi sissehi upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggahoMama kammaṃ pakittesi saṅkhittena mahāmuni Tāhaṃ dhammaṃ suṇitvāna abhivādetvāna satthunoAñajalimpaggahetvāna pakkāmiṃ dakkhiṇamukho Saṅkhittena suṇitvāna vitthārena adesayiṃ Sabbe sissā attamanā sutvāna mama bhāsato Sakadiṭṭhiṃ vinodetvā buddhe cittaṃ pasādayuṃSaṅkhittenapi desemi vitthārena tatheva haṃ  Abhidhammanayaññuhaṃ kathāvatthuvisuddhiyoSabbesaṃ viññapetvāna viharāmi anāsavo Ito pañcasate kappe caturo suppakāsakāSattaratanasampannā catudipambhi issarā Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇeṇā mattāniputto thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Puṇṇamattāniputtattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ  Kevitimaññanti the ma  Abhāsayiṃ ma  Piyā the  Desesiṃ ma Pibhāsayiṃ ma  Nayaññehaṃ ma   Upālittherāpadānaṃ Nagare haṃsavatiyā sujāto nāma brāhmaṇoAsitikoṭinicayo pahutadhanadhaññacā Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāraguLakkhaṇe itihāse ca sadhamme pāramiṃ gato Paribbājā ekasikhā gotamā buddhasāvakāCarakā nāpasā ceva caranti mabhiyā tadā Tepi maṃ parivārenti brāhmaṇo vissuto itiBahujjano maṃ pujeti nāhaṃ pujemi kañcanaṃ Pujārahaṃ na passāmi mānatthaddho ahaṃ tadāBuddhoti vacanaṃ natthi tāva nupapajjate jano Accayena ahorattā padumuttaranāyako Sabbaṃ tamaṃ vinodetvā loke uppajji cakkhumā Vitthārino bāhujaññe puthubhute ca sāsaneUpāgami tadā buddho nagaraṃ haṃsasavhayaṃ  Pitu atthāya so buddho dhammaṃ desesi cakkhumāTena kālena parisā samantā yojanaṃ tadā Sammato manujānaṃ so sunando nāma tāpasoYāvatā buddhaparisā pupphehacchādayi tadā Catusaccaṃ pakāsente seṭṭhe ca pupphamaṇḍapeKoṭisatasahassānaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu Sattarattindivaṃ buddho vassetvā dhammavuṭṭhiyo Aṭṭhame divase patte sunandaṃ kittayī jino Devaloke manusse vā saṃsaranto ayaṃ bhaveSabbesaṃ pavaro hutvā bhavesu saṃsarissati Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmitoMattāniputto puṇeṇāti hessati Vitthārike ma  Yo ma se  Heṭṭhā ca ma heṭṭhato the  Vasasitvā ma  Vuṭṭhiyā  the  So buddho Ma  Katañajali namassanti sunandaṃ tapasaṃ janāBuddhe kāraṃ karitvāna sodhesi gatimattano Tattha me ahu saṅkappo sutvāna munito vacaṃAhampi kāraṃ kassāmi yathā pasasāmi gotamaṃ Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna kiriyaṃ cintayiṃ mamaṃKyāhaṃ kammaṃ ācarāmi puññakkhette anuttare Ayañca pāṭhiko bhikkhu sabbapāṭhina sāsaneVinaye ca agganikkhitetā taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ ahaṃ Idaṃ me amitaṃ bhogaṃ akkhobhaṃ sāgarūpamaṃTena bhogena buddhassa ārāmaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃ Sobhanaṃ nāma ārāmaṃ nagarassa puratthatoKitvā satasahassena saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ  Kūṭāgāre ca pāsāde maṇḍape hammiye guhāCaṅkame sukate katvā saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ Jantāgharaṃ aggisālaṃ atho udakamāḷakaṃNahānagharaṃ māpayitvā bhikkhusaṅghassadāsabhaṃ Āsandiyo piṭhake ca paribhoge ca bhājaneĀrāmikañca bhesajjaṃ sabbametaṃ adāsabhaṃ Ārakkhaṃ paṭṭhapetvāna pākāraṃ kārayiṃ daḷhaṃMā naṃ koci viheṭhesi santacittāna tādinaṃ Āvāsaṃ satasahassena saṅghārāme amāpayiṃVepullataṃ pāpayitvā sambuddhaṃ upanāmayiṃ Niṭṭhāpito mayā rāmo sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ muniNiyyādesasāmi te vīra adhivāsehi cakkhuma Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggahoMama saṅkappamaññāya adivāsesi nāyako Adhivāsanamaññāya sabbaññussa mahesinoBhojanaṃ paṭiyādetvā kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ Ārocitambhi kālambhi pudumuttaranāyakoKhiṇāsamasahassehi ārāmaṃ me upāgami Nisinnaṃ kālamaññāya annapānena tappayiṃBhuttāviṃ kālamaññāya idaṃ vacanamabuviṃ Tadā  se  Sodheti the  Citatayi the  Pāṭhito ma pāṭiko the  Sabbapāṭhissa masabbapāṭhiva the sabbapāṭhika a mu  Patthaye a mu  Māpaye a mu  Katvā  the Satasahassenāvāsaṃ ma āvāsasatasahasse se āvāsasatasabhassena the  Saṅghārāmaṃ  Vepullaṃ taṃ māpayitvā ma the  Niye jessami the  Taṃ ma se the  Kito sumāpitaṃBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā idaṃ vacanamabravi Yo so buddhassa pādāsi saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃTamahaṃ kittayissāmi puṇātha mama bhāsato  Hatthi assā rathā patti senā ca caturaṅginiParivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni bheriyo samalaṅkatāParivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ Chaḷāsītisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatāVicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā Āḷārapamhā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimāParivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissatiSahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajajaṃ karissati Devarājena pattabbaṃ sabbaṃ dhārento  se  Yathā sulāvuto poso rājadaṇḍena tajjitoSule sātaṃ avindanto parimuttiṃva icchati Tathehāhaṃ mahāvīra bhavadaṇḍena tajjitoKammasulāvuto santo pipāsāvedanaṭṭito Bhave sātaṃ na vindāmi ḍayahanto tihi aggihiParimuttiṃ gavesāmi yathāpi rājadaṇḍito  Yathā visādo puriso visena paripiḷitoAgadaṃ so gaveseyya visaghātāyupānaṃ Gavesamāno passeyya agadaṃ visaghātakaṃTaṃ pivitvā sukhī assa visamhā parimuttiyā Tathehāhaṃ mahāvīra yatā visahato naroSamapiḷito avijjāya saddhammādamesayiṃ Dhammāgadaṃ gavesanto adadakkhiṃ sakyasāsanaṃAggaṃ sabbosadhānaṃ taṃ sabbasallavinodanaṃ Dhammosadhaṃ pipitvāna visaṃ sabbaṃ samuhaniṃAjarāmaraṃ sitibhāvaṃ nibbāṇaṃ phassayiṃ ahaṃ Yathā bhūtaṭṭito poso bhūtagāhena piḷitoBhūtavejjaṃ gaveseyya bhūtasmā parimuttiyā Gavesamāno passeyya bhūtavijjāsu santipadamanuttaraṃĀdāya viharāmetaṃ garuḷo pannagaṃ yathā Na vindanto  the  Vedanaddito the  Visārado the Yupāyanaṃ ma se a yupāyaso   Pivitvāna the  Visato ma  Mesahaṃ  the Dhammosadha the paṭikamme ca ṭhānāṭhāna ca kovidoOsāraṇe vuṭṭhāpane sabbattha pāramiṃ gato Vinaye khandhake cāpi nikkhipitvā padaṃ ahaṃUbhato viniveṭhetvā rasato osareyyahaṃ Niruttiyā sukusalo atthānatthe ca idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Āsīvisaṃ va kupitaṃ aggikkhandhaṃva āgataṃMatataṃva kuñajaraṃ dantiṃ yaṃ sayambhumasādadhiṃ Āsādito mayā buddho ghoro ugagatapo jinoPurā sabbe vinassāma khamāpessāma taṃ muniṃ No abhāsitthāti Bhāgineyyaupālittherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ  Soṇakoṭikaṇṇattherāpadānaṃ Anomadassimunino lokajeṭṭhassa tādinoSudhāya lepanaṃ katvā caṅkamaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ Nānāvaṇṇehi pupphehi caṅkamaṃ santhariṃ ahaṃĀkāse vitānaṃ katvā bhojasiṃ buddhamuttamaṃ Bhāgineyyaupālittherassa aṭṭhakathā sihalakkharamuddita potthake bhāgineyya iti nadissate Kuṭikaṇṇa itipi pātho Ito paṭṭhāya dissamānaṃ apadānaṃ soṇakeṃḷiyavessattherassāti sihalakkharamudditaapadānapāḷiyaṃ ca soṇakoḷivisattherassāni marammakkharamudditāpadānapāḷiyaṃ caāgacchati Theragāthaṭṭhakathāyampi imā gāthā kolivisattheracarite nicesitāApadānaṭṭhakathā cariyo pana apadānamidaṃ soṇakoṭikaṇṇattherassāni ca so therokoliyarājavajase jāno ti ca dassesi so panāyaṃ thero soṇo koḷiviso vā soṇo kuṭikaṇṇo vābhavatu ayaṃ ambhākaṃ bhagavato sāsane etadaggaṭṭhānaṃ labhiti apadānapāḷiyā evaviññāyate Āraddhaviriyānaṃ aggataṃ gato soṇo kolivisatthero campānagare vessakule jātoni ca kalyāṇavākkaraṇānaṃ aggaṭṭhānappatto koṭikaṇṇatthero avantijanapade kāḷiyānama seṭṭhihariyāya kucchimbhi uppannoti ca mahāvaggapāḷi manorathapuraṇiādihipāmāṇikehi gatthehi suvisadaṃ pākaṭi bhavati Apadānapāḷiyaṃ ekunacattāḷisatimevaggedisasamānaṃ soṇakoṭivisattherassa apadānaṃ pana manorathapuraṇiyā dassitenaāraddhaviriyānaṃ aggataṃ gatassa soṇakoḷivisattherassa caritte saddhiṃ sameti Tasmāidaṃ apadānaṃ apadānaṭṭhakathāyaṃ dissamānassa soṇassa koṭikaṇṇattherassevātiavagantabbaṃ  Añajalimpaggahetvāna abhivādetvāna subbataṃDighasālaṃ bhagavato niyyādesamahaṃ tadā Mama saṅkappamaññāya satthā loke anutataroPaṭiggahesi bhagavā anukampāya cakkhumā Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho dakkhiṇeyyo sadevakeBikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo so haṭṭhena cittena dighasālaṃ akāsi meTamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato  Imassa maccukālambhi puññakammasamaṅginoSahassayuttassaratho upaṭṭhassati tāvade Tena yānenayaṃ poso devalokaṃ gamissatiAnumodissare devā sampate kusale bhave Mahārahaṃ vyamhaseṭṭhaṃ ratanamattikalepanaṃKuṭāgāravarūpetaṃ vyambhaṃ ajjhavasissati Tiṃsa kappasahassāni devaloke ramissatiPañcavisati kappāni devarājā bhavissati Sattasattatikkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissatiYasodhara sanāmā te sabbepi ekanāmakā Dve sampatti anubhotvā cinitvāpuññasañcayaṃAṭṭhavisatikappambi cakkavatti bhavissati Tatrāpi vyamhaṃ pavaraṃ vissakammena māpitaṃDasasaddāvicittaṃ taṃ puramajjhivasissati Aparimeyye ito kappe bhumipālo mahiddhikoOkkāko nāma nāmena rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati Soḷasitthisahassānaṃ sabbāsaṃ pavarā ca sāAbhijātā khattiyāni tava putte janessati Tava putte janetvāna khattiyāni marissatiTaruṇi ca piyā aññā mahesittaṃ karissati Okkākaṃ tosayitvāna varaṃ kaññā labhissatiVaraṃ laddhānaṃ sā kaññā putte pabbajayissati Pabbājitā ca te sabbe gamissanti taguttamaṃJātibhedabhayā sabbe bhaginihi saṃvasissare Ekā ca kaññā vyadhihi bhavissati parikkhatāMā no jāti pabhijja ti nikkhiṇissanti khattiyā Khattiyo niharitvāna tāya saddhiṃ vasisasatiBhavissati tadā bhedo okkākakulasambhavo Adāsi the se machasaṃ  Ratanabhittisamujjalaṃ the  Samānā simu  Vaḍḍhetvā simu  Yā the sāyā  Sāsiyā the kaññā machasaṃ  Kaññaṃ the  Varaladadhā the Vasissare machasaṃ   Purakkhatā  se syā   Tesaṃ pajā bhavissanti kolāyā nāma jātiyāTattha mānusakaṃ bhogaṃ anubossantanappakaṃ Tamhā kāyā cavivona devalokaṃ gamissatiTatrāpi pavaraṃ vyambhaṃ vindissati manoramaṃ Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codinoĀgantvāna manussattaṃ soṇo nāma bhavissati Āraddhaviriyo pabhitatto padahaṃ satthu sāsaneSabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissanatāsavo Anantadassi bhagavā gotamo sakyapuṅgavoVisesaññu mahāvīro aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati  Uttame damathe danto cittaṃ me suppaṇihitaṃBhāro me obhito sabbo nibbutomhi anāsavo Aṃgiraso mahānāgo abhijātova kesarīBhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā apadānaṃ dūtiyaṃ  Kāḷigodhāputtabhaddiyattherāpadānaṃ Padumuttarasambuddhaṃ mettacittaṃ mahāmuniṃUpeti janatā sabbā sabbalokagganāyakaṃ Vattha ṃsenāsanaṃ ceva āmisaṃ pānabhojanaṃDadanti satthuno sabbe puññakkhette anuttare  Ahampi dānaṃ dassāmi devadevassa tādinoBuddhaseṭṭhaṃ nimantetvā saṃghampi ca anuttaraṃ Uyyojitā mayā cete nimantesuṃ tathāgataṃKevalaṃ bhikkhusaṅghañca puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ Labhissati the machasaṃ  Atthadassi se the vuṭṭhāmbhi deve caturaṅgulambhi  tiṇeanilerita aṅgaṇambhi ṭhātvāna yogassa payuttatādino  tatottariṃ pajaragatā na vijjatidissate cāyaṃ gāthā maramma chaṭṭhasaṅgiti potthake Theragāthaṭṭhakathāyaṃ panavaṭṭambhi deve caturaṅgule patite anileritāpādapasampaghuṭṭhe jhane ratassappasussatatādino tato rati paramatarā na vijjatiti gāthā āgatā tathāpissā ḷuttha ucitanā natthi Uttamena damathena te  Bhadadiyattherāpadānaṃ sī mu  Satatukañcabaddhakañcamachasaṃ  padakaṃ se sattukañca pavākañca syā  Satasahassa pallaṅkaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ goṇakatthataṃTulikā paṭalikāya khomakappāsikehi caMahārahaṃ paññapesiṃ āsanaṃ buddhayuttakaṃ Padumuttaro lokavidu devadevo narāsabhoBhikkhusaṃghaparibbuḷho mama dvāraṃ upāgami Paccuggantvāna sambuddhaṃ lokanāthaṃ yasassinaṃPasannacitto sumāno atināmayiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ Bhikkhunaṃ satasahassaṃ buddañca lokanāyakaṃPasannacitto sumano paramannena tappayiṃ Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggahoBhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhasatha Yenidaṃ āsanaṃ dinnaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ goṇakatthataṃTamahaṃ kittayisasāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Catusattatikkhattuṃ so devarajjaṃ karissatiAnubhossati sampattiṃ accharāhi purakkhato Padesarajjaṃ sahassaṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissatiEkapaññasakkhattuñca cakakvatti bhavissati Sabbāsu bhavayonisu uccākuli bhavissatiSo ca pacchā pabbajitvā sukkamūlena coditoBhaddiyo nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako Vivekamanuyuttomhi pantasenanivāsahaṃPhalañcādhigataṃ sabbaṃ cattakelayomhi ajajahaṃ Mama sabbaṃ abhiññāya sababaññu lokanāyakoBhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ sanniṭṭhāpako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Sanniṭapakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ  Pañcahatthiyattherāpadānaṃ Sumedho nāma sambuddho gacchate antarāpaṇeOkkhittacakkhu mitabhāṇi satimā saṃvutindriyo thomitatoTiṃsakappasahassāni devarajjaṃ karissati Kappasatasahassambhi aṃgirasasanāmakoVivattacchaddo sambuddho uppajjissati tāvade Tassa dhammesu dāyado oraso dhammanimmito Sataraṃsiti nāmena arahā so bhavissati Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃSataraṃsimbhi nāmena pabhā niddhāvate mama Maṇḍape rukkhamule vā jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃDhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane Saṭṭhikappasahassambhi caturo rāma nāmakāSattaratanasampannā vakkavatti mahabbalā  Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sataraṃsiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Sataraṃsikattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ  Sayanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ Padumuttarabuddhassa sabbalokānukampinoSayanaṃ tassa pādāsiṃ vippasannena cetasā Tena sayanadānena sukhette bijasampadāBhogā nibbattare tassa sayanassa idaṃ phalaṃ Ubbiddhaṃ machasaṃ  Vicittachando machasaṃ se  Roma  se  Sataraṃsimachasaṃ  Bhogo nibbattate  se  Ākāse seyyaṃ kappemi dharemi imaṃPāṇesu me issariyaṃ sayanassa idaṃ phalaṃ Pañcakappasahassambhi aṭṭha āsuṃ mahāvarā Catuttiṃse kappasate caturo ca mahabbalā Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sayanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Sayanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  Gandhodakiyattherāpadānaṃ Padumuttarabuddhassa mahābodhimaho ahuVicittaṃ ghaṭamādāya gandhodakamadāsahaṃ Nahāpanakāle bodhiyā mahāmegho pavassathaNinnādo ca mahā āsi asaniyā phalantiyā Tenevāsanivegena tathe kālakato ahuṃ Devaloke ṭhito santo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsahaṃ  Aho buddho aho dhammā aho no satthusampadāKalebaraṃ me patitaṃ devaloke ramāmahaṃ Ubbadidhaṃ bhagavaṃ mayhaṃ satabhumaṃ samuggataṃKaññāsatasassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā Ābādhā me na vijjanti soko mayhaṃ na pijjatiPariḷāhaṃ na passāmi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ Aṭṭhavise kappasate rājā saṃvasito ahuṃSattaratanampanno cakakvatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhodakiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Gandhodakiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ  Opavayha ttherāpadānaṃ Padumuttarabuddhassa ājāniyamadāsahaṃNiyyādetvāna sambuddhe agamāsiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ Devalo nāma nāmena satthuno aggasāvakoVaradhammassa dāyādo āgacchi mama santikaṃ Mahātejā machasaṃ mahāvīrā syā   Nahānakāle ca bodhiyā simu  Ahuṃ  Ahaṃ machasaṃ  Opavuyha bahūsu  Sambuddhaṃ   Sapattahāro bhagavā ājāneyyo na kappatiTava saṅkappamaññāya adhivāsesi cakkhumā Agaghāpevo vātajavaṃ sindhavaṃ sighavāhanaṃPadumuttarabuddhassa khamaniyamadāsahaṃ Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃKhamaniyā vātajavā cittā nibbattare mama  Lābhā tesaṃ suladdhaṃva ye labhantupasampadaṃPunapi payirupāseyyaṃ buddho loke save bhave Aṭṭhavisatikkhattuṃhaṃ rājā āsiṃ mahabbaloCāturanno vijitāvi jambusaṇḍassa issaro Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavoPattosmi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ hitvā  Saparicārāsanattherāpadānaṃ Padumuttarabuddhassa piṇḍapātaṃ adāsahaṃGantvā taṃ bhojanaṭṭhānaṃ mallikāhi parikkhipaṃ Tamhāsanambhi āsino buddho lokagganāyakoAkittayi piṇḍapātaṃ ujubhuto samābito jalajuttaranāmakoPiṇḍapātaṃ thavitvāna pakkāmi uttarāmukho Deve ca mānuse bhave simu bhavane sabbadā mama   Khamaniyaṃ vātajavaṃmachasaṃ khamaniyo vātajavo se ājāniyāvātajavā syā  Citte  se cittaṃ thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Saparivārāsanattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ  Pañcadipakattherāpadānaṃ Padumuttarabuddhassa sabbabhūtānukampinoSusaṇṭhahitvā saddamme ujudiṭṭhi ahosahaṃ Padipadānaṃ pādāsiṃ parivāretvāna bodhiyaṃSaddahanto padipāni akariṃ tāvade ahaṃ Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃKākāse ukkaṃ dhārenti dipādānassidaṃ phalaṃ Tirokuḍḍaṃ tiroselaṃ samatiggayha pabbataṃSamantā Dhajadāyakattherāpadānaṃ Padumuttarabuddhassa bodhimha pādaputtameHaṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena dhajamāropayiṃ ahaṃ Patita pattāni gaṇhitvā bahiddhā chaḍḍhayiṃ ahaṃAntosuddhaṃ bahisuddhaṃ adhimuttamanāsavaṃSammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ acandiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ  Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggahoBhikkhusaṃghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha Saddahitvāna machasaṃ se  Satta se a pana  padipadāyaka  Iminā dhajadānena upaṭṭhānena cubhayaṃKappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggahassaṃ duggatiṃ so na gacchati Devesu devasobhaggaṃ anubhossatanappakaṃAnekasatakkhattuñca rājā raṭṭhe bhavissatiUggato Ekapaññāsasahasse kappe uggatasavahayoPaññāsatisahasse khattiyo meghasamahayo Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhajadāyako Abbhuṭṭhāsi  a abbhuṭṭhāhi ca se  Desetto  se a  Dipadinda lokajeṭṭhanarāsabha  iti sabbattha  Āvo  se  Mālaṃ se  Saddhāgamaniya se  Parappasādakattherāpadānaṃ Usahaṃ pavaraṃ vīraṃ mahesiṃ buddhassa ko disvā nappasiditi Anilajova asaṅkhobhā yathākāso asaṅkhiyoTatheva ñāṇaṃ buddhassa ko disvā nappasiditi  Imāhi catugāthāhi brāhmaṇo senasamhayoBuddhaseṭṭhaṃ thavitvāna siddhatthaṃ Pupphacaṅgoṭiyattherāpadānaṃ Abhitarūpaṃ sihaṃva abhijātaṃva kesariṃVyagghusabhaṃva pavaraṃ garūḷaggaṃva pakkhinaṃ  Sikhiṃ tilokasaraṇaṃ anejaṃ aparājitaṃNisinnaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ bhikkhusaṃghapurakkhataṃ Adhopupphiyattherāpadānaṃ Abhibhu nāma so bhikkhu sikhino aggasāvakoMahānubhāvo tevijjo himavannaṃ upāgami Ahampi himavantambhi ramaniyassame isiVasāmi appamaññāsu iddhisu ca tadā vasi Pakkhajāto apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  Vikappetuṃ machasaṃ  Nāradavahaya vacachalo machasaṃ  Nupapajjatha simu  Migarājā tadā āsiṃ abhijāto sukesariGiriduggaṃ gavesanto addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ Ayaṃ nukho mahāvīro nibbāpeti seyyaṃ kappemi avidūre sikhisatthuno Sāyaṃ pātañca passāmi buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃDeyyadhammo ca me nathi dipadindassa tādino  Piyāpaphalamādāya agamaṃ buddhasantikaṃPaṭiggahesi bhagavā lokajeṭṭho sahasesa kappānaṃ aṭṭhatiṃse teIsimuggasanāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalā Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā isimuggadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Isimuggadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ  Bodhiupaṭṭhākattherāpadānaṃ Nagare rammavatiyā āsiṃ murajavādakoNiccupaṭṭhānayuttomhi gatohaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ Sāyaṃ pātaṃ upaṭṭhitvā āyusaṅkhayāTayo saddā niccharanti devānaṃ anumodataṃ Ito bho sugatiṃ gaccha manussānaṃ sahavyataṃManussabhuto saddhamme saddhamanuttaraṃ Vataraṃsiṃva machasaṃ  Pisetthā machasaṃ saṃditvā se saṃdetvā mulajātā patiṭṭhitāYāvajīvaṃ asaṃhirā saddhamme suppavedite  Kāyena kusalaṃ katvā vādāya kusalaṃ bahuṃManasā kusalaṃ katvā avyāpajjhaṃ nirūpadhiṃ Tato opadhikaṃ puññaṃ katvā dānena taṃ bahuṃAññepi macce saddhamme brahmacariye nivesaya Imāya anukampāya devā devaṃ yadā viduVacantaṃ anumodanti ehi devapuraṃ puna Saṃvego me tadā āsi devasaṅghe samāgateKaṃ su nāma ahaṃ yoniṃ gamissāmi ito cuto Mama apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  Padipiyattherāpadānaṃ  Devabhuto ahaṃ santo oruyha paṭhaviṃ tadāPadipe pañca pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ padipamadaṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dīpadānassidaṃ apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   Maghavapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ Nammadānadiyā tīre sayambhu aparājitoSamādhiṃ so samāpanno vippasanno anāvilo Disvā pasanno sumano sambuddhaṃ aparājitaṃTāhaṃ maghavapupphena sayambhuṃ pujayiṃ tadā  Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maghavapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Maghavapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamayaṃ  Upaṭṭhākadāyakattherāpadānaṃ Rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃDipadindaṃ mahānāgaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ Pakkosāpiya tassāhaṃ sabbalokahitesinoUpaṭṭhāko mayā dinno siddhathessa mahesino Paṭiggahetvā sambabuddho niyyātesi mahāmuniUṭṭhāya āsanā tamhā pakkāmi pācināmukho Catunavute ito kappe upaṭṭhākamadaṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ Sattapaññāsito kappe balasena sanāmakoSattaratanasampanenā cakkavatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upaṭṭhākadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Upaṭṭhākadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   Apadāniyattherāpadānaṃ Apadānaṃ sugatānaṃ kittayiṃhaṃ mahesinoPāde ca sirasā vandiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi Dvenavute ito kappe apadānaṃ pakittayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā apadāniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Apadāniyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamayaṃ   Sattāhapabbajitattherāpadānaṃ Vipassissa bhagavato saṅgho sakkatamānitoVyasanaṃ me anuppatataṃ ñātibhedo pure ahu Pabbajja mubagantvāna vyasanupasamāyahaṃSattāhābhirato tattha satthusāsanakamyatā Ekanavute ito kappe yamahaṃ pabbajiṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pabbajjāya idaṃ phalaṃ Sattasaṭṭimbhito kappe satta āsuṃ mahipatiSunikkhamāti ñāyanti cakkavatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sattāhapabbajito thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Sattāhapabbajitattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  Buddhupaṭṭhākattherāpadānaṃ Veṭambariti me nāmaṃ pitusantaṃ mamaṃ tadāMama hatthaṃ gahetvāna upānayi mahāmuniṃ Ime maṃ uddisissanti buddhā lokagganāyakāTehaṃ upaṭṭhiṃ sakkaccaṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi Voṭambhiniti machasaṃ vedhambhiniti syā  Ekatiṃse ito kappe buddhe paricariṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ Tevisambhi ito kappe caturo āsu khattiyoSamaṇupaṭṭhākā nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhupaṭṭhāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthātiBuddhapaṭṭhākattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   Pubbaṅgamiyattherāpadānaṃ Cullāsitisahassāni pabbajimha akiñcanāTesaṃ pubbaṅgamo āsiṃ uttamatthassa pattiyā Sarāgā sabhavā cete vippasnanamanāvilāUpaṭṭhahiṃsu sakkaccaṃ pasannā sehi pāṇiha Khiṇāsavā vantadosā katakiccā anāsavāPhariṃsu mettacittena sayambhu aparājitā Tesaṃ upaṭṭhahitvāna sambuddhānaṃ patissatoMaraṇañca anuppatto devattañca agamhase Catunavute ito kappe yā silamanupālayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saññamassa idaṃ phalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pubbaṅgamiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Pubbaṅgamiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ UddānaṃPaṇṇaṃ phalaṃ puccuggamaṃ ekapupphi ca maghavāUpaṭṭhākā padānañca pabbajjā baddhupaṭṭhākoPubbaṅgamo ca gāthāyo aṭṭatāḷisa kitatitāni Paṇṇādāyakavaggo ekunatiṃsatimo  Samaṇupaṭṭhakā si mu  Samohā syā  Vippasannamanāvilaṃ simu  Pharisuṃ simu Uggamiya simu  Citakapujakattherāpadānaṃ Ajito nāma nāmena ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadāĀhutiṃ siṭṭhukāmāhaṃ nānāpuphaṃsamānayiṃ Jalantaṃ citakaṃ disvā sikhino lokabandhunoTaṃ ca pupphaṃ samānetvā citake okiriṃ ahaṃ  Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi budadhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ Sattavise ito kappe sattāsuṃ manujādhipāSupajjalitatāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Citakapujakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ  Pupphadhārakattherāpadānaṃ Vākatiradharo āsiṃ ajānuttaravāsanoAbhāññāpañcanibbattā candassa parimajjako Vipassiṃ lokapajjotaṃ disvā ahigataṃ mamaPāricchattakapupphāni dhāresiṃ satthuno ahaṃ Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhādhārayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhāraṇāya idaṃ phalaṃ Sattāsitimbhito kappe eko āsiṃ mahipatiSamantadhāraṇo nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphadhārako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Pupphadhārakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   Chattadāyakattherāpadānaṃ Putto mama pabbajito kāsāyavasano tadāSo ca buddhattaṃ sampatto nibbuto lokapujato Vicinanto sakaṃ puttaṃ agamaṃ pacchato ahaṃNibbutassa mahantassa citataṃ agamāsahaṃ Paggayha añjaliṃ tattha vanditvā citakaṃ ahaṃSetacchattañca paggayha āropesiṃ ahaṃ tadā Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ chattamabhiropayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi chattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  Pañcavise ito kappe satta āsuṃ janādhipāMahāraha sanāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā chattadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Chattadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  Saddasaññakattherāpadānaṃ Anuggatamhi ādicce panādo vipulo ahuBuddhaseṭṭhassa lokamhi pātubhāvo mahesino Sadadmassohaṃ tattha na ca passāmi taṃ jinaṃMaraṇe ca anuppatte buddhasaññamanussariṃ Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saddasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Saddasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   Gosisanikkhepakattherāpadānaṃ Ārāmadvārā nikkhamma gosisaṃ santhataṃ mayāAnubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ Ājāniyā vātajavā sindhavā sīghavāhanāAnubhomi sabbametaṃ gosisassa idaṃ phalaṃ Aho kāraṃ paramakāraṃ sukhette sukataṃ mayāSaṅghe katassa kārassana aññaṃ kalamagghati Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ sisaṃ santhariṃ ahaṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi santharassa idaṃ phalaṃ Pañcasattatikappamhi suppatiṭṭhita nāmakoEko āsiṃ mahātejo cakkavatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gosisanikkhepako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Gosisanikkhepakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   Pādapujakattherāpadānaṃ Pabbate himavantamhi ahosiṃ kinnaro tadāAddasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ pitaraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃ Upetaṃ kamahaṃ buddhaṃ vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃCandanaṃ tagarañcāpi pāde osiñcahaṃ tadā Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pādamabhipujayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pādapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pādapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Pādapujakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ  Upetopi tadā syā  Desakittakattherāpadānaṃ Upasāḷhaka nāmohaṃ ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadāKānanaṃ vanamogāḷhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ Disvāna vandiṃ pādesu lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃPasannacittaṃ mā ñatvā buddho antaradhāyatha Kānanā abhinikkhamma buddhaseṭṭhamanussariṃTaṃ desaṃ kittayitvāna kappaṃ saggambhi modahaṃ Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ desamabhikittayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā desakittako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Desakittakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ  Saraṇagamanayatherāpadānaṃ Pabbate himavantamhi ahosiṃ luddako ahaṃVipassiṃ addasaṃ buddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ Upāsitvāna sambuddhaṃ veyyāvaccamakāsahaṃSaraṇañca upāgacchiṃ dipadindassa tādino  Catunavute ito kappe saraṇaṃ yamagacchahaṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saraṇagamanapphalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saraṇagamaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Saraṇagamaniyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  Ambapiṇḍiyattherāpadānaṃ Romaso nāma nāmena dānavo iti vissutoAmbabapiṇḍī mayā dinnā vipassissa mahesino Ekanavute ito kappe yammabamadadiṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ambadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Ambapiṇḍo mayā dinno syā  Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambapiṇḍiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Ambapiṇḍiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ  Anusaṃsāvakattherāpadānaṃ Piṇḍāya caramānāhaṃ vipassiṃ addasaṃ jānaṃUḷuṅkabhikkhaṃ pādāsiṃ dipadindassa tādino Pasannacitto sumano abhivādesahaṃ tadāAnusaṃsāvayiṃ buddhaṃ uttamatthassa pattiyā Catunavute ito kappe anusaṃsāvayiṃ ahaṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi anusaṃsāvanāphalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anusaṃsāvako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Anusaṃsāvakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ UddānaṃCitakaṃ pārichatto ca sadda gosisasantharaṃPadaṃ padesaṃ saraṇaṃ ambo saṃsāvako pi caSattāḷisa gāthāyo gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi Citakapujakavaggo tiṃsatimo  Atha vagguddānaṃKaṇikāro hatthidado ālambaṇudakāsanaṃTuvaraṃ thomako veca ukkhepaṃ sisupadhānaṃPaṇṇado citapuji ca gāthāyo ceva sabbasoCattāri ca satāniha ekapaññāsameva caPañcavisasatā sabbā dvāsattati taduttariTisataṃ apadānānaṃ gaṇitā atthadassihi Tatiyaṃ satakaṃ samattaṃ Kaṇikāravaggadasakaṃ machasaṃ  Padumakesariyattherāpadānaṃ Isisaṅghe ahaṃ pubbe āsiṃ mātaṅgavāraṇoMahesinaṃ pasādena padamakesaramokiriṃ Paccekajinaseṭṭhesu dhutarāgesu tādisuTesu cittaṃ pasādetvā kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ Catunavute ito kappe kesaraṃ okiriṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumakesariyo kappe yaṃ gandhamadadiṃ pureDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi gandhadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  Ito paṇṇarase kappe sucelo nāma khattiyoSattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca sudaṃ āyasmā paramannadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Paramannadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  Dhammasaññakattherāpadānaṃ Vipassino bhagavato mahābodhimaho ahuRukkhaṭṭhe yeva sambuddhe Dhammasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   Phalasāyakattherāpadānaṃ Bhāgirathinaditire ahosi assamo tadāTamahaṃ assamaṃ gacchiṃ phalahattho apekkhavā Vipassiṃ tattha addakkhiṃ pitaraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃYaṃ me atthi phalaṃ sabbaṃ adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ Rukkhaṭṭhasseva smabuddho machasaṃ  Desiyi syā  Dhamamasavassidaṃ phalaṃmachasaṃ dhammasavaṇassidaṃphalaṃ simu  Apekhavā simu  Ekanavute ito imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Phaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ  Sampasādakattherāpadānaṃ Namo te buddhaviratthu vippamuttosi sabbadhiVyasanaṃ hi anuppatto tassa me saraṇaṃ bhava Siddhattho tassa vyākāsi loke appaṭipuggaloMahodadhisamo saṅgho appameyyo anuttaro Tattha tvaṃ viraje khette anantaphaladāyakeSaṅgho cittaṃ pasādehi subījaṃ vāpi ropaya Idaṃ vavona sabbaññu lokajeṭṭho narāsabhoMamevaṃ anusāsitvā vehāsaṃ nabhamuggami Aciraṃ gatamattamhi sabbaññumhi narāsabheMaraṇaṃ samanuppatto tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ Tadāhaṃ viraje khette anantaphaladāyakeSaṅghe cittaṃ pasadetvā kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ sampasādāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Sampasādakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ  Byasanamhi machasaṃ  Pasādetvā masaṃ  Cāpa machasaṃ  Mameva machasaṃ Catunnavutito machasaṃ   Ārāmadākattherāpadānaṃ Siddhatthassa bhagavato ārāmo ropito mayāSandacchāyesu rukkhesu upasantesu pakkhisu Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃĀrāmaṃ atināmesiṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena phalaṃ pupphañcadāsahaṃTato jātappasādo ca taṃ vanaṃ pariṇāmayiṃ Buddhassa yamidaṃ dāsiṃ vippasannena cetasāBhave nibbattamānamhi nibbattati phalaṃ mama Catunavute ito kappe yamārāmaṃ phalaṃ dadiṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ārāmassa idaṃ phalaṃ Sattatiṃse ito kappe sattāsuṃ mudusitalāSattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbalā Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ārāmadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Ārāmadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ  Anulepadāyakattherāpadānaṃ Atthadassa munino addasaṃ sāvakaṃ ahaṃKavakammaṃ karontassa simāya upagacchahaṃ Niṭṭhite kavakamme ca anulepamadāsahaṃPasannacitto sumano puññakkhette anuttare Aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi anulepassidaṃ phalaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anulepadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Anulepadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  Phalaṃ pupphamadāsahaṃ machasaṃ  Padādo ca simu  Yaṃ ārāmamadaṃ tadāmachasaṃ   Buddhasaññakattherāpadānaṃ Udentaṃ sataraṃsiṃva pitarāsiṃva bhānumaṃVanantaragataṃ santaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ Addasaṃ Nābhijānāmi kāyena vācāya uda cetasāSaṃyatānaṃ tapassinaṃ kataṃ akkositaṃ mayā Tena sucaritenāhaṃ cittassa paṇidhihi caSabbesaṃ pujino homi anakkossidaṃ phalaṃ Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyiidaṃ phalaṃ Ito ekādase kappe sahassārosi khattiyoSattaratanasampanno cakkavattī mahabbalo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumanāveliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Sumanāveliyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  Anubhomi machasaṃ  Esā gāthā machasaṃ potthake natthi  Pupaphachattiyattherāpadānaṃ Siddhatthassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādinoSaccaṃ pakāsayantassa nibbāpentassa pāṇito Jalajaṃ āharitvāna satapattaṃ manoramaṃPupphassa chattaṃ katvāna buddhassa abhiropayiṃ  Siddhattho ca lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggabhoBhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satho imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha Yo me cittaṃ pasādetvā pupphachattaṃ adhārayiTena cittappasādena duggatiṃ so na gacchati Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho siddhattho lokanāyakoUyyojetvāna parisaṃ vehāsaṃ nabhamuggami Vuṭṭhite naradevambhi setacchattampi vuṭṭhahiPurato buddhaseṭṭhassa gacchati chattamuttamaṃ Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ naruttamaṃHaṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ Susaṅgahitayāvaṃva dāntova sācakuttamoUpagantvāna sambuddhaṃ matthake sampatiṭṭhahi Anukampako kāruṇiko buddho lokagganāyakoBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Imā gāthā sīmu  Ādhārayiṃ machasaṃ akārayi sīmu  Yena chattamidaṃ dinnaṃ alaṅkataṃ manoramaṃTena cittappasādena duggatiṃ so na gacchati  Sattakkhattuñca devesu devarajjaṃ Tiṇakuṭidāyakattherāpadānaṃ Nagare bandhumatiyā ahosiṃ parakammikoParakammāyane yutto parabhattaṃ apassino Rahogato nisīditvā evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadāBuddho loke samuppanno adhikāro ca natthi me  Kālo gatiṃ sodhetuṃ khaṇo me paṭipāditoDukkho nirayasamphasso apuññānaṃ hi pāṇinaṃ Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna kammasāmiṃ upāgamiṃEkāhaṃ kammaṃ yācitvā vipinaṃ pāvisiṃ ahaṃ Tiṇakaṭṭhañca valliñcaña āharitvānahaṃ tadāTidaṇḍake ṭhapetvāna akaṃ tiṇakuṭiṃ ahaṃ Saṅghassatthāya kuṭikaṃ niyyātetvāna taṃ ahaṃTadaheyeva āgantvā kammasāmiṃ upāgamiṃ Tena kammena sukatena tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃKattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ tiṇakuṭikāya nimmitaṃ Sahassakaṇḍaṃ satabheṇḍu dhajālu haritāmayaṃSatasahassaniyyuhā vyamhe pātubhaviṃsu me Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃMama saṅkappamaññāya pāsādo upatiṭṭhati Bhayaṃ vā sampadāGotamassa bhagavato dhammaṃ sacchikariṃ ahaṃ Kālo me gatiṃ machasaṃ  Kuṭikāya sunimmitaṃ machasaṃ  Sahassakaṇḍosatabheṇḍu dhajāluharitāmayo simu  Sarisapā machasaṃ  Na pāpasupinasasānimachasaṃ tathāgataṃ  hapaniyo mahāvīro adeyyo kassaci jinoNa me paṭissuto buddho carassu amitaṃ dhanaṃ Vinicchayaṃ pāpuṇāma puccissāmi vinicchayeYathāsantaṃ kathessanti paṭipucchāma taṃ tathā Rañño hatthe hahetthāna agamāsiṃ vinicchayaṃParato akkhadassānaṃ idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ  Suṇantu me akkhadassā jīvitampi pacārayiNa kiñci ṭhapayitvāna rājā varamadāsi me Tassa me varadinnassa buddhaseṭṭhaṃ variṃ ahaṃSudinno hoti me buddho athavā saṃsayaṃ mama Sossāma tava vacanaṃ bhumipālassa rājinoUbhinnaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā chindissāmettha saṃsayaṃ Sabbaṃ deva tayā dinnaṃ imassa sabbagāhikaṃNa kiñci ṭhapayitvāna jīvitampi pavārayi Ayācito tathāgato syā  Javitamatthikaṃ syā  Yathāsaṇḍaṃ machasaṃ  Rājāvaramadāsi me machasaṃ  Jīvitampi pavārayi machasaṃ  Sabbagāhitaṃ syā   purato  Kicchappattova hutvāna yāci caramanuttaraṃImaṃ sudukkhitaṃ ñātvā adāsiṃ sabbagābhikaṃ Parājāyo tavaṃ deva assa deyyo tathāgatoUbhinnaṃ saṃsayo jinno yathāsantambhi tiṭṭhatha Rājā tattheva ṭhatvāna akkhadasestadabraviSammā mayhampi deyyātha puna buddhaṃ labhāmahaṃ Puretvā tava saṅkappaṃ bhojayitvā tathāgataṃPuna deyyāsi sambuddhaṃ ānandassa yasasino Akkhadassebhivādetvā ānandañcāpi khattiyaṃTuṭṭho pamudito hutvā sambuddamupasaṅkamiṃ Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃSirasā abhivādetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Vasisatasahassehi adhivāsehi cakkhumaHāsayanto mamaṃ cittaṃ nivesanamupehi me Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggahoMama saṅkappamaññāya adhivāsesi cakkhumā Adhivāsanamaññāya abhivādiya satthunoHaṭṭho udaggacittohaṃ nivesanamupāgamiṃ Mittāmacce samānetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃSudullabho mayā laddho maṇi jotiraso yathā Kena taṃ pujayissāma appameyyo anupamoAtulo asamo dhīro jino appaṭipuggalo Tathā samasamo ceva adutiyo narāsabhoDukkaraṃ adhikāraṃ hi buddhānucchavikaṃ mayā  Nānāpupphe samānetvā karoma pupphamaṇḍapaṃBuddhānucchavikaṃ etaṃ sabbapujā bhavissati Yāvajivamanuttaraṃ syā  Tuvaṃ machasaṃ  Yathāsaṇḍamhi machasaṃ  Mamacittaṃ machasaṃ  Uppalaṃ padumaṃ cāpi vassikaṃ adhimuttakaṃCampakaṃ nāgapupphañca maṇḍapaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ Satāsanasahassāni chattacachāyāya paññapiṃPacchimaṃ āsanaṃ mayhaṃ adhikaṃ satamagghati Satāsanasahassāni chattacchāyāya paññapiṃPaṭiyādetvā antapānaṃ kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ Ārocitambhi kālambhi padumuttaro mahāmuniVasi satasahassehi nivesanamupesi me Dhārentamupicchatte suphullapupphamaṇḍapeVisasatasahassehi nisīdi purisuttamo Chattasatasahassāni satasahassamāsanaṃKappiyaṃ anavajjañca paṭigaṇhābhi cakkhuma Padumuttaro lovidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggahoMamaṃ tāretukāmo so sampaṭicchi mahāmuni Bhikkhuno ekamekassa paccekaṃ pattadāsahaṃJabhiṃsu pubbakaṃ pattaṃ lohapattamadhārasuṃ Sattarattandavaṃ buddho nisīdi pupphamaṇḍapeBodhayanto bahu satte dhammacakkaṃ pavattayi Dhammacakkaṃ pavatente heṭṭhato pupphamaṇḍapeCulalāsitisahassānaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu Sattame divase pate padumuttaro mahāmuniChattacchāyāya māsino imā gāthā abhāsatha Anunakaṃ dānavaraṃ yo me pādāsi māṇavoTamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato Hatthi assā rathā patti senā ca caturaṅginiParivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ savikā sandamānikāUpaṭṭhissantimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Saṭṭhirathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitāParivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ  Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni bheriyo samalaṅkatāVajjayissanatimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Dhārentaṃ uparicchattaṃ machasaṃ  Sumahakaṃ machasaṃ sambhataṃ syā Pavattento machasaṃ  Taṃ syā  Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni machasaṃ  Chaḷāsitisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatāVicittavatthabharaṇā āvuttamaṇikuṇḍalā Aḷārapamhā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimāParivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissatiSahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissatiPadesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ Devaloke vasantassa puññakammasamaṅginoDevalokapariyattaṃ ratanachattaṃ dhariyati Icchissati yadā chāyaṃ chadanaṃ dussapupphajaṃImassa cittamaññāya nibaddhaṃ chādayissati Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamupena coditoPuññakamme na saṃyutto brahmabandhu bhavissati Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavoBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapessati Piḷindivaccha nāmena hessati satthusāvakoDevānaṃ asurānañca gandhabbānaṃ ca sakkato Bhikkhunaṃ bhikkhunīyaṃ ca gihīnaṃ ca tatheva soPiyo hutvāna sabbesaṃ viharissatanāsavo Satasahasesa kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idhaSumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayī mama Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ puññakkhette anuttareYattha kāraṃ karitvāna pattombhi acalaṃ padaṃ Anutakaṃ dānavaraṃ adāsi yo hi māṇavoĀdi pubbaṅgamo āsi tassa dānassidaṃ phalaṃ Chatte sugate datvāna saṅghe gaṇavaruttameAṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama  Sītaṃ uṇhaṃ na jānāmi rajojallaṃ na limpatiAnupaddavo aniti ca homi apacitto sadā Āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā machasaṃ  Dharissati machasaṃ  Yadāvāyaṃ syā  Gottenamachasaṃ  Piḷindavaccha machasaṃ  Jhāpayissati simu  Chatte ca sugate datvāmachasaṃ  Sukhumacchaviko homi visadaṃ hoti mānasaṃChattasatasahassāni bhave saṃsarato mama Sabbālaṅkārayuttāni tassa kammassa vāhasāImaṃ jātiṃ ṭhapetvāna matthake dhārayanti me Kasmā imāya rātiyā natthi me chattadhāraṇāMama sabbaṃ kataṃ kammaṃ vimuttichattapattiyaṃ Dussāni sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttemeAṭṭānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo virajo sappabhāso patāpavāSiniddhaṃ hoti me gattaṃ bhave saṃsarato mama Dussasatasahassāni setā pitā ca lohitāDhārenti matthake mayhaṃ dussadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Koseyyakambaliyāni khomakappāsikāni caSabbattha paṭilabhāmi tesaṃ nissandato ahaṃ Patte sugate datvāna saṅghe gaṇavarutatameDasānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama Suvaṇṇathāle maṇithāle rajate pi ca thālakeLohitaṃkamaye thāle paribhuñajāmi sabbadā Anupaddavo aniti ca homi apacito sadāLābhi antassa pānassa vatthassa sayanassa ca Na vinassanti me bhogā ṭhitacitto bhavāmahaṃDhammakāmo sadā homi appakleso anāsavo Devaloke manussa vā anubandhā ime guṇāChāyā yathāpi rukkhassa sabbattha na jahanti maṃ Cittabandhanasambaddhā sukatā vāsiyo bahuDatvāna buddhaseṭṭassa saṅghassa ca tathevahaṃAṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama  Suro homavisāri ca vesārajjesu pāramiDhiti viriyavā bhomi paggahītamano sadā Kilesacchedanaṃ ñāṇaṃ sukhumaṃ atulaṃ suciṃSabbattha paṭilabhāmi tassa nissandato ahaṃ Tasmā syā  Akakkase apharuse sudhote satthake bahuPasannacitto datvāna buddhe saṅghe tatheva ca Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mamaKalyāṇacittaṃ viriyaṃ khattiñca mettasatthakaṃ Taṇhāsallassa chinnattā paññāsatthaṃ anuttaraṃVajirena samaṃ ñāṇaṃ tesaṃ nissandato labhe Suciyo sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttemePañcānisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama Na saṃsayo kaṅkhacchedo abhirūpo ca bhogavāTikkhapañño sadā homi saṃsaranto bhavābhave Gamhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ atthaṃ ñaṇena passayiṃVajiraggasamaṃ ñāṇaṃ hoti me tamaghātanaṃ Nakhacchedane sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇuttamePañcanisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama Dāsidāse gavasse bhatake ārakkhake bahuNhāpite bhattake sude sabbattheva labhāmahaṃ Vidhupane sugate datvā tālavaṇṭe ca sobhaneAṭṭhānisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama Sītaṃ uṇhaṃ jānāmi pariḷāho na vijjatiDarathaṃ nābhijānāmi cittasantāpanaṃ mama Rāgaggi dosamohaggi mānaggi diṭṭiaggi caSabbaggi nibbutā mayhaṃ tassa nisasandato mama Morahatthe cāmariyo datvā saṅghe gaṇuttameUpasantakilesohaṃ virāmi anaṅgaṇo  Parissāvane sugate datvā dhammakaruttamaPañcanisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama Sabbesaṃ samatikkhamma dibbaṃ āyuṃ labhāmahaṃAppasayho sadā homi corapaccatthikehi ca Nāṭake bahu machasaṃ  Datvā sukate dhammakuttare syā  Satthena vā visena vā vihesampi na kubbateAntarā maraṇaṃ natthi tesaṃ nissandato mama Teladhare sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttamePañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama Uṇṇike padumake ca atho lohitavandaneBimbohane upadhemi uttamaṅgaṃ sadā mama Aṭṭaṅgike maggavare sāmaññe caturo phaleTesu ñāṇaṃ upanetvā vihare sabbakālikaṃ Dāne dame sañcame ca appamaññāsu rūpisuTesu ñāṇaṃ upanetvā vihare sabbakālikaṃ Vatte guṇe paṭipatatiācārakiriyāsu caÑāṇaṃ upadahitvāna vihare sabbadā ahaṃ Caṅkame vā padhāne vā viriyebodhipakkhiyeTesu ñāṇaṃ upanetvā viharāmi yathicchakaṃ  Sīlaṃ patto santisukhaṃ sivaṃ Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piḷindivaccho thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Piḷindivacchattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ  Bhattaṃ machasaṃ  Selattherāpadānaṃ Nagare haṃsavatiyā vithisāmi ahosahaṃMamaṃ ñāti samānetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Buddho loke samuppanno puññakkhettamanuttaraṃĀsi so sabbalokassa āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho Khattiyā negamā ceva mahāsālā ca brāhmaṇāPasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Hatthārohā aṇikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakāPasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te  Uggā ca rājaputtā ca cesiyānā ca brāhmaṇāPasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Āḷārikā kappakā ca nhāpakā mālakārakāPasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Rajakā pesakārā ca cammakārā ca nhāpikāPasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Usukārā bhamakārā cammikā ceva tacchakāPasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Kammārā soṇṇakārā ca tipulohakarā tathāPasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Bhatakā ceṭakā ceva dāsakammakarā bahuYathāsakena thāmena pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Udahāra kaṭṭhahārā kassakā tiṇahārakāYathāsakena thāmena pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Pupphikā mālikā ceva paṇṇikā phalahārakāYathāsakena thāmena pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Gaṇikā kumbhadāsī ca puvikā macchikāpi caYathāsakena thāmena pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te Etha sabbe samāgantvā gaṇaṃ bandhama ekatoAdhikāraṃ karissāma puññakkhette anuttare Mama machasaṃ  Puññakkhetto anuttaro machasaṃ  Āsisaso simu ādhāro  Āḷārakā ca suda syā  Cammakārā ca machasaṃ  Te me sutvāna vacanaṃ gaṇaṃ bandhiṃsu tāvadeUpaṭṭhānasālaṃ sukataṃ bhikkhusaṅghassa kārayuṃ Niṭṭhāpetvāna taṃ sālaṃ udaggo tuṭṭhamānasoPareto tehi sabbehi sambuddheṃ upasaṅkamiṃ Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ lokanāthaṃ narāsabhaṃCanditvā satthuno pāde idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Ime tīṇi satā vīra purisā ekato gaṇāUpaṭṭhānasālaṃ sukataṃ niyyātenti tavaṃ muni Bhikkhusaṅghassa purato sampaṭicchitva cakkhumāTiṇṇaṃ satānaṃ purato imā gāthā abhāsatha Tisataṃ pi ca jeṭṭho ca anuvattiṃsu ekatoSampattiṃ hi karitvāna sabbe anubhavissatha  Pacchimabhave sampatte sitibhāvamanuttaraṃAjaraṃ amataṃ santaṃ nibbāṇaṃ phassayissatha Evaṃ buddho viyākāsi sabbaññu samaṇuttaroBuddhassa vacanaṃ sutvā somanassaṃ pavedayiṃ Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃDevādhipo pañcasataṃ devarajjamakārayiṃ Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakakvati ahosabhaṃDevarajjaṃ karontassa mahādevā avandiṃsu Idha mānuseka rajje parisā honti bandhavāPacchimabhatva sampatte vāseṭṭho nāma brāhmaṇo Asitikoṭinicayo tassa putto ahosahaṃSelo itimamaṃ nāmaṃ chaḷaṅge pāramiṅgato Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ sasissehi purakkhetoJaṭākhārikabharitaṃ keṇiyaṃ nāma tāpasaṃ Paṭiyattāhutiṃ disvā idaṃ vacanamabuviṃĀvaho vā vicāho cā rājā vā te nimantito Āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmohaṃ brāhmaṇe devasammateNa nimantemi rājānaṃ āhuti me na vijjati Niyyādenti machasaṃ  Tuvaṃ machasaṃ  Samāpatti hi syā  Pacchime bhavemachasaṃ  Rajjaṃ machasaṃ  Na vatthi mayhaṃ āvaho vivābho me na vijjatiSakyānaṃ nandijanano seṭṭho loke sadevake Sabbalokahitatthāya sabbasattasukhāvahoSo me nimantito ajja tassetaṃ paṭiyādataṃ Timbarūsakavaṇṇabho appameyyo anupamoRūpenāsadiso buddho svātanāya nimantito Ukkāmukhapahaṭṭhova khadiraṅgārasannibhoVijjupamo mahāvīro so me buddho nimantito Pabbatagge yathā acci puṇṇamāyeva candimāNaḷaggivaṇṇasaṅkāso so me buddho nimantito Asambhito bhayānito bhavantakaraṇo muniSihupamo vahāviro so me buddho nimantito  Kusalo buddhadhammehi appasayho parehi soNāgupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Anantavaṇṇo amitayaso vicittasabbalakkhaṇoSakkupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Vasi gaṇi patāpi ca tejassi ca durāsadoBrahmupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Pattadhammo dasabalo balātibalapāraguDharaṇupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Silavicisamākiṇṇo dhammaviññāṇakhohitoUddhupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Durāsado duppasaho acalo uggato brahāNerūpamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Anantañāṇo asamasamo atulo aggataṃ gatoGaganupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Paṇṇarasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ machasaṃ  Patiṭṭhā bhayabhitānaṃ tāṇo saraṇagāminaṃAssāsako mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Āsayo buddhimantānaṃ puññakkhettaṃ sukhesitaṃRatanākaro mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Assāsako vedakaro sāmaññaphaladāyakoMeghupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Lokacakkhu mahātejo sabbatamavinodanoSuriyupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Ārammaṇavimuttīsu sabhāvadassano muniCandupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Vuddho samussito loke lakkhaṇehi alaṅkatoAppameyyo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Yassa ñāṇaṃ appameyyaṃ sīlaṃ yassa anupamaṃVimutti asadisā yassa so me buddho nimattito Yassa dhiti asadisā thamo yassa acintiyoYassa parakkamo jeṭṭho so me buddho nimattito Rāgo doso ca moho ca visā sabbe samuhatāAgadupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito  Kilesavyādhi bahudukkhasabbatamacinodanoVejjupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito Buddhoti bho yaṃ vadesi ghosopeso sudullabhoBuddho buddhoti sutvāna piti me upapajjatha Abbhantaramagaṇhanti piti me bahi nicchareSohaṃ pitimano santo idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Kahaṃ nu kho so bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabhoTattha gantvā namassassaṃ sāmaññaphaladāyakaṃ Paggayha dakkhiṇaṃ bāhuṃ vedajāto katañajaliĀcikkhi me dhammarājaṃ sokapallavinodanaṃ Buddho machasaṃ  Kelasavyādhi machasaṃ  Sabbatamacinodako simu  Udentaṃva mahāmeghaṃ nīlaṃ añajanasannibhaṃSāgaraṃ viya dissantaṃ passasetaṃ mahāvanaṃ Ettha so vasate buddho adantadamako muniVinayanto ca veneyye bodhento bodhipakkhiye Pipāsitova udakaṃ bhojanaṃva jighacchitoGāmi yathā vacchagiddhā evāhaṃ viciniṃ jinaṃ Ācāraupacāraññu dhammānucchavisaṃvaraṃSikkhāpesiṃ sake sisse gacchante jinassantikaṃ Durāsadā bhagavanto sihāva ekacārinoPade padaṃ nikkipantā āgacechayyātha māṇavā Āsiviso yathā ghoro migarājāva kesariMattocava kuñajaro danti evaṃ buddhā durāsadā Ukkāsitañca khipitaṃ ajjhupekkhiya māṇavāPade padaṃ nikkhipantā upetha buddhasantikaṃ Paṭisallānagarukā appasadā durāsadāDurūpasaṅkamā buddhā garū honti sadevake Yadāhaṃ pañhaṃ pucchāmi gaṭisammodayāmi vāAppasaddā tadā hotha munibhūtāva tiṭṭhatha  Yaṃ so deseti saddhammaṃ khemaṃ nibbaṇapattiyāTamevatthaṃ nisāvetha saddhammasavaṇaṃ sukhaṃ Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ sammodiṃ muninā ahaṃTaṃ kathaṃ vitasāretvā lakkhaṇe upadhārayiṃ Lakkhaṇe dveva kaṅkhāmi passāmi tiṃsalakkhaṇeKosobhitavatthaguyhaṃ iddhiyā dassayi muni Jivhaṃ ninnāmayitvāna kaṇṇasote ca nāsikePaṭimasi nalāṭantaṃ kevalaṃ chādayi jano Dhammānucchavasaṃvareṃ simu  Sambuddho machasaṃ  Dve ca machasaṃ  Tassāhaṃ lakkhaṇe disvā paripuṇṇe savyañajaneBuddhoti niṭṭhaṃ gantvāna saha sissehi pabbajiṃ Satehi tihi sahito pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃAddhamāse asampatte sabbe pattāmha nibbutiṃ Ekato kammaṃ katvāna puññakkhette anuttareEkato saṃsaritvāna ekato vinivattayuṃ Gopānasiyo davona pugadhamme vasī ahaṃTena kammena sukatena aṭṭahetu labhāmahaṃ Disāsu pujito homi bhogā ca amitā mamaPatiṭṭhā homi sabbesaṃ tāso mama na vijjati Vyādhayo me na vijjanti dighāyuṃ pālayāmi caSukhumacchaviko homi āvāse patthite vase Aṭṭha gopānasi datvā pugadhamme vasi ahaṃPaṭisambhidāehattañca etaṃ me aparaṭṭhamaṃ Sabbavositavosāno katakicco anāsavoAṭṭhagopānasi nāma tava putto mahāmuni Pañcathambhāni datvāna pugadhamme vasi ahaṃTena kammena sukatena pañcahetu labhāmahaṃ Acalo homi mettāya anunaṅgo bhavāmahaṃĀdeyyavacano homi na dhaṃsemi yathā ahaṃ Abhantaṃ hoti me cittaṃ acalo homi kassaciTena kammena sukatena vimalo homi sāsane  Sagāravo sappatisso katakicco anāsavoSāvako te mahāvīra bhikkhu taṃ vandate muni Katvā sukatapallaṅkaṃ sālāyaṃ paññapesahaṃTena kammena sukatena pañca hetu labhāmahaṃ Ucce kule pajāyitvā mahābhogo bhavāmahaṃSabbasampattiko homi maccheraṃ me na vijjati Gamane patthite mayhaṃ pallaṅko upatiṭṭhatiSaha pallaṅkaseṭṭhena gacchāmi mama patthitaṃ Casiṃ machasaṃ  Āvāse patte vase syā  Tena pallaṅkadānena tamaṃ sabbaṃ vinodayiṃSabbābhiññābalappatto thero candati taṃ muni Parakiccattakiccāni sabbakiccāni sādhayiṃTena kammena sukatena pāvisiṃ abhayaṃ puraṃ Pariniṭṭhitasālaṃ hi paribhogamadāsahaṃTena kammena sukatena seṭṭattaṃ ajjhupāgeto Ye keci damakā loke hatthi asse damenti yeKaritvā kāraṇā nānā dāruṇena dāmanti te Nahevaṃ tvaṃ mahāvīra damesi naranāriyoAdaṇḍena asatthena damesi uttame dame Dānassa vaṇṇe kittento desanākusalo muniEkaṃ pañahaṃ kathentova bodhesi tisate muni Dantā mayaṃ sārathinā suvimuttā anāsavāSabbābhiññābalappattā nibbutā upadhikkhāye Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadāAtikkantā bhayā sabbe sālādānassidaṃ phalaṃ Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā selo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Selattherassapadānaṃ dutiyaṃ  Ekapañahaṃ machasaṃ   Sabbakittikattherāpadānaṃ Kaṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ diparukkhaṃva ujjalaṃOsadhiṃva virovantaṃ vijjutaṃ gagane yathā Asambhitaṃ anutrāsiṃ migarājaṃva kesariṃÑāṇālokaṃ pakāsentaṃ maddantaṃ titthiye gaṇo Uddharantaṃ imaṃ lokaṃ chindantaṃ sabbasaṃsayaṃGajjantaṃ migarājaṃva addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ Jaṭājinadhāro āsiṃ bahā uju patāpavāVākaviraṃ gahetvāna pādamule avatthariṃ Kāḷānusāriyaṃ gayha anulimpiṃ tathāgataṃSambuddhamanulimpetvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ Samuddharasimaṃ lokaṃ oghatiṇṇa mahāmuniÑāṇālokena jotesi nāvaṭaṃ ñāṇamuttamaṃ Dhammacakkaṃ pavattesi maddase paratitthiyeUsabho jitasaṅgāmo sampakampesi medini Mahāsamuddo ūmiyo velantambhi pabhijjareTatheva tava ñāṇamhi sabbadiṭṭhi pabhijjare Sukhumacchikajālena sarambhi sampatāniteAntojālagatā pāṇā pilitā honti tāvade Tatheva titthiyā loke puthupāsaṇḍanissitāAntoñāṇavare tuyhaṃ parivattanti mārisa Patiṭṭhā vuyhataṃ oghe tvaṃ hi nātho abandhunaṃBhayaṭṭitānaṃ saraṇaṃ muttatthinaṃ parāyaṇaṃ Ekaviro asadiso karuṇāmettasañcayoSusilo asamo santo vasi tādi jitañajaso  Dhīro vigatasammoho anojo akathaṅkathiVusito vantadososi nimmalo payato suci Jalitaṃ machasaṃ  Jotitaṃ syā  Anuttāsiṃ machasaṃ  Asambhitaṃ syā  Oghatiṇṇosyā  Pavaraṃ syā vajira   Muttatthinaṃ machasaṃ Mettākaruṇā sañcayomachasaṃ saññuto syā  Asamo susamo satto machasaṃ  Tusito machasaṃ  Saṃyatomachasaṃ  Saṅgātigo hatamādā tevijjo tibhavattagoSimātigo dhammagaru katattho hitavappatho Tārako tvaṃ yathā nāvā nidhivassāsakārakoAsambhito yathā siho gajarājāva dassito Thometvā dasagāthāhi padumuttaraṃ mihāyasaṃVanditvā satthuno pāde tuṇhi aṭṭhāsahaṃ tadā Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggahoBhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo me silañca ñāṇañca dhammañcāpi pakittayiTamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Saṭṭhikappasahassāni devaloke ramissati aññe deve abhihotvā issaraṃ kārayissati So pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena coditoGotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissati Pabbajitvāna kāyena pāpakammaṃ vicajjiyaSabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo Yathāpi megho thanayaṃ tappeti mediniṃ imaṃTatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra dhammena tapapayi mamaṃ Sīlaṃ paññaca dhammañca thavitthā lokanāyakaṃPatombhi paramaṃ santiṃ nibbāṇaṃ padamaccutaṃ Aho nūna sa bhagavā ciraṃ tiṭṭheyya cakkhumāAññatañca vijaneyyuṃ phuseyyuṃ amataṃ padaṃ Ayaṃ me paccimā jāti bhavā sabbe samuhatāSabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ buddhamabhithomayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ Gatamado syā  Gatatthohitavabbhuto machasaṃ  Saddhammañcāpi vaṇṇayimachasaṃ  Aññe devebhibhavitvā machasaṃ  Nibbāyissatināsavo machasaṃ   Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sabbakittiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Sabbakittikattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  Madhudāyakattherāpadānaṃ Sindhuyā nadiyā tīre sukato assamo mamaTattha vācemahaṃ sisse itihāsaṃ salakkhaṇaṃ Dhammakāmā vinitā te sotukāmā susāsanaṃChaḷaṅge pāramippattā sindhukule vasatti te Upapātagamane ceva lakkhaṇesu ca kovidāUttamatthaṃ gavesantā vasati pavane tadā Sumedho nāma sambuddho loka uppajji tāvadoAmbhākaṃ anukampanto upagacchi vināyako Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃTiṇasatthārakaṃ kavo lokajeṭṭhassadāsahaṃ Pavanāto madhuṃ gayha buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃSambuddho pibhuñajitvā idaṃ vacanamabravi Yo taṃ adāsi madhuṃ me pasanno sehi pāṇihiTamahaṃ kittasissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Iminā dhudānena tiṇasatthārakena caTiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati Tiṃsakappasahasasamhi okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati Vipine machasaṃ  Vipanāto machasaṃ  Gottena machasaṃ  Tassa dhammesu dāyado oraso dhammanimmitoSabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo Devalokā idhāgantvā mātukucchiṃ upāgateMadhuvassaṃ pavassittha chādayaṃ madhunā mahiṃ Mayi nikkhantamattambhi kucchiyā ca suduttaraṃTatrāpi madhuvassaṃ me vassate niccakālikaṃ  Agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃLābhi annassa pānasa madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ Sabbakāmasamiddhohaṃ bhavitvā devamānuseTeneva madhudānena pattombhi āsavakkhayaṃ Vuṭṭhambhi deve caturaṅgule tiṇeSampupphite dharaṇiruhe sañachanneSuññe ghare maṇḍaparukkhamuleVasāmi niccaṃ sukhito anāsavo Majjhe mahante hine ca bhave sabbe atikkamiṃAjja me āsavā khiṇā nathidoni punabbhavo Tiṃsakappasahassamhi yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi
