Supupphite syā  Cappadese syā  Maṇḍaparukkhamulake machasaṃ  Majjhemayahaṃ bhavā assu syā   Ye bhave samatikkamiṃ syā   Padumakuṭāgāriyattherāpadānaṃ Piyadassi nāma bhagavā sayambhu lokāyakoVivekakāmo sambuddho samādhikusalo muni Vanasaṇḍaṃ samogayha piyadassi mahāmuniPaṃsukulaṃ pattharitvā nisīdi purisuttamo Migaluddo pure āsiṃ vipite kānane ahaṃPasadaṃ migamesante ābhiṇḍami ahaṃ tadā Tatthadadasāsiṃ sambuddheṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃPupphitaṃ sālarājāṃva sataraṃsiṃva uggataṃ Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ piyadassiṃ mahāyasaṃJātassaraṃ samogayha padumaṃ āhariṃ tadā Āharitvāna padumaṃ satapattaṃ manoramaṃKuṭāgāraṃ karitvāna chādayiṃ padumenahaṃ  Anukampako kāruṇiko piyadassi mahāmuniSattarattindivaṃ buddho kuṭāgāre vasi jino Purāṇaṃ chaḍḍhayitvāna navena chādayiṃ ahaṃAñjaliṃ paggahetvāna aṭṭhāsiṃ tāvade ahaṃ Vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā piyadassi mahāmuniDisā anucilokanto nisīdi lokanāyako Tadā sudassano nāma upaṭṭhāko mahiddhikoCittamaññāya buddhassa piyadassassa satthuno Asitāya sahassehi bhikkhuhi parivāritoVanante sukhamāsinaṃ upesi lokenāyakaṃ Yāvatā vanasaṇḍamhi adhivatthā ca devatāBuddhassa cittamaññāya sabbe santipatuṃ tadā Samāgatesu yakkhesu kumbhaṇḍe saha rakkhaseBhikkhusaṅghe ca sampatte gāthāmā vyāhari jiko Yo maṃ sattāhaṃ pujeyi āvāsañca akāsi meTamahaṃ kintiyissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato Araññe machasaṃ  Gāthā pabyāhari machasaṃ gāthā sabyāhari syā  Sududadasaṃ sunipuṇaṃ gambhiraṃ suppakāsitaṃÑāṇena kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Catuddasāni kappāni devarajjaṃ karissatiKuṭāgāraṃ brahaṃ tassa padumapupphehi chāditaṃĀkāse dhārayissati pupphakammassidaṃ phalaṃ Catubbise kappasate vokiṇṇaṃ saṃsarissatiTattha pupphamayaṃ vyamahaṃ ākāse dhārayissati Yathā padumapattambhi toyaṃ na upalimpatiTathevimassa cañāṇamhi kilesā nopalimpare Manasā vinivaṭṭhetvā pañcanivaraṇe ayaṃCittaṃ janetvā nekkhamme agārā pabbajissatiTato pupphamaye vyambhe dhārente nikkhamissati Rukkhamule vasantassa nipakassa satimatoTattha pupphamayaṃ vyamhaṃ matthake dhārayissati Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃDatvāna bhikkhusaṅghassa nibbāyissatanāsavo Kūṭāgārena caratā pabbajjaṃ abhinikkhamiṃRukkhamule vasantamhi kūṭāgāraṃ dhariyati  Cīvare piṇḍapāte ca cetanā me na vijjatiPuññakammena saṃyutto labhāmi pariniṭṭhataṃ Gaṇanāto asaṃkheyyā kappakoṭi bahu mamaRittakā te atikkantā pamutatā lokanāyakā Aṭṭhārase kappasate piyadasasi vināyakoTamahaṃ payirupāsitvā imaṃ yoniṃ upāgato Idhaddasāsiṃ sambudadhaṃ anomaṃ nāma cakkhumaṃTamahaṃ upagantvāna pabbajaṃ anagāriyaṃ Dukkhassantakaro buddho maggaṃ me adesasi jinoTassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāna pattomahi acalaṃ padaṃ Tosayitvāna sambudadhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃSabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anasāvo Mahantassa machasaṃ  Padamapupphehi machasaṃ  Pupphamayaṃ vyambhaṃdhārentaṃ machasaṃ  Caraṇā simu  caete syā  Casantampi machasaṃ  Idhapassāmi machasaṃ  Aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ buddamabhipujayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāSabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumakuṭāgāriyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Padumakuṭāgāriyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ  Bakkulattherāpadānaṃ  Hivamantassa avidūre sobhito nāma pabbatoAssamo sukato mayhaṃ sakasissehi māpito Maṇḍapā ca bahu tattha pupphitā sinduvārakāKapitthā ca bahu tattha pupphitā jivajivakā Nigguṇḍiyo bahu tattha badarāmalakāni caPhārusakā alābu ca puṇḍarikā ca pupphitā Ālakā beluvā tattha kadali mātuluṅgakāMahānāmā bahu tattha ajjuṇā ca piyaṅgukā  Kosambā salalā nipā nigrodhā ca kapitthanāEdiso assamo mayhaṃ sasissohaṃ tahiṃ vasiṃ Anomadassi bhagavā sayambhu lokanāyakoGavesaṃ paṭisallānaṃ mamassamamupāgami Upetamhi mahāvire anomadassimahāyaseKhaṇena lokanāthassa vātābādo samuṭṭhahi Vicaratto araññamhi addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃUpagantvāna sambuddhaṃ cakkhumantaṃ mahāyasaṃ Iriyañcāpi disvāna upalakkhesahaṃ tadāAsaṃsayaṃ hi buddhassa vyādhi no upapajjatha Campakā nāma ketakā syā  Āḷakā machasaṃ aḷakkā syā  Udapajjatha machasaṃbākulattherāpadāna machasaṃ  Khippaṃ assamamāgacchiṃ mama sissāna santikeBhesajjaṃ kattukāmohaṃ sisse āmantayiṃ tadā Paṭissuṇitvā me vākyaṃ sissā sabbe sagāravāEkajjhaṃ sannipatiṃsu satthugāravatā mama Kippaṃ pabbatamāruyha sabbosadhamahāsahaṃPāniyayogaṃ katvāna buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ Paribhutte mahāvire sabbaññulokanāyakeKhippaṃ vāto vupasami sugatassasa mahesino Passaddhaṃ darathaṃ disvā anomadassi mahāyasoSakāsane nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo me pādāsi bhesajajaṃ vyādhiñca samayi mamaTamahaṃ kittayisasāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Kappasatasahassani devaloke ramissatiVādite turiye tattha modissati sadā ayaṃ Manussalokamāgantvā sukkamūlena coditoSahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati Pañcapaññāsakappamhi anomo nāma khattiyoCaturanto vijitivi jambumaṇḍassa issaro Sattaratanampanno cakkavatti mahabbaloTāvatiṃsepi khebhetvā issaraṃ kārayissati  Devabhuto manusso vā appabādho bhavissatiPariggahaṃ vivajjetvā vyādhiṃ loke tarissati Aparimeyye ito kappe okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati Tassa dhammesu dāyado oraso dhammanimmitoSabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo Kilese jhāpayitvāna taṇhāsotaṃ tarissatiBakakulo nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako Idaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavoBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapessati Pāniyayoggaṃ katvā simu  Jambudipassa syā  Gottena machasaṃ  Bākulomachasaṃ  Anomadassi bhagavā sayambhu lokanāyakoVivekānuvilokanto mamassamamupāgami Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ sabbaññuṃ lokanāyakaṃSabbosadhena tappesiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi Tassa me sukataṃ sukhette bijasampadāKhepetuṃ neva sakkomi tadā hi sukataṃ mama Lābhā mama suladdhaṃ me yohaṃ adadakkhi nāyakaṃTena kammāvasesena pattombhi acalaṃ padaṃ Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavoBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ Aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhesajjassa idaṃ phalaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāSabbesavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bakakulo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Bakakulattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ  Girimānandattherāpadānaṃ Bhariyā me kālakatā putto sivathikaṃ gatoMātā pitā ca bhāta ca ekacitakamhi ḍayhare Tena sokena santatto kiso paṇḍu ahosahaṃCittakkhepo ca me āsi tena sokena aṭṭito  Sokapallaparetohaṃ vanantamupasaṅkamiṃPavattaphalaṃ bhuñjitvā rukkhamule vasāmahaṃ Sumedho nāma sambuddho dukkhassantakāro jinoMamuddharitukāmo so āgacchi mama santike  Padasaddaṃ suṇitvāna sumedhassa mahesinoPaggahetvānahaṃ sisiṃ ullokesiṃ mahāmuniṃ Upagacchi mahāvīro piti me upapajjathaTadāsi mekaggamano disvāna taṃ lokanāyakaṃ Satiṃ paṭilabhitvāna paṇṇamuṭṭhimadāsahaṃNisīdi bhagavā tattha anukampāya cakkhumaṃ Nisajja tattha bhagavā sumedho lokanāyakoDhammaṃ me kathayi buddho sokasallavinodanaṃ Anavahitā tato āguṃ ananuññātā ito gatāYathāgatā tathā gatā tattha kā paridevanā Yathāpi pathikā sattā vassamānāya vuṭṭhiyāSabhaṇḍā upagacchanti vassassāpatanāya te Vasse ca te oramite sampayanti yadicchakaṃEvaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ kattha kā paridevatā Āgantukā pāhuṇakā caliteritakampitāEvaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ tattha kā paridevatā Yathāpi urago jiṇṇaṃ hitvā gacchati santacaṃEvaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ santuṃ idha hīyare Buddhassa giramaññāya sokalassaṃ vivajjayiṃPāmojjaṃ janayitvāna buddhaseṭṭhamavandihaṃ Vanditvāna mahānāgaṃ girimañajarimapujayiṃDibbagandhena sampannaṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ Pujayitvāna sambuddhaṃ sire katvāna añjaliṃAnussaraṃ guṇaggāni santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ  Nittiṇṇosi mahāvīra sabbaññu lokanāyakaSabbe satte uddharasi ñāṇena tvaṃ mahāmune Vimatiṃ dveḷahakaṃ cāpi sañachindasi mahāmuniPaṭipadesi me maggaṃ tava ñāṇena cakkhuma Arahā siddhipattā ca chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikāAntalikkhacarā dhīrā parivārenti tāvade Upāgate mahāvire machasaṃ  Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandahaṃ machasaṃ  Pujayiṃgirimañajariṃ machasaṃ  Dibbagandhaṃ sampavattaṃ machasaṃ  Tittaṇehāsi katthavi Vasippantā ca machasaṃ  Paṭipannā ca sekhā ca phalaṭṭhā santi sāvakāSurodayeva padumā pupphanti tava sāvakā Yathā samuddo akkhobho atulo ca duruttaroEvaṃ ñaṇena sampanno appameyyosi cakkhuma Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃDisvāna cittamāpajjaṃ satto ko nāmayaṃ bhave Lakkhaṇāni viloketvā mama vijjaṃ anussariṃSutaṃ hi metaṃ vuddhānaṃ paṇḍitānaṃ subhāsitaṃ Tesaṃ yathā taṃ saritvāna bhiyo hāsaṃ janesahaṃ Tusitāhaṃ cavitvāna okkamiṃ mātukucchiyaṃJāyamānassa sattassa āloko vipulo ahu Agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃBācariṃ upasaṅkamma sissattaṃ ajjhupāgamiṃ pajānasiTuvamaggiṃ paricara handa te aggidārukaṃ  Tato kaṭṭhaṃ gahetvāna aggiṃ ujjālayī jinoNa tattha kaṭṭhaṃ pajjhāyi pāṭihīraṃ mahesino Na te aggi pajjalati āhutī te na vijjatiNiratthakaṃ vataṃ tuyhaṃ aggiṃ paricarassu me  Kīdiso so mahāvīra aggi tava pavuccatiMahampi kathayassetaṃ ubho parivarāmase  Metteyyattherāpadānaṃ sīmu Bhohiti machasaṃ Tuvaṃ aggiṃ machasaṃ  Pāṭibheraṃ machasaṃ Te syā  Hetudhamma nirodhāya kilesasamanāya caIssā macchariyaṃ hitvā tayo ete mamāhunī  Kīdiso tvaṃ mahāvīra kathaṃ gottosi mārisaĀcārapaṭipatti te bāḷahaṃ kho mama ruccatī Khattiyamhi        kule jāto abhiññā pāramiṃ gatoSabbāsavaparikkhiṇo natthidāni punabbhavo  Yadi buddhosi sabbaññū pabhaṅkara tamonudaNamassissāmi taṃ deva dukkhassantakaro tuvaṃ Pattharitvā jinacammaṃ nisīdana madāsahaṃNisīda nātha sabbaññu upaṭṭhissamahaṃ tuvaṃ Nisīdi bhagavā tattha ajinamhi suvitthateNimantayitvā sambuddhaṃ pabbataṃ agamāsahaṃ Khāribhārañca pūretvā tindukaphalamāhariṃMadhunā yojayitvāna phalaṃ buddhassa dāsahaṃ Mama nijjhāyamānassa paribhuñji tadā jinoTattha cittaṃ pasādesiṃ pekkhanto lokanāyakaṃ Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahoMamassame nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo maṃ phalena tappesi pasanno sehi pāṇihiTamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Pañcavīsatikkhattuṃ so devarajjaṃ karissatiSahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati Tassa saṅkappamaññāya pubbakammasamaṅginoAnnaṃ pānañca vatthañca sayanañca anāmayo Puññakammena saṃyuttā nibbattissanti tāvadeSadā pamudito cāyaṃ bhavissati anāmayo Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattaṃ atha mānusaṃSabbattha sukhito hutvā manussattaṃ gamissati Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāraguSambuddhamupagantvāna arahā so bhavissati   Yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato pattosmi viññutaṃBhoge me ūnatā natthi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ Varadhammamanuppatto rāgadose samūhaniṃSabbāsavaparikkhiṇo natthidāni punabbhavo Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tissametteyyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiTissametteyyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhama Puṇṇakattherāpadānaṃ Pabbhārakūṭaṃ        nissāya sayambhu aparājitoĀbādhiko garu buddho vasatī pabbatantare Mama assamasāmantā panādo āsi tāvadeBuddhe nibbāyamānambhi āloko upapajjatha  Yāvatā vanasaṇḍasmiṃ acchakokataracchakāVyagghā ca kesarī sabbe abhigajjiṃsu tāvade Uppānaṃ tamahaṃ disvā pabbataṃ agamāsahaṃTatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ nibbutaṃ aparājitaṃ Suphullaṃ sālarājaṃva sataraṃsiṃva uggataṃVītaccikaṃva aṅgāraṃ nibbutaṃ aparājitaṃ Tiṇaṃ kaṭṭhañca pūretvā citakaṃ tatthakāsahaṃCitakaṃ sukataṃ katvā sarīraṃ jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ Sarīraṃ jhāpayitvāna gandhatoyaṃ samokiriṃAntalikkhe ṭhito yakkho nāmamaggahi tāvade Yaṃ pūritaṃ tayā kiccaṃ sayambhussa mahesinoPuṇṇako nāma nāmena sadā bhohi tuvaṃ mune  Ābādhiko ca so buddho machasaṃ Ādi tāvade syā udapajjatha machasaṃ Vāḷā machasaṃ Pabbhāraṃ machasaṃ Taṃ puritaṃ syā Yadā hosi syā Muni sīmu  Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna devalokaṃ agacchahaṃTattha dibbamayo gandho antalikkhe pavāyati Tatrāpi nāmadheyyaṃ me puṇṇakoti ahū tadāDevabhūto manusso vā saṅkappaṃ pūrayāmahaṃ Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattatī bhagavāIdhāpi puṇṇako nāma nāmadheyyaṃ pakāsati Tosayitvāna sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃSabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadāSabbāsavā nābhijānāmi tanukiccassidaṃ phalaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatāSabbāsavā parikkhiṇā viharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇṇako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiPuṇṇakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ Mettaguttherāpadānaṃ Himavantassa        avidūre asoko nāma pabbatoTatthāsi assamo mayhaṃ vissakammena māpito Sumedho nāma sambuddho aggo kāruṇiko muniNivāsayitvā pubbanhe piṇḍāya maṃ upāgami Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃPaggayha sugatappattaṃ sappitelena pūrayiṃ Datvānahaṃ buddhaseṭṭhe sumedhe lokanāyakeAñjalimpaggahetvāna bhīyo hāsaṃ janesahaṃ Iminā sappidānena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caDevabhūto manusso vā labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ Vinipātaṃ vivajjetvā saṃsarāmi bhavābhaveTattha cittaṃ paṇidhitvā labhāmi acalaṃ padaṃ  Antalikkhā pavassati machasaṃ Vattate machasaṃ Ekanavutito kappe machasaṃ Himavattassāvidure machasaṃ Visukammena sīmu Sugataṃ pattaṃ sīmu Subhakaṃ pattaṃ  Sappitelaṃ apūrayiṃ machasaṃ Bhiyyo machasaṃ  Lābhā tuyhaṃ suladdhaṃ te yaṃ maṃ addakkhi brāhmaṇaṃ Mama dassanamāgamma arahā tvaṃ bhavissasi Vissattho hohi mā bhiyi adhigantvā mahāyasaṃMamaṃ hi sappiṃ datvāna parimokkhasi jātiyā Iminā sappidānena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caDevabhūto manusso vā labhase vipulaṃ sukhaṃ Iminā sappidānena mettacittavatāya caAṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissasi Aṭṭhatiṃsatikkhattuñca devarājā bhavissasiPadesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissasiCāturanto vijitāvī jambusaṇḍassa issaro Mahāsamuddovakkhobho duddharo paṭhavi yathāEvameva ca te bhogā appameyyā bhavissare  Saṭṭhikoṭi bhiraññassa cajitvā pabbajiṃ ahaṃKiṃ kusalaṃ gavesanto bāvariṃ upasaṅkamiṃ Tattha        mante adhīyāmi chaḷaṅgaṃ nāma lakkhaṇaṃTamandhakāraṃ vidhamaṃ uppajjitvaṃ mahāmuni Tava dassanakāmohaṃ āgatomhi mahāmuniTava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ Tiṃsakappasahassamhi sappiṃ buddhassadāsahaṃEtthantare nābhijāne sappi viññāpitaṃ mayā Mama saṅkappamaññāya uppajjati yadicchakaṃCittamaññāya nibbattaṃ sabbe santappayāmahaṃ Aho buddho aho dhammo aho no satthusampadāThokaṃ hi sappiṃ datvāna appameyyaṃ labhāmahaṃ Mahāsamudde udakaṃ yāvatā nerupassatoMama sappiṃ upādāya kalabhāgaṃ na phassati Brāhmaṇa machasaṃ Jambumaṇḍassa machasaṃ Catvā na sīmu datvāna syā Sappiṃ viññāpitaṃ mayā machasaṃ Aho buddhā aho dhammā machasaṃ Na hessati machasaṃ Hissati syā  Yāmatā cakkavāḷassa kariyantassa rāsitoMama nibbattavatvatthānaṃ okāso so na sammati Pabbatarājā himavā pavaropi siluccayoMamānulittagandhassa upanidhiṃ na hessati Vatthaṃ gandhañca sappiñca aññañca diṭṭhadhammikaṃAsaṅkhatañca nibbānaṃ sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ Satipaṭṭhānasayano samādhijhānagotaroBojjhaṅgabhojano ajja sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ ādhismā mettagutthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiMettaguttherassa apadānaṃ katiyaṃ Dhotakattherāpadānaṃ Gaṅgā bhāgirathi nāma himavantā pabhāvitāHaṃsavatiyā dvārena anusandati tāvade Sobhito nāma ārāmo gaṅgākūle sumāpitoTattha padumuttaro buddho vasate lokanāyako Tidasehi        yathā indo manujehi purakkhatoNisīdi tattha bhagavā asambhitova kesarī Nagare haṃsavatiyā vasāmi brāhmaṇo ahaṃChaḷaṅgo nāma nāmena evannāmo mahāmuni Aṭṭhārasasissasatā parivārenti maṃ tadāTehi sissehi samito gaṅgātīrā upāgamiṃ Tatthaddasāsiṃ samaṇe nikkuhe dhotapāpakeBhāgīrathiṃ tarantehaṃ evaṃ cittesi tāvade Kārayantassa syā Kayirantassa  Upanidhaṃ simu Bojjhaṅgajanano syā Ahosiṃ syā Tarantohaṃ syā  Sāyaṃ pātaṃ tarantāme buddhaputtā mahāyasāVihesayanti attānaṃ tesaṃ attā vihaññati Sadevakassa lokassa buddho aggo pavuccatiNatthi me dakkhiṇe kāraṃ gatimaggavisodhanaṃ Yannūna buddhaseṭṭhassa setuṃ gaṅgāya kārayeKārāpetvā imaṃ kammaṃ santarāmi imaṃ bhavaṃ  Satasahassaṃ datvāna setuṃ kārāpayiṃ ahaṃSaddahanto kataṃ kārāṃ vipulaṃ me bhavissati  Kārāpetvāna taṃ setuṃ upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃSirasi añjaliṃ katvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Satasahassassa vayaṃ katvā kārāpito mayāTavatthāya mahāsetu paṭigaṇha mahāmuni  Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahoBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo me setuṃ akāresi pasanno sehi pāṇihi tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mamabhāsato Darito pabbatātovā rukkhāto patitopayaṃCutopi lacchati ṭhānaṃ setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ Nāssa corā pasahanti nātimaññanti khattiyāSabbe tarissanāmitte setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ Abbhokāsagataṃ        santaṃ kaṭhinātapatāpitaṃPuññakammena saṃyuttaṃ na bhavissanti cedanā Devaloke manusse vā hatthiyānaṃ sunimmitaṃTassasa saṅkappamaññāya nibbattissati tāvade Sahassassā vātajavā sindhavā sīghavāhanāSāyaṃ pātaṃ upessanti setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ Āgantvāna manussattaṃ sukhitoyaṃ bhavissatiIhāpi manujasseva hatthiyānaṃ bhavissati Datvā machasaṃ Pabbatato Avandihaṃ machasaṃ Upasīvo nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako syā  Nandakattherāpadānaṃ Migaluddo        pure āsiṃ araññe kānate ahaṃPasadaṃ migamesanto sayambhuṃ addasaṃ jinaṃ   Anuruddho nāma sambuddhosayambhū aparājitoVivekakāmo so dhīro vanamajjhogahī tadā Catudaṇḍe gahetvāna catuṭṭhāne ṭhapesahaṃMaṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā padamapupphehi chādayiṃ Maṇḍapaṃ chādayitvāna sayambhuṃ abhivādayiṃDhanuṃ tattheva nikkhippa pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ Pabbajitassa aciraṃ vyādhi me upapajjathaPubbakammaṃ saritvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ Pubbakammena saṃyutto tusitaṃ agamāsahaṃTattha soṇṇamayaṃ vyamhaṃ nibbattati yadicchakaṃ Sahassayuttahavāhiṃ dibbayānamadhiṭṭhitoĀruhitvāna taṃ yānaṃ gacchāmahaṃ yadicchakaṃ Tato me nīyamānassa devabhūtassa me satoSamantā yojanasataṃ maṇḍapo me dharīyati Sayanehaṃ tuvaṭṭāmi accantaṃ pupphasanthateAntaḷikkhā ca padumā vassanti niccakālikaṃ Marīvike phandamāne tappamāne ca ātapeNa maṃ tāpeti ātāpo maṇḍassa idaṃ phalaṃ Duggatiṃ samatikkanto apāyā pihitā mamaMaṇḍape rukkhamūle vā santāpo me na vijjati Mahīsaññaṃ adhiṭṭhāya loṇatoyaṃ tarāmahaṃTassa me sukataṃ kammaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Apathampi pathaṃ katvā gacchāmi anilañjaseAho me sukataṃ kammaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Pubbenivāsaṃ        jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃĀsavā me parikkhiṇā buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Jahitā purimā jāni buddhassa oraso ahaṃDāyādomhi ca saddhamme buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Ahaṃ machasaṃ Na ciraṃ pabbajitassa machasaṃ Acchante machasaṃ Vassante machasaṃ Abbhamhi syā  Ārādhitomhi sugataṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃDhammaddhajo dhammadāyādo buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Upaṭṭhitvāna sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃPāraṅgamaniyaṃ maggaṃ apucchiṃ lokanāyakaṃ Ajjhiṭṭho kathayī buddho gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ padaṃTassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ parimuttomhi jātiyāSabbāsavaparikkhiṇo natthidāni punabbhavo Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ sabbe samūhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā muni Visārado sasamaye paravāde ca kovidoPaṭṭho bhūmantalikkhambhi uppātambhi ca kovido Vītasoko nirārambho appāhāro alolupoLābhālābhena santuṭṭho jhāyī jhānarato muni Piyadassī nāma sambuddho aggo Sikkhāpayissati machasaṃ Bheriyo machasaṃ  Catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissatiPadesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ Anūnabhogo hutvāna manussattaṃ gamissati Ajjhāyako bhavitvāna tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragūUttamatthaṃ gavesanto carissati mahiṃ imaṃ So pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena coditoGotamassa bhagavato sāsanebhi ramissati Ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃKilese jhāpayitvāna arahāyaṃ bhavissati Vipine vyaggharājāva migarājāva kesarīAbhīto viharāmajja sakyaputtassa sāsane Devaloke manusse vā daḷidde duggatimbhi vāNibbattiṃ me na passāmi upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ Vivekamanuyuttombhi upasanto nirūpadhiNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ gavā sabbe samūhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jatukaṇṇithero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiJatukaṇṇittherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ Gottena machasaṃ Ārādhayitvāna machasaṃ  Udenattherāpadānaṃ Himavantassa        avidūre padumo nāma pabbatoAssamo sukato mayhaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā Nadiyo sandare supatitthā manoramāAcchodakā sītajalā sundarā nadiyo sadā Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā muñjarohitāSobhentā nadiyo ete vasanti nadiyā sadā Ambajambūhi sañchannā kareritilakā tathāUddālakā pāṭaliyo sobhenti mama assamaṃ Aṅkolakā bimbijālā māyākārī ca pupphitāGandhena upavāyantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Atimuttā sattalikā nāgā sālā ca pupphitāDibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Kosambā salalā nīpā aṭṭhaṅgā ca supupphitāDabbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assama Harītakā āmalakā ambajambu vibhīṭakāKolā bhallātakā billā phalāni bahu assame Kalambā kandalī tattha pupphanti mama assameDibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Asokapiṇḍī cavarī nimbarukkhā ca pupphitāDibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Punnāgā giripunnāgā timirā tattha pupphitāDibbagandhaṃ smapavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Nigguṇḍī sirinigguṇḍī camparukkhettha pupphitāDibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Avidūre pokkharaṇī cakkavākūpakūjitāMandalakehi sañchannā padumuppalakehi ca Sandare machasaṃ Dibbagandhā sīmu Asokapiṇḍicārī va machasaṃ  Acchodakā        sītajalā supatitthā manoramāAcchā phalikasamānā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Padumā pupphare tattha puṇḍarīkā ca uppalāMandalakehi sañchannā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchāvalajā muñjarohitāVicarantā ca te tattha sobhenti mama assamaṃ Kumbhīlā suṃsumārā ca kacchapā ca gahā bahūOguhā ajagarā ca sobhenti mama assamaṃ Pārevatā ravihaṃsā cakkavākā nadīcarāDindibhā sālikā cettha sobhenti mama assamaṃ Nayitā ambagandhī ca ketakā tattha pupphitāDibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ Sīhā vyagghā ca dīpī ca acchakokataracchakāAnusañcarantā pavane sobhenti mama assamaṃ Jaṭābhārena bharitā ajinuttaravāsanāAnusañcarantā pavane sobhenti mama assamaṃ Ajīnāni dharā ete nipakā santavuttinoAppahārā ca te sabbe sobhenti mama assamaṃ Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna ajjhogayha vanaṃ tadāMūlaphalāni bhuñjantā vasanti assame sadā Na te dāruṃ āharanti udakaṃ pādadhovanaṃSabbesaṃ ānubhāvena sayamevāharīyati Cullāsīti sahassāni isayettha samāgatāSabbeva jhāyino ete uttamatthagavesakā Tapassīno brahmacārī codentā appaṇāvateAmbarāvacarā sabbe vasanti assame tadā Pañcāhaṃ sannīpatanti ekaggā santavuttinoAññoññaṃ abhivādetvā pakkamanti disāmukhā Ogahā machasaṃ  Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragūTamandakāraṃ vidhamaṃ uppajji tāvade jino Mama        assamasāmantā yakkho āsi mahiddhikoSo me saṃsittha sambuddhaṃ jalajuttamanāyakaṃ Esa buddho samuppanno padumuttaro mahāmuniKhippaṃ gantvāna sambuddhaṃ payirupāsaya mārisa Yakkhassa vacanaṃ sutvā vippasannena cetasāAssamaṃ saṃsāmetvāna nikkhamiṃ vipinā tadā Ceḷeva ḍayhamānambhi nikkhamitvāna assamāEkarattiṃ nivasitvā upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahoCatusaccaṃ pakāsonto desesi amataṃ padaṃ Supullaṃ padumaṃ gayha upagantvā mahesinoPasannacitto sumano buddhassa abhiropayiṃ Pūjayitvāna sambuddhaṃ jalajuttamanāyakaṃEkaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ Yena ñāṇena sambuddho vasatīha anāsavoTaṃ ñāṇaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato Saṃsārasotaṃ chinditvā tāresi sabbapāṇinoTava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna taṇhāsotaṃ taranti te Tuvaṃ satthā ca ketu ca dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃParāyaṇo patiṭṭhā ca dīpo ca dipaduttama  Yāvatā gaṇino loke satthavāhā pavuccareTuvaṃ aggosi sabbaññu tava antogadhāva te Tava ñāṇena sabbaññu tāresi janataṃ bahuṃTava dassanamāgamma dukkhassantaṃ karissare Ye keci me gandhajātā loke vāyanti cakkhumaTava gandhasamo natthi puññakkhette mahāmune Mahandhakāraṃ sīmu Payirupāsa machasaṃ Nivāsetvā machasaṃ Dvīpaduttama machasaṃ  Tiracchānayoniṃ nirayaṃ parimocesi cakkhumaAsaṃkhataṃ padaṃ santaṃ desesitvaṃ mahāmune Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahoBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo        me ñāṇaṃ apūjesi pasanno sehi pāṇihiTamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissatiSahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati  Suladdhalābhaṃ laddhombhi tosayitvāna subbataṃSabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā vibharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChalabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udeno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiUdenattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃUddānaṃMetteyyo puṇṇako thero mettagū dhotakopi caUpasīvo ca nando ca hemako sattamo tahiṃTodeyyo jatukaṇṇī ca udeno ca mahāyasoTīṇi gāthāsatānettha asīti tīṇi cuttarīṃMetteyyavaggo ekacattāḷīsatimo  Parimocehi syā Desehi syā Ekacattāḷīsamo sīmu machasaṃ  Bhaddālittherāpadānaṃ Sumedho nāma sambuddho aggo kāruṇiko muniVivekakāmo lokaggo himavantamupāgami Ajjhogahetvā himavaṃ sumedho lokanāyakoPallaṅkamābhujitvāna nisīdi purisuttamo Samādhiṃ so samāpanto sumedho lokanāyakoSattarattindivaṃ buddho nisīdi purisuttamo Khārikājaṃ gahetvāna vanamajjhogahiṃ ahaṃTatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna sammajjitvāna assamaṃCatudaṇḍe thambhītvāna akāsiṃ maṇḍapaṃ tadā Sālapupphaṃ        āharitvā maṇḍapaṃ jādayiṃ ahaṃPasannacitto sumano abhivandiṃ tathāgataṃ Yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Buddhassa giramañña sabbe devā samāgamuṃAsaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho imā gāthā abhāsatha Sumedho nāma sambuddho āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahoDevasaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo me sattāhaṃ maṇḍapaṃ dhārayī sālachāditaṃTamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Devabhūto manusso vā hemavaṇṇo bhavissatiPahūtabhogo hutvāna kāmabhogī bhavissati Saṭṭhināgasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitāSuvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā hemakappanavāsasā Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅgusapāṇihiSāyaṃpāto upaṭṭhānaṃ āgamissantimaṃ naraṃTehi nāgehi parivuto ramissati ayaṃ naro Bāribhāraṃ  machasaṃ  hapetvāna  machasaṃ Sāyapāto    Saṭṭhīassahasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitāĀjānīyā va jāniyā sindhavā sīghavāhino Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi illiyācāpadhārihiParivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Saṭṭhirathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitāDīpā athopi veyyagghā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi cāpahatthehi vammihiParivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Saṭṭhigāmasahassāni paripuṇṇāni sabbasoPahūtadhanadhaññāni susamiddhāni sabbasoSadā pātubhavissanti buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Hatthi assā rasā patti senā ca caturaṅginiParivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissatiSahassakkhattuṃ rājā dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmitoSabbāsave pariññāya viharissatanāsavo Tiṃsakappasahassambhi addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃEtthantaramupādāya gavesiṃ amataṃ padaṃ Lābhā mayhaṃ suladdhaṃ me yamahaññāsi Setacchattaṃ gahetvāna buddhaseṭṭhassa dhārayiṃEkāhaṃ dhārayitvāna buddhaseṭṭhamavandahaṃ Atthadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabhoBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo me chattamadhāresi nāsento uppajjissati cakkhumā Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmitoSabbāsave pariññāya viharissatanāsavo  Yato ahaṃ kammamakaṃ chattaṃ buddhassa dhārayaṃEtthantare na jānāmi setacchattaṃ adhāritaṃ sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekachattiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiEkachattiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ Tiṇasulakachadaniyattherāpadānaṃ Jātijarañca maraṇaṃ paccavekkhiṃ nānādijagaṇāyuto Mamupenti ca vissatthā kūjanti ca manoharaṃRamamāno saha tehi vasāmi assame ahaṃ Mama assamasāmantā migarājā catukkamoĀsayā abhinikkhamma gajji so asanī viya Nidite        migarāje ca pūjanāya ca  Sīsaṃ nahāto cayaṃ poso pupphamākaṅkhate yadiPuññakammena saṃyutto purato pātubhavissati Yaṃ yaṃ icchati kāmehi taṃ taṃ pātubhavissatiSaṃkappaṃ paripūretvā nibbāyissatanāsavo Aṭṭhārasamaṃ paccaye sayanāsaneTattha me ūnatā natthi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Sodāni patto amataṃ santaṃ padamanuttaraṃSabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃDuggatiṃ coditoPacchime vattamānambhi kilese jhāpayissati Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃTattha bhutvā pivitvā ca labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā pubbakammaṃ viharāmi anāsavo Ekanavute        ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ madhumaṃsadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiMadhumaṃsadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ Nāgapallavakattherāpadānaṃ Nagare bandhumatiyā rājuyyāne vasāmahaṃMama assamasāmantā nisīdi lokanāyako Nāgapallavamādāya buddhassa abhiropayiṃ pasannacitto sumano sugataṃabhivādayiṃ Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pallavamapūjayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ Madhudānena machasaṃ Ekadīpiyattherāpadānaṃ Parinibbutambhi sugate siddhatthe lokanāyakeSadevamānusā sabbe pūjenti dipaduttamaṃ Āropite ca citake siddhatthe lokanāyakeYathāsakena thāmena citaṃ pūjenti satthuno Avidūre citakassa dīpamujjālayiṃ ahaṃYāva udeti suriyo dīpaṃ me tāva ujjali Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ Tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ ekadīpiti ñāyatiDīpasatasahassāni vyamhe pajjalare mama Udayantoma        suriyo deho me jotate sadāSabbabhāhi sarīrassa āloko hoti me sadā Tirokuḍḍaṃ tiroselaṃ sasamatiggayhaṃ pabbataṃSamantā yojanasataṃ passāmi cakkhunā ahaṃ Sattasattatikkhattuñca devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃEkatiṃsatikkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃ Aṭṭhivīsatikkhattuñca cakkavattī ahosahaṃPadesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ Devalokā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhasaññako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiBuddhasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ Dullabhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  machasaṃ Āyanatī nāgapotāca  Buddhasaññayidaṃ sabbattha  Bhisadāyakattherāpadānaṃ Ogayhāhaṃ pokkharaṇiṃ nānākuñjarasevitaṃUddharāmi bhisaṃ tattha ghāsahetu ahaṃ tadā Bhagavā tamhi samaye padumuttarasavhayoRattambaradharo buddho gacchati anilañjase Dhunanto paṃsukūlāni saddamassosahaṃ tadāUddhaṃ nijjhāyamānohaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ Tattheva ṭhitako santo āyāciṃ lokanāyakaṃMadhuṃ bhisehi sahitaṃ khīraṃ sappiṃ muḷālikaṃ  Patigaṇhātu me buddho anukampāya cakkhumāTato kāruṇiko satthā oruhitvā mahāyaso Paṭigaṇhi mamaṃ bhikkhuṃ anukampāya cakkhumāPaṭiggahetvā sambuddho akā me anumodanaṃ Sukhī hohi mahāpuñña gati tuyhaṃ samijjhatuIminā bhisadānena labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  Idaṃ        vatvāna sambuddho jalajuttamanāmakoBhikkhamādāya sambuddho ambarena gamā jino Tato bhisaṃ gahetvāna sañcālesi vanaṃ tadāĀkāso abhinādittha asaniyā phalantiyā Mahāvāto vuṭṭhahitvā sañcālesi vanaṃ tadāĀkāyo abhinādittha asaniyā phalantiyā Tato me asanīpāto matthake nipati tadāSohaṃ nisinnako santo tattha kālakato ahuṃ Puññakammena saṃyutto tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃKalekharaṃ me patitaṃ devaloke ramiṃ abhaṃ Chaḷāsītisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatāSāyapātaṃ upaṭṭhanti bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Manussayo nimāgantvā sukhito homahaṃ sadāBhoge me ūnatā natthi bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Anukampitako tena devadevena tādināSabbāsavaparikkhīṇo natthidāni punabbhavo Madhūbhisehi sacati khīrasappimuḷālihi machasaṃ   Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ bhikkhamadadiṃ tadāDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa caAnvesanto ācariyaṃ vasāmi ekako ahaṃ Sumedho nāma sambuddho loke uppajji tāvadeCatusaccaṃ pakāseti uddharanto mahājanaṃ Nāhaṃ suṇomi sambuddhaṃ napi me kovi bhāsatiAṭṭhavasse atikkante assosiṃ lokanāyakaṃ Aggidāruṃ        nīharitvā sammajjitvāna assamaṃKhāribhāraṃ gahetvāna nikkamiṃ vipinā ahaṃ Ekarattiṃ vasantohaṃ gāmesu nigamesu caAnupubbena candavatiṃ tadāhaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ Bhagavā tamhi samaye sumedho lokanāyakoUddharanto bahū satte deseti amataṃ padaṃ Janakāyamatikkamma vanditvā jinasāgaraṃEkaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ Tuvaṃ satthā ca ketu ca dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃParāyaṇo patiṭṭhā ca dīpo ca dipaduttamoEkavīsatimo bhāṇavāro   Nepuñño dassane vīro tāresi janataṃ tuvaṃNatthañño tārako loke tavuttaritaro mune Sakkā bhave kusaggena pametuṃ sāgaruttamoNattheva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave Tulāmaṇḍale ṭhapetvāna mahiṃ sakkā dharetaveNatveva tava paññāya pamāṇaṃ atthi cakkhuma Ākāso minitu sakkā rajjuyā aṅgulena vāNatveva tava sabbaññū sīlaṃ sakkā pametave Mahāsamudde udakaṃ ākāso ca vasundharāParimeyyāni etāni appameyyosi cakkhuma  Chahi gāthāhi sabbaññuṃ kittayitvā mahāyasaṃAñjaliṃ paggahetvāna tuṇhī aṭṭhāsahaṃ tadā  Yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti bhuripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃBhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha Yo me ñāṇaṃ pakittesi pasanno sena cetasāTamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato Sattasattatikappāni devaloke ramissatiSahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati Anekasatakkhattuñca cakkavattī bhavissatiPadesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ Devabhūto        manusso vā puññakammasamāhitoAnūnamanasaṅkappo tikkhapañño bhavissati Tiṃsakappasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati Agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajissatakiñcanoJātiyā sattavassena arahattaṃ phusissati   Yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato pattesmi sāsanaṃEtthantare na jānāmi cetanaṃ amanoramaṃ Saṃsaritvā bhave sabbe sampattānubhaviṃ ahaṃBhoge me ūnatā natthi phalaṃ ñāṇassa thomane Tivaggī nibbutā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatāSabbāsavā parikkhīṇā natthidāni punabbhavo Tiṃsakappasahassamhi yaṃ ñāṇambhithomayiṃDuggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phalaṃ ñāṇassa thomane Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ Pabbajitvāna kāyena pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃVacīduccaritaṃ hitvā nadīkule vasāmahaṃ Ekakaṃ maṃ viharantaṃ buddhaseṭṭho upāgamiNāhaṃ jānāmi buddhoti akāsiṃ paṭisantharaṃ  Karitvā paṭisanthāraṃ nāmagottamapucchahaṃDevatānusi gandhabbo ādu sakko purindado Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto mahābrahmā idhāgatoVirocesi disā sabbā udayaṃ suriyo yathā Sahassārāni        cakkāni pāde dissanti mārisaKo vā tvā kassa vā putto kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃNāmagottāṃ pavedehi saṃsayaṃ apanehi me Paṭisatthāraṃ machasaṃ  Namhi devo na gandhabbo nāpi sakko purindadoBrahmabhāvo ca me natthi etesaṃ utatamo ahaṃ Atīto visayaṃ tesaṃ dālayiṃ kāmabandhanaṃSabbe kilese jhāpetvā patto sambodhimuttamaṃ Tassa vācaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ idaṃ vacanamabraviṃYadi buddhosi sabbaññu nisīda tvaṃ mahāmuniTamhaṃ pūjayissāmi dukkhassantakaro tuvaṃ Pattharitvājinavammaṃ adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃNisīdi tattha bhagavā sīhova girigabbhare Khippaṃ pabbatamāruyha ambassa phalamaggahiṃSālakalyāṇikaṃ pupphaṃ candanaṃ ca mahārahaṃ Khippaṃ paggayha taṃ sabbaṃ upetvā lokanāyakaṃPhalaṃ buddhassa datvāna sālapupphamapūjayiṃ Candanaṃ anupimpitvā avandiṃ satthuno ahaṃPasannacitto sumano vipulāya ca pītiyā Ajinambhi nisīditvā sumedho lokanāyakoMama kammaṃ pakittesi haṃsayanto mamaṃ tadā Iminā phaladānena gandhamālehi cūbhayaṃPañcavīse kappasate devaloke ramissatiAnūnamanasaṃkappo vasavattī bhavissati Chabbisatikappasate manussattaṃ gamissatiBhavissati cakkavatti cāturanto mahiddhiko Vebhāraṃ nāma nagaraṃ vissakammena māpitaṃHessati sabbasovaṇṇaṃ nānāratanabhusitaṃ Eteneva upāyena saṃsarissati so bhaveSabbattha pūjito hutvā devatte atha mānusePacchime bhave sampatte brahmabandhu bhavissati Agārā abhinikkhamma anagāri bhavissatiAbhiññāpāragū hutvā nibbāyissatanāsavo  Idaṃ        vatvāna sambuddho sumedho lokanāyakoMama nijjhāyamānassa pakkāmi anilañjase Hāsayanto machasaṃ Pacchima bhave sīmu Nibbāyissatināsavo machasaṃ  Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ Tusitāto cavitvāna nibbattiṃ mātukucchiyaṃBhoge me ūnatā natthi yamhi gabbhe vasāmahaṃ Mātukucchigate mayhaṃ annaṃ pānañca bhojanaṃMātuyā mama chandena nibbattati yadicchakaṃ tāpasoTattha me caṅkamo āsi amanussehi māpito Jaṭābhārena bharito kamaṇḍaludharo tadāUttamatthaṃ gavosanto pavanā abhinikkhamiṃ  Cullāsasītisahassāni sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃSakakammābhipasutā vasanti pavane tadā Assamā abhinikkamma akaṃ pulinacetiyaṃNānāpupphaṃ samānetvā taṃ cetiyamapūjayiṃ Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā assamaṃ pavisāmahaṃSabbe sissā samāgantvā etamatthamapukacchu maṃ Pulinena kate thupe yaṃ tvaṃ devaṃ namassasiMayampi ñātumicchāma puṭṭho ācikkha no tuvaṃ Niddiṭṭhā no mantapade cakkhumanto mahāyasaTe kho ahaṃ namassāmi buddhaseṭṭhe mahāyase Kīdisā te mahāvīrā sabbaññu lokanāyakāKathaṃ vaṇṇā kathaṃ sīlā kīdisā te mahāyasā Khattiṃ salakkhaṇā buddhā cattārīsadvijāpi caNettā gopakhumā tesaṃ jiñjukāphalasannibhā Gacchamānā ca te buddhā yugamattaṃva pekkhareNa tesaṃ jāṇu nadati sandhisaddo na suyyati Gacchamānā ca sugatā uddharantāva gaccharePaṭhamaṃ dakkhiṇaṃ pādaṃ buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā Asambhitā ca te buddhā migarājāva kesarī nevukakkaṃsenti attānaṃ no ca vambhentipāṇinaṃ Jaṭābhārassa syā Vipīnā nikkhamiṃ tadā machasaṃ Vipine machasaṃ Etamatthaṃ pucchiṃsu maṃ machasaṃ Kato thūpo machasaṃ Deva machasaṃ Niddiṭṭhānu machasaṃ Diṭṭhāno vo syā Yugamattañca machasaṃ  Mānāvamānato muttā samā sabbesu pāṇisuAnattukkaṃsakā buddhā buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā Uppajjantā ca sambuddhā ālokaṃ dassayanti teChappakāraṃ pakampenti kevalaṃ vasudhaṃ imaṃ Passanti        nirayaṃ cete nibbāti nirayo tadāPavassati mahāmegho buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā Edisā te mahānāgā atulyā ca mahāyasāVaṇṇato anatikkantā appameyyā tathāgatā Anumodiṃsu me vāyyā sabbe sissā sagāravāTathā ca paṭipajjiṃsu yathāsatti yathābalaṃ Patipūjenti pulinaṃ sakakammābhilāsinoSaddahantā mamaṃ vākyaṃ buddhattagatamānasā Tadā cavitvā tusitā devaputto mahāyasoUppajji mātukucchismiṃ dasasahassī pakampatha sikatāthupasantikeSo dāni bhagavā satthā mātukucchimupāgami  Tesaṃ dhammakathaṃ katvā kittayitvā mahāmuniṃUyyojetvā sake sisse pallaṅkaṃ ābhujiṃ ahaṃ Balañca vata me khīṇaṃ vyādhito paramenahaṃ abhivādetvā āmaṇḍamadadiṃ phalaṃ Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi āmaṇḍassa idaṃphalaṃ Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatāNāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi himavāva samādhināĀkāso viya paññāya asaṅgo anīlo yathā Sa kadāci mahāvīro parisāsu visāradoSaccāni sampakāsesi uddharanto mahājanaṃ Tadāhi bāraṇasiyaṃ seṭṭhiputto mahāyasoĀsahaṃ dhanadhaññassa devātidevaṃ taṃ sutvā ca madhuraṃ giraṃPahāyānappake bhoge pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ Evaṃ pabbajito cāhaṃ na cirena bahussutoAhosiṃ dhammakathiko vicittapaṭibhāṇavā Mahāparisamajjhehaṃ haṭṭhacitto punappunaṃVaṇṇayiṃ hemavaṇṇassa vaṇṇaṃ vaṇṇavisārado Esa khiṇāsavo buddho anīgho chinnasaṃsayoSabbakammakkhayaṃ patto vimuttopadhisaṃkhaye Esa so bhagavā buddho esa sīho anuttareSadevakassa lokassa yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃMettacitto paricariṃ sato paññāsamāhito Tena kammavipākena cetanāpaṇīdhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ Sataṃ tīṇikkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃSatānaṃ phalaṃ Duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye atha brāhmaṇeNīce kule na jāyāmi suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ Pacchimbhave sampatte brahmabandhu ahosahaṃSāvatthiyaṃ vippakule paccājāto mahaddhane Mātā candavatī nāma Theragāthaṭṭhakathā  Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvadeTāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ brāhmaṇo sādhusammatoUpecca lokapajjotaṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ Tadā mahāparisatiṃ mahāpurisasāvakaṃhapentaṃ etadaggamhi sutvāna mudito ahaṃ Mahatā parivārena nimannetvā mahājinaṃBrāhmaṇānaṃ sahassena saha dānamadāsahaṃ Mahādānaṃ daditvāna abhivādiya nāyakaṃEkamante ṭhito haṭṭho saha dānamadāsahaṃ Tayi saddhāya me vīra adhikaraguṇena caParisā mahatī hotu nibbattassa tahiṃ tahiṃ Tadā avoca parisaṃ gajagajjitasussaroKaravīkaruto satthā etaṃ passatha brāhmaṇaṃ Hemavaṇṇaṃ mahābāhuṃ kamalānanalovanaṃUddhaggatanujaṃ haṭṭhaṃ saddhāvantaṃ guṇe mama Esa patthayate ṭhānaṃ sīhaghosassa bhikkhunoAnāgatamhi addhāne lacchite taṃ manorathaṃ Satasahasse ito kappe asadiso phusso lokagganāyako So ca sabbaṃ namaṃ hantvā vijaṭetvā mahājaṭaṃVassate amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ tappayanto sadevakaṃ Tadāhi hi bārāṇasiyaṃ rājāpaccā ahumhaseBhātaromha tayo sabbe saṃvissatthā ca rājino Ekamantaṃ machasaṃ Udaggatanujaṃ machasaṃ Saddhavatta machasaṃ Patthayi taṃ ṭhānaṃ syā Gottena machasaṃ Saṃvisaṭṭhāva machasaṃ  Vīraṅgarūpā balino saṅgāme aparājitāTadā kupitapaccanto amhe āha upapajjimha ko vādo mānusake bhave Deve mahiddhikā ahumbha mānusakamhi ko vādoSattaratanassa mahesi itthiratanaṃ ahaṃ āsiṃ Idha sañcitakusalā susamiddhakulappajāDhanañajāni ca khemā ca ahmapi ca tayo vitthataṃ Asaṅkhiyāni dipāni parivāre jalanti meYāvatā devabhavanaṃ dipālokena jotati Parammukhā nisīditvā yadi icchāmi passituṃUddhaṃ adho ca tiriyaṃ sabbaṃ passāmi cakkhunā Yāvatā abhikaṅkhāmi Mānāsaṃ dehaṃ  simu  Sucittatāva   Ahamajaja  sīmu  Tadā jinassa mātucchā mahāgotami bhikkhunīTahiṃ kate pure ramme vasi bhikkhunupassaye Bhikkhunīhi vimuttāhi satehi saha pañcahiRahogatāya tassevaṃ cittassāsi vitakkitaṃ Buddhassa parinibbāṇaṃ sāvakaggayugassa vāRāhulānandanandānaṃ nāhaṃ lacchāmi passituṃ  Paṭigaccāyusaṅkhāre ossajitvānanibbutiṃGaccheyyaṃ lokanāthena anuññātā mahesinā Tathā pañcasatānampi bhikkhunīnaṃ vitakkitaṃĀsi khemādikānampi etadeva vitakkitaṃ Bhūmicālo tadā āsi nāditā devadundubhiUpassayādhivatthayo devatā sokapiḷitāVipalannā sakaruṇaṃ tathessuni pavattayuṃ Mittā bhikkhunīyo tā hi upagantvāna gotamiṃNipacca sirasā pade idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Tattha toyalavāsittā mayamayye rahogatāSācalā calitā bhumi naditā devadundubhiParidevā ca suyanti kimatthaṃ nūna gotami Tadā avoca sā sabbaṃ yathāparivitakkitaṃTāyopi sabbā āhaṃsu yathāparivitakkati Ṃ Yadi te rucitaṃ ayye nibbāṇaṃ paramaṃ sivaṃNibbāyissāma sabbāpi buddānuññāya subabate Mayaṃ sahāva nikkhantā gharāpi va bhavāpi caSahayeva gamissāma nibbāṇapuramuttamaṃ Nibbānāya vajantinaṃ kiṃ vakkhāmiti sā vadaṃSaha sabbāhi niggacchi bhikkhunīnilayā tadā Tahiṃ yeva  syā  Citatasasāpi  machasaṃ  Paṭikacacāyusaṅkhāraṃ  machasaṃ Visajajitvāna  machasaṃ  Sukaruṇaṃ  machasaṃ  Sababā  syā  Imisasā gāthāyānanajaraṃ simu machasaṃpotthakesu buddhassa parinibbāṇāsābakaggayugasasa ca mahākassapanandānaṃ ānandarāhulāna ca ayampi gāthā dissate nasyāma potthakesu  Upassaye yādhivatthā devatā tā khamantu meBhikkhunīnilayassedaṃ pacchimaṃ dassanaṃ mama Na jarā maccu vā yattha appiyehi samāgamoPiyehi vippayogonatthi taṃ vajissaṃ asaṅkataṃ Acitarāgā taṃ sutvā vacanaṃ sugatorasāSokaṭṭā parideviṃsu aho no appapuññatā  Bhikkhunīnilayo suñño bhūto tāhi vinā ayaṃPabhāte viya tārāyo na dissanti jinorasā Nibbānaṃ gotami yāti satehi saha pañcahiNadisatehiva saha gaṅgā pañcahi sāgaraṃ Rathikāya vajantiṃ taṃ disvā saddhā upāsikāGharā nikkhamma pādesu nipacca idamabraviṃ Pasidassu mahābhoge anāthāyo vihāya noTayā na yutataṃ nibbātuṃ iccaṭṭaṃ vilapiṃsu tā Tāsaṃ sokapahāṇatthaṃ avoca madhuraṃ giraṃRuditena alaṃ puttā hāsakāloyamajja vo Pariññātaṃ mayā dukkhaṃ dukakhahetu vivajjitoNirodho me sacchikato maggo cāpi subhāvitoBhāṇavāraṃ paṭhamaṃ Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃOhito garuko bhāro bhavanetti samuhatā Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasmānagāriyaṃSo me attho anuppatto sabbasaññojanakkhayo Buddho tassa ca saddhammo anuno yāva tiṭṭhati nibbātuṃ tāva kālo me mā maṃsocatha puttikā Piyehi na viyogopi  machasaṃ  Vajajisaṃ  syā  Vajanatiyā  machasaṃ vapanatinaṃ  Yutakā  machasaṃ  Icchaṭaṭā  machasaṃ syā iccaṭṭā   Koṇḍaññānandinandādī tiṭṭhanati rāhulo jinoSukhito sahito saṅgho hatadappā ca titthiyā Okkākavaṃsassa yaso usasito māramaddanoNanu sampati kālo me nibbānatthāya puttikā Cirappabhūti yaṃ mayhaṃ patthitaṃ ajja sijjhateĀnandabherikāloyaṃ kiṃ vo assuhi puttikā Save mayi dayā atthi yadi catthi kataññutāSaddammaṭṭhitiyā sabbā kirotha viriyaṃ daḷhaṃ Thinaṃ adāsi pabbajjaṃ sambuddho yācito mayāTasmā yathāhaṃ nandissaṃ tathā tamanutiṭṭhatha Tā evamanusāsitvā bhikkhunīhi purakkhatāUpecca buddhaṃ vanditvā idaṃ vacanamabravi  Ahaṃ sugata mātā te tvaṃ ca vīra pitā mamaSaddhammasukhado nātha tayā jātambhi gotama Saṃvaḍḍhitoyaṃ sugata rūpakāyo mayā tavaAnindiyo dhammakāyo mama saṃvaḍḍhito tayā Muhutatataṇhāsamanaṃ khiraṃ tvaṃ pāyito mayāTayāhaṃ santamaccantaṃ dhammakhiraṃ hi pāyitā Vaddhanarakkhane mayhaṃ anaṇo tvaṃ mahāmunePuttakāmā thiyo yā tā labhantu tādisaṃ sutaṃ Mandhātādinarindānaṃ yā mātā sā bhavaṇṇaveNimuggāhaṃ tayā putta tāritā bhavasāgarā Rañño mātā mahesiti sulabhaṃ nāmamitthinaṃBuddamātāti yaṃ nāmaṃ etaṃ paramadullabhaṃ Tañca laddhaṃ mayā vīra paṇidhānaṃ mamaṃ tayāAnukaṃ vā mahantaṃ vā taṃ sabbaṃ puritaṃ mayā Temātā  sabbesu  Saddhammasukhada  machasaṃ  Jātāmhi  machasaṃ Saṃvadadhitoyaṃ  machasaṃ  Anindito  machasaṃ ānandiyo  syā  Dhamamatanu simu  Muhuttaṃ  machasaṃ  Dhamamakhiramapi  syā  Banadhanārakkhate machasaṃ  Aṇaṇo  machasaṃ  Yācaṃ  machasaṃ  Labhanti  machasaṃ syā theri  Parinibbātumicchāmi vihāyemaṃ kalebaraṃAnujānāhi me vīra dukkhantakara nāyaka Cakkaṅkusadhajākiṇṇe pade kamalakomalePasārehi paṇāmaṃ te karissaṃ puttapemasā Suvaṇṇarāsisaṃkāsaṃ sariraṃ kuru pākaṭaṃKatvā dehaṃ sudiṭṭhaṃ te santiṃ gacchāmi nāyaka Dvattiṃsalakkhaṇupetaṃ suppabhālaṅkataṃ tanuṃSañajhāghanāva bāla kkaṃ mātucchaṃ dassayi jino Phullāravindasaṅkāse taruṇādiccasappabheCakkaṅkite pādatale tato sā sirasā pati Paṇamāmi narādiccaṃ ādiccakulaketukaṃPacchime maraṇe mayhaṃ na taṃ ikkhāmahaṃ puno  Itthiyo nāma lokagga sabbadosakarā matāYadi ko natthi doso me khamassu karuṇākara Itthikanāñca pabbajjaṃ yamahaṃ yāciṃ punappunaṃTattha ce atthi doso me taṃ khamassu narāsabha Mayā bhikkhunīyo vīra tavānuññāya sāsitāTatu ce atthi dunatitaṃ taṃ khamassu khamādhipa Akkhante nāma khantabbaṃ kiṃ bhave guṇabhusaneKimuttaraṃ te vadakkhāmi nibbānāya vajantiyā Suddhe anune mama bhikkhusaṅgheLokā ito nisasarituṃ kamantePabhātakāle vyasanaṃ gahānaṃDisvāna niyyāti ca candalekhā Tadetarā bhikkhunīyo jinaggaṃTārāva candānugatā sumeruṃ ṭhitā mukhantaṃ samudikkhamānā Kalevaraṃ  machasaṃ  Putata utatame  machasaṃ putata pemahaṃ  syā  Saraṇaṃ syā  Yaṃ taṃ  machasaṃ  Khamāmiti  syā  Khamaneta  machasaṃ  Gatānaṃ machasaṃ  Kacca  machasaṃ  Na tittapubaṃ tava dassanenaCakkhuṃ na sotaṃ tava bhāsitenaCinnaṃ mamaṃ kevalamekamecaPappuyya taṃ dhammarasena tittiṃ Nadatoparisāyaṃ te vādidappāpahārinoYe te dakkhanti vadanaṃ dhaññā te narapuṅgava Dighaṅguli tambanakhe subhe āyatapaṇahikeYe pāde paṇamisasnati tepi dhaññā guṇandhara  Madhurāni pahaṭṭhāni dosagghāni hitāni caYe te vākyāni sossanti tepi dhaññā naruttama Dhaññāhaṃ te mahāvīra pādapujanatapparāTiṇṇasaṃsārakantārā suvākyena sirimato Tato sā anusāsetvā bhikkhusaṅghampi subbatāRāhulānandanande ca vanditvā idamabravi Āsivisālayasame rogāvāse kalebareNibbinnā dukkhasaṃghāte jarāmaraṇagecare Nānākalimalākiṇṇe parāyatte nirihakeTena nibbātumicchāmi anumaññatha puttakā Nando rāhulabhaddo ca vitasokā nirāsavāhitācalaṭṭhitithirā dhammataṃ anucintayuṃ Dhiratthu saṅkhataṃ lolaṃ asāraṃ kadalumapamaṃMāmarivisadisaṃ ittaraṃ anavaṭṭhitaṃ Yattha nāma jinassāyaṃ mātucchā buddhaposikāGotami nidhanaṃ yāti aniccaṃ sabbasaṅkhataṃ Titatipubbaṃ  machasaṃ  Vāditabbapahārino  machasaṃ  Paṇamāyanati  syā Suyyanati  machasaṃ  Sadadhammena sirimatā   Dukkhasaṅsāṭe  machasaṃdukkhasaṅkete  syā  Kalalamākiṇṇe   kuṇapamalākiṇṇe  syā   hitācalā dhītādhirā  syā   Ānando ca tadā sekho sokaṭṭo jinavacchaloTatthassuti dharanto so karunaṃ paridevati Hā santiṃ gotami yāti nūna buddhopi nibbutiṃGacchati na cireneva aggiriva nirindhano Evaṃ vilapamānaṃ taṃ anandaṃ āha gotamiSunisāgara gambhira buddhupaṭṭhānatappara Na yuttaṃ socituṃ putta hāsakāle upaṭṭhiteTava me saraṇaṃ putta nibbānaṃ samupāgataṃ Tayā tāta samajjhiṭṭho pabbajjaṃ anuni noMā putta vimano hohi saphalo te parissamo  Yaṃ na diṭṭhaṃ purāṇehi titthikācariyehi piTaṃ padaṃ sukumārihi sattavassāhi veditaṃ Buddhasāsanapāletā pacchimaṃ dassanaṃ tavaTattha gacchāmahaṃ putta gato yattha na dissate Kadāci dhammaṃ desento khipi lokagganāyako tadāhaṃ āsiṃsavacaṃ avocaṃanukampikā Ciraṃ jiva mahāvīra kappaṃ tiṭṭha mahāmuneSabbalokassa atthāya bhavassu ajarāmaro Taṃ tathāvādinaṃ buddho mamaṃ so etadabraviNa hevaṃ vandiyā buddhā yathā vandasi gotami Kathaṃ carahi sabbaññu vanditabbā tathāgatāKathaṃ avandiyā buddhā taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito Āraddhaviriye pahitatte niccaṃ daḷhaparakkameSamagge sāvake passe phasā buddhānavandanā Bhāsanti  syā  Tayā  machasaṃ  Nibabāṇanatamupāgataṃ  simu Āsiṃsavācaṃ  machasaṃ  Pasasa  machasaṃ syā  Etaṃ buddānavandanaṃmachasaṃ  Tato upassayaṃ gantvā ekikāhaṃ vicintayiṃSamaggaṃ parisaṃ nātho rocati tihavantago Handāhaṃ parinibbissaṃ mā vipattiṃ tamaddasaṃEvāhaṃ cintayitvāna disvāna isisattamaṃ Parinibbānakālaṃ me ārocesiṃ vināyakaṃTato so samanuññāsi kālaṃ jānāhi gotami Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Thinaṃ dhammābhisamaye ye bālā vimatiṃ gātāTesaṃ diṭṭhipahānatthaṃ iddhiṃ dassehi gotami Tadā nipacca sambuddaṃ upapatitvāna ambaraṃIddhi anekā dassesi buddhānuñāya gotami Ekikā bahudhā āsi bahukā cekikā tathāĀvibhāvaṃ tirobhāvaṃ tirokuḍḍaṃ tironagaṃ  Asajjamānā agamā bhumiyampi nimujjathaAbhijjamāne udake agañchi mabhiyā yathā Sakuṇiva yathākase pallaṅkena gami tadāVasaṃ vattesi kayena yāva brahmanivesanaṃ Sineruṃ daṇḍaṃ katvāna chattaṃ katvā mahāmahiṃSamulaṃ parivattetvā dhārenti caṅkami nabhe Chassurodayakāleva lokañcākāsi dhumikaṃYugante viya lokaṃ sā jālāmālākulaṃ akā Rodhesi  machasaṃ  Vipatatitamadadasaṃ  machasaṃ  Maṃ  syā  Dhārayaṃ machasaṃ  Mucalindaṃ mahāpesalaṃ meru mandāra daddare Sāsaperiva sabbāni ekenaggahi muṭṭhitā Aṅgulaggena chādesi hākaraṃ sanisākaraṃCandasurasahasasāni āvelamiva dhārayi Catusāgaratoyāni dhārayi ekapāṇināYugantajaladākāraṃ mahāvassaṃ pavasayi Cakkavattiṃ saparisaṃ māpayī sā nabhatthaleGaruḷaṃ dviradaṃ sihaṃ vinadantaṃ ca dassayī Ekikā abhinimmitvāppameyyaṃ bhikkhunīgaṇaṃPuna annaradhāpetvā ekikā munimabravi Mātucchā te mahāvīra tavasāsanakārikāAnuppattā sakaṃ atthā pade vandati cakkhuma Dassetvā vividhā iddhī orohitvā nabhatthalāVanditvā lokapajjotaṃ ekamantaṃ nisīdi sā Sā visaṃvassasatikā jātiyāhaṃ mahāmune alamettāvatā vīra nibbāyisasāmi nāyaka Tadātivimbhitā sabbā parisā sā katañajaliAvocayye kathaṃ āsi atuliddhiparakkamā  Padumuttaro nāma jito sabbadhammesu cakkhumāIto satasahassambhi kappe uppajji nāyako Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātāmaccakule ahuṃSabbupakārasampanne iddhe phīte mahaddhane Kadāci pitunā saddhiṃ dāsigaṇapurakkhatāMahatā parivārena taṃ upecca narāsabhaṃ Merumulanadaṅkare  machasaṃ meruṃ mandāradanatare  syā  Pavassatha  machasaṃ Vandāmi  machasaṃ syā  Visavassasatikā  machasaṃ  Vasavaṃ viya vassentaṃ dhammameghaṃ anāsavaṃSaradādiccasadisaṃ raṃsimālākulaṃ jinaṃ Disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā sutvā cassa subhāsitaṃMātucchaṃ bhikkhunīṃ agge ṭhapentaṃ naranāyakaṃ Sutvā datvā mahādānaṃ sattāhaṃ tassa tādinoSasaṅghassa naraggassa pavacayāni bahuni ca Nipajja pādamulambhi taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃTato mahāparisati avoca isisattamo Yā sasaṅghaṃ abhejesi sattāhaṃ lokanāyakaṃTamahaṃ nittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati Tassa dhammesu dāyadā orasā dhammanimmitāGotami nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvikā Tassa buddhassa mātucchā jīvitāpādikā ayaṃRattaññunañca aggantaṃ bhikkhunīnaṃ labhissati Taṃ sutvāna pamuditā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃPavacayehi upaṭṭhitvā tato kālakatā ahaṃ Tāvatiṃsesu dovesu sabbakāmasamiddhisuNibbatatā dasahaṅgehi aññe abhibhaviṃ ahaṃ Rūpasaddehi gandhehi rasehi phusanehi caĀyunāpi ca vaṇṇena sukhena yasasāpi ca Tathevādhipateyyena adhigayha virocahaṃAhosiṃ amarindassa mahesi dayitā tahiṃ  Saṃsāre saṃsarantihaṃ kammavāyusameritāKāsissa rañño visaye ajāyiṃ dāsagāmake Pañcadāsasatānunā nivasanti tahiṃ tadāPabbesaṃ tattha yo jeṭṭho tassā jāyā abhosahaṃ Vassantaṃ  machasaṃ  Raṃsijālasamujajalaṃ  machasaṃ syā raṃsijālakulaṃ jinaṃ   Satasahassito  machasaṃ  Nāthena  simu  Jivitepālikā  syā  Sutvāhaṃ  sīmu syā Pamoditvā  machasaṃ  Sayambhuno pañcasatā gāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisuṃTe disvāna ahaṃ tuṭṭhā saha sabbehi ñātihi Katvā pañcasatakuṭi catumāse upaṭṭhiyaTicivarāni datvāna pasananāmbha sasāmikā Tato cutā sapatikā tāvatiṃsagatā mayaṃPacchime ca bhavedāni jātā devadahe pure Pitā añajanasakko me mātā mama sulakkhaṇāTato kapilavatthūsmiṃ suddhodanagharaṃ gatā Sesā sakyakule jātā sakyānaṃ gharamāgamuṃAhaṃ visiṭṭhā sabbāsaṃ jinassapādikā ahuṃ Mama putetābhinikkhamma buddho āsi vināyakoPaccāhaṃ pabbajitvāna satehi saha pañcahi Sākiyānihi dhīrāhi saha santisukhaṃ phusiṃYe tadā pubbajātiyaṃ ambhākaṃ ahu sāmino Saha puññassa kattāro mahāsamayakārakāPhusiṃsu arahattaṃ te sugatenānukampitā Tadetarā bhikkhunīyo āruhiṃsu nabhatthalaṃSaṅgatā viya tārāyo virociṃsu mahiddhikā Iddhi anekā dassesuṃ piḷandhavikati yathāKammaro kanakasesava kammaññassa susikkhito Dassetvā pāṭihirāni vicitatāni bahuni caTosetvā vādipavaraṃ muniṃ saparisaṃ tadā Orohitvāna gaganā vanditvā isisattamaṃAnuññātā naraggena yathāṭhane nisīdisuṃ Ahonukampikā amhaṃ sabbāsaṃ vīra gotamiVāsitā tava puññehi pattā no āsavakkhayaṃ Sabbāhi itthihi  machasaṃ  Pagā hutvānava sabbayo  machasaṃ  Upaṭṭhahuṃmachasaṃ  Saṃsarimhaṃ sīmu machasaṃ  Sabbāpitā  machasaṃ  Sabbā  syā  Sa meputto  syā  Khagatā sīmu  Piḷanadhavikatiṃ  machasaṃ  Puññakammesu sikkhitā syā  Vividhāni  syā   Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi vijjatiÑāṇaṃ ambhaṃ mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike Asmāhi pariciṇṇosi mettacittāhi nāyakaAnujānāhi sabbāsaṃ nibbāsaṃ nibbānāya mahāmune Nibbāyissāma iccevaṃ kiṃ vakkhāmi vadantiyoYassadāni ca vo kālaṃ maññāthāti jinobravi Gotami ādikā tāyo tadā bhikkhunīyo jinaṃVanditvā āsanā tamhā vuṭṭhāya agamaṃsu tā Mahatā janakāyena saha lokagganāyakoAnusaṃyāsi so viro mātucchaṃ yāva koṭṭhakaṃ Tadā nipati pādesu gotami lokabandhunoSahetarāhi sabbāhi pacchimaṃ pādavandanaṃ Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ lokanāthassa dassanaṃNa puno amatākaraṃ passissāmi mukhaṃ tava Na ca me vandanaṃ vīra tava pade sukomaleSamphusissāmi lokagga ajja gacchāmi nibbutiṃ Sabbayo  syā  Vadantinaṃ  simu  Anusaṃsāvayi  syā  Sahevatāhi  machasaṃ  Rūpena kiṃ tavānena diṭṭhe dhamme yathātatheSabbaṃ saṅkhatamevetaṃ anassāsitamittaraṃ Sā tāhi saha gantvāna bhikkhunupassayaṃ sakaṃAḍḍhapallaṅkamābhujja nisīdi paramāsane Tadā upāsikā tattha buddasāsanacchalāTassā pavattiṃ sutvāna upesuṃ pādavandikā Karehi uraṃ pabhanatvā chinnamulā yathā latāRodantā karuṇaṃ rāvaṃ sokaṭṭā bhumipātikā  Mā no saraṇade nāthe vihāya gami nibbutiṃNipatitvāna yācāma sabbāyo sirasā mayaṃ Yā padānatamā tāsaṃ saddhā paññā upāsikāTassā sīsaṃ pamajjanti idaṃ vacanamabravi Alaṃ puttā visādena mārapāsānuvattināAniccaṃ saṅkhataṃ sabbaṃ viyogantaṃ calācalaṃ Tato sā tā vissajjitvā paṭhamaṃ jhānamuttamaṃDutiyaṃ tatiyaṃ cāpi samāpajji catutthakaṃ Ākāsāyatanañceva viññāṇāyatanaṃ tathāĀkiñcaññaṃ nevasaññaṃ samāpajji yathākkamaṃ Paṭilomena jhānāni samāpajjittha gotamiYāvatā paṭhamaṃ jhānaṃ tato yāva catutthakaṃ Tato vuṭṭhāya nāṭoSokenevātidino ca viravo āsi sāgaro Sā saha tāhi  machasaṃ  Ravaṃ  machasaṃ  Bhumipātitā  machasaṃ bravi pātitā Nirāsavā  machasaṃ  Sokena cātidinova machasaṃ  Devā nāgāsurā brahmā saṃviggābhaṃsu nirānando asasunā puṇṇalocanoGaggadena sarenāha samāgacchantu bhikkhavo Pubbadakkiṇapaccāsu uttarāyaṃ vasanti yeSuṇantu bhāsitaṃ mayhaṃ bhikkhavo sugatorasā Yā vaḍḍhayi payattena sarīraṃ pacchimaṃ muneSā gotami gatā santiṃ tārāva suriyodaye Budadhamātāni paññattiṃ ṭhapayitvā gatāsamaṃNa yattha pañcanettopi gataṃ dakkhati nāyako Yassatthi sugate saddhā yo ca piyo mahāmune buddhamātari sakkāraṃ karotuṃsugatoraso Suduraṭṭhāpi taṃ sutvā sighamāgañachu bhikkhavoKeci buddhānubhāvena keci iddhisu kovidā Kūṭāgagāravare ramme sabbasoṇaṇamaye subheMañcakaṃ samaropesuṃ yattha suttāsi gotami Saṃviggahiṃsu  machasaṃ  Dipasikhā  syā  Sutasāgaraṃ  machasaṃ  Gatiṃ machasaṃ  Yo vā sisso  sīmu  Buddamātussa  machasaṃ budadhassamātu  syā Samāropesuṃ  machasaṃ  Cattāro lokapālā te aṃsehi samadhārayuṃSesā sakkādayo devā kūṭāgāre samaggahuṃ Kūṭāgārāni sabbāni āsuṃ pañcasatānipiSaradādiccavaṇṇāni vissakammakatāni hi Sabbāpi tā bhikkhunīyo āsuṃ mañcesu sāyitāDevānaṃ khandhamāruḷhā niyyanti anupubbaso Sabbaso chāditaṃ āsi vitānena nabhatthalaṃSatārā candasuriyā lañachitā kanakāmayā  Patākā ussitā nekā vitatā pupphakañcukāOgatākāsapadumā mahiyā pupphamuggataṃ Dissanti candasuriyā Buddhassa parinibbānaṃ nedisaṃ āsi yādisaṃGotami parinibbānaṃ ativacchariyaṃ ahu Buddho buddhassa nibbāne nopadissati bhikkhavoBudedhā gotaminibbāne sāriputtādikā tathā Citakāni karitvāna sabbagandhamayāni teGandhacuṇṇāvakiṇṇāni jhāpayiṃsu ca tā tahiṃ Pañcasatāni hi  simu  Sabbā tāpi  machasaṃ  Dasasanti  machasaṃ  Yathāsattiṃ simu  Na buddho buddhanibbāṇe  machasaṃ  Nopaṭiyādi dukkhassantaṃ karissathātiItthaṃ sudaṃ mahāpajāpati gotami imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti Mahāpajāpati gotami theriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ  Ḍayyāñcassā  machasaṃ  Saṅketaṃ  machasaṃ syā  Ānandapassa buddhassa syā  Jānātha   viññātha  syā  Sukhaṃ  simu machasaṃ  Khemāpadānaṃ Padumuttaranāmajino sabbadhammesu cakkhumāIto satasahassambhi kappe uppajaji nāyako Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātā seṭṭhikule sahasāvakaṃ Atikkante ca santāhe mahāpaññānamuttamaṃBhikkhunīṃ etadaggambhi ṭhapesi narasārathi Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā puno tassa mahesinoKāraṃ katvāna taṃ ṭhānaṃ paṇipacca paṇidahiṃ Tato maṃ sa jino āha sijjhataṃ paṇidhi tava sasaṃghe me kataṃ kāraṃappameyyaphalaṃ tayā Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulambhavoGotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati Tassa dhammesu dāyāda orasā Bhavāmi tena kammena yogena jinasāsaneSabbā sampattiyo mayhaṃ sulabhā manaso piyā Yopi me bhavate bhattā yattha yattha gatāyapiVimāneti na maṃ koci paṭipattiphalena me Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyasoNāmena koṇāgamano uppajji vadataṃ varo Tadāhaṃ bārāṇasiyaṃ susamiddha kulapapajāDhanañajāni sumedhā ca ahampi ca tayo janā Saṅghārāmamadāsimbha dānasahāyikā pureSaṅghassa ca vihāraṃhi  syā  Dāyikā    Tato cutā mayaṃ sabbā tāvatiṃsupagā ahuṃYasasā aggataṃ pattā manussesu tatheva ca Imasmiṃ yeva kappambhi brahmabandhu mahāyesoKasasapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaroKāsirājā kiki nāma bārāṇasipuruttame Tassāsiṃ jeṭṭhikā ṭhitā samaṇi iti vissutāDhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ  Anujāni na no tāto akāreva tadā mayaṃVisavassasahassāni vicarimha atanditā Komāribrahmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukhedhitaKhuddhupaṭṭhānaniratā muditā satta dhitaro Samaṇi samaṇaguttā ca bhikkhunī bhikkhudāsikāDhammā ceva sudhammā ca sattami saṅghadāsikā Ahaṃ uppalavaṇṇā ca paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalāKisāgotami dhammadinnā visākhā hoti sattami Kadāci so narādicecā dhammaṃ deseti abbhatuṃMahānidānasuttantaṃ sutvā taṃ pariyāpuṇiṃ Tebhi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ Pacchime ca bhavedāni sāgalāyaṃ puruttameRañño madadassa dhītāmhi manāpā dayitā piyā Saha me jātamattamhi khemaṃ tamhi pure ahuTato khemāti nāmaṃ me guṇato upapajjatha Yadāhaṃ yobbanaṃ pattā rūpalāvaññabhusitāTadā adāsi maṃ tāto bimbisārassa rājino Nāthena  sīmu  Bhikkhudāyikā  machasaṃ  Saṅghadāyikā  machasaṃ Guṇitaṃ upapajjatha   Rūpalāvaṇaṇa vibhusitā  syā rūpavantā vibhusitā    Tassāhaṃ suppiyā āsiṃ rūpakelāyane ratāRūpānaṃ dosavāditi na upesiṃ mahādayaṃ Bimbisāro tadā rājā mamānuggahabuddhiyāVaṇaṇayitvā veḷuvanaṃ gāyake gāpayi mamaṃ Rammaṃ veḷuvanaṃ yena na diṭṭhaṃ sugatālayaṃNa tenana nandanaṃ diṭṭhaṃ iti maññāmase mayaṃ Yena veḷuvanaṃ diṭṭhaṃ naranandananandanaṃSudiṭṭhaṃ nandinaṃ tena amarindasunandanaṃ  Vihāya nandanaṃ devā otaritvā mahitalaṃRammaṃ veḷuvaṃ disvā na tappatti suvimhitā Rājapuññena nibbattaṃ buddhapuññena bhusitaṃKo vattā tassa nissesaṃ vanassa guṇasañcayaṃ Taṃ sutvā vanasamiddhaṃ mama sotamanoharaṃDaṭṭhukāmā tamuyyānaṃ rañño ārocayiṃ tadā Mahatā parivārena tadā ca so mahipatiMaṃ pesesi tamuyyānaṃ dassanāya samussukaṃ Gaccha passa mahābhoge vanaṃ nettarasāyanaṃYaṃ sadā bhāti siriyā sugatābhānurañajitaṃ Yadā ca piṇḍāya muni giribbajapuruttamePaviṭṭhohaṃ tadāyeva vanaṃ daṭṭhumupāgamiṃ Tadāhaṃ phullavipinaṃ nānāhamarakujitaṃKokilāgitasahitaṃ mayuragaṇanacatitataṃ Appasaddamanākiṇṇaṃ nānācaṅkamabhusitaṃKuṭimaṇḍapasaṅkiṇaṇaṃ yogivaracirājitaṃ Vicaranti amaññissaṃ saphalaṃ nayanaṃ mamaTatthāpi taruṇaṃ bhikkhuṃ yuttaṃ disvā vicintayiṃ Mahitale  syā  Maṃ  syā  Sampesesi  syā sama pāpesi    Īrisepi vane ramme ṭhitatoyaṃ navayobbaneVasantamiva kantena rūpena ca samanacito Nisitto rukkhamulambhi muṇḍo saṅghāṭipārutoJhāyate vatayaṃ bhikkhu hitvā visayajaṃ ratiṃ Nanu nāma gahaṭṭhena kāmaṃ bhutvā yathāsukhaṃPacchā jiṇeṇana dhammoyaṃ caritabebā subhaddako  Suññakatti viditvāna gandhagehaṃ jinālayaṃUpetvā jinamaddakkhiṃ udayantaṃva bhākaraṃ Ekakaṃ sukhamāsinaṃ vijamānā varitthiyāDisvānevaṃ vicintesiṃ nāyaṃ lukho narāsabho Sā kaññā kanakāhāsā padumānanalocanāBimboṭṭhi kundadasanā manonettarasāyanā Hemadolāhasavanā kalasākāra sutthatiTanumajjhā ca sussoṇi rambhoru cārubhusanā Rattaṃsukupasabyānā nilamaṭṭhanivāsanāAtappaneyyarūpena hāvabhāvasamanavitā Disvā tamevaṃ cintesi ahoyaṃ abirupiniNa mayātena nettena diṭṭhapubbā kudācanaṃ Tato jarābhubhūtā sā vivaṇaṇā vitatānanāBhinnadantā setasirā salālavadanāsuci Saṅkhittakaṇṇā setakkhi lambāsubhapayodharāVicitatasabbaṅgi sirāvitatadehini Nataṅgā daṇḍadutiyā uppaṇḍuppaṇḍukā kisāPavedhamānā patitā nissasanti muhuṃ muhuṃ Īdise vipine  machasaṃ  Vijamānaṃ  machasaṃ  Kalikākāra  machasaṃ Vedimajjhāva sussoṇi  machasaṃ vedimajjhā varasoṇi  syā  Ramemāru  syā  Ratataṃsakasusaṃvitā   Anappaneyyarūpena sīmu  Sabbābharaṇabhusitā  syā Uppāsulikatā  machasaṃ  Tato me āsi saṃvego abbhuto lomahaṃsanoDhiratthu rūpaṃ asuciṃ ramante yattha bālisā Tadā mahākāruṇiko disvā saṃviggamānasaṃUdaggacitto sugato imā gāthā abhāsatha  Āturaṃ asuciṃ putiṃ passa kheme samussayaṃUggharantaṃ paggharantaṃ bālānaṃ abhinanditaṃ Asubhāya cittaṃ bhāvehi ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃSati kāyagatā tyatthu nibbidābahulā bhava Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃAjjhattiñca bahiddhā ca kāye chandaṃ virājaya Animittañca bhāvetha mānānusayamujjahaTato mānābhisamayā upasantā carissasi Ye rāgarattānupatanti sotaṃSayaṃ kataṃ makkaṭakova jālaṃEtampi chetvāna paribbajantiAnapekkhino kāmasukhaṃ pahāya Tato kallitacittaṃ maṃ ñatvāna narasārathiMahānidānaṃ desesi suttantaṃ vinayāya me Sutvā suttantaseṭṭhaṃ taṃ pubbasaññamanussariṃTattha ṭhitāvahaṃ satti dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ Nipatitvā mahesissa pādamulamhi tāvadeAccayaṃ desanatthāya idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Nāmo te sabbadassāvi namo te karuṇākaraNamo te tiṇṇasaṃsāra namo te amataṃdada Sumano  syā  Na pekkhino  machasaṃ  Kallikacattaṃ  syā kalika citataṃ    Diṭṭhigahanapakkhantā kāmarāgavimohitāTayā sammā upāyena vinitā cinaye ratā Adassanena vibbhogā tādisānaṃ mahesinaṃAnubhonti mahādukkhaṃ sattā saṃsārasāgare Yadāhaṃ lokasaraṇaṃ araṇaṃ maraṇantaguṃNāddasāsimaduraṭṭhaṃ desayāmi tamaccayaṃ Mahāhitaṃ varadadaṃ ahitoti visaṅkitaṃNopesiṃ rūpaniratā desayāmi tamaccayaṃ  Tadā madhuraniggoso mahākāruṇiko jinoAvoca tiṭṭha khemetati siñcanto amatena maṃ Tadā paṇamya sirasā katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃGantvā disvā narapatiṃ idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Aho sammāupāyo te cintitoyamarindamaVanadassanakāmāya diṭṭho nibbānedo muni Yadi te ruccate rāja sāne tassa tādinoPabbajissāmi rūpehaṃ nibbintā munivāṇinā Bhāṇavāraṃ dutiyaṃ  Añajali paggahetvāna tadāha sa mahipatiAnujānāmi te bhadde pabbajjā tava sijjhatu Pabbajitvā tadācāhaṃ addhamāse upaṭṭhiteDipodayañña bhedañca disvā saṃviggamānasā Nibbittā sabbasaṅkhāre paccayākārakovidāCaturoghe atikkamma arahattamapāpuṇiṃ Iddhiyā ca vasi āsiṃ dibbāya sotadhātuyāCetopariyañāṇassa vasi cāpi bhavāmahaṃ Pakkhandā  machasaṃ  Maraṇanatagaṃ  syā  Desessāmi  syā  Rājā  syā Munibhāṇinā  syā  Satatamāse  syā   Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃSabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva caParisuddhaṃ mama ñāṇaṃ uppannaṃ buddhasāsane Kusalāhaṃ visuddhisu kathāvatthu visāradāAbhidhammanayaññu ca vasippattāmbhi sāsane Tato bhojanavatthusamiṃ raññā kosasāmināPucchitā nipuṇe pañhe vyākaronti yathātathaṃ Tadā sa rājā sugataṃ upasaṅkamma pucchathaTatheva buddho vyākāsi yathā te vākatā mayā Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃMahāpaññānamaggāti bhikkhunīnaṃ naruttamo  Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ khemā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti Khemātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ  Uppalavaṇṇāpadānaṃ Bhikkhunī uppalavaṇṇā iddhiyā pāramiṅgatāVanditvā satthuno pāde idaṃ vacanamabravi Nittiṇṇā jātisaṃsāraṃ pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃSabbadukkhaṃ mayā khiṇaṃ arocemi mahāmuni Yāvatā parisā atthi pasannā jānasāsaneYesañca meparadhotthi khamantu jānasammukhā Saṃsāre saṃsarantāya khalitaṃ me sace bhaveĀrocemi vahāvira aparādhaṃ khamassu taṃ Toraṇavatthusaciṃ  machasaṃ sya  Jātisaṃsārā  machasaṃ  Yasā ca  machasaṃ Saṃsaranatiyā  machasaṃ saṃsaranatā me  syā  Me  syā  Iddhiṃ cāpi nidassehi mama sāsanakārikeCatasso parisā ajja kaṃkhaṃ jindāhi yāvatā Dhitu tuyahaṃ mahāvīra paññāvanta jutijharaBahuṃ ca dukkaraṃ kammaṃ kataṃ me atidukkaraṃ Uppalasseva me vaṇṇo nāmenuppalanāmikāSāvikā te mahāvīra pade vandati cakkhuma Rāhulo ca ahañceva nekajātisate bahuEkasmiṃ sambhave jātā samānacchandamānasā Nibbatti ekato hoti jātisu bahuso mamaPacchimabhave sampatte ubhopi nānāsambhāvā Putto ca rāhulo nāma dhītā uppalasavhayāpassa vira mamaṃ iddhiṃ balaṃ dassemi satthuno  Mahāsamudde caturo pakkhipi hathepātiyaṃTelaṃ hatthagataṃ ceva vejjo komārako yathā Ubbattayitvā paṭhaviṃ pakkhipi hatthapātiyaṃCittamuñajaṃ yathā nāma luñci komārako yuvā Cakakavāḷasamaṃ pāṇiṃ chādayitvāna matthakeVassāpetvāna phusitaṃ nānāvaṇaṇaṃ punappunaṃ Bhumiṃ udukkhalaṃ katvā dhaññaṃ katvāna sakkharaṃSineru musalaṃ katvā maddi komārikā yathā Dhitāhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa nāmenuppalasavahayāAbhiññāsu vasibhūtā tava sāsanakārikā Nānā vikubbaṇaṃ katvā dassetvā lokanāyakaṃNāmagottañca sāvetvā pāde vandāmi vakkhuma Dhītā  machasaṃ  Jātiyāpi ca ekato  machasaṃ syā  Pacchime bhave machasaṃ  Vatthigataṃ  simu  Khiḍḍo  machasaṃ  Cittaṃ muñajaṃ machasaṃ Pakāsetvā  syā  Iddhiyā ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyāCetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmune Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃSabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva caÑāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ pabhāvena mahesino Purimānaṃ jinaggānaṃ sammukhā ca parammukhāAdhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmuni Yaṃ mayā puritaṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sara me muniTavatthāya mahāvīra puññaṃ upacitaṃ mayā Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā parivajjenti anācāraṃTavatthāya mahāvīra cattaṃ jīvitamuttamaṃ Asakoṭisahassāni adāsiṃ mama jīvitaṃPariccantaṃ ca me hoti tavatthāya mahāmuni Tadātivimhitā sabbā sirasāva katañajaliAvocayye kathaṃ āsi atuliddhiparakkamā  Satasahasse ito kappe nāgakaññā ahuṃ tadāVimalā namā nāmena kaññānaṃ sādhusammatā Mahorago mahānāgo pasanto jinasāsanePadumuttaraṃ mahātejaṃ nimantesi sasāvakaṃ Ratanāmayaṃ maṇḍapañca pallaṅkaṃ ratanāmayaṃRatana vālukākiṇṇaṃ upabhogaṃ ratanāmayaṃ Maggaṃ ca paṭiyādesi ratanaddhajabhusitaṃPaccuggantvāna sambuddhaṃ vajjanto turiyehi so Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇā  machasaṃ  saṅgamaṃ te nidassitaṃ  machasaṃ  Purimaṃ  syā Saṃsāre   Vāranto  machasaṃ paripācento  syā  Anācaraṃ  machasaṃsyā  Mayhaṃ  simu  Pariccattā  machasaṃ  Homi  machasaṃ  Satasahasasito machasaṃ  Ahaṃ  machasaṃ  Ratanamayaṃ machasaṃ  Ratanaṃ  machasaṃ Turiyehi  machasaṃ  Parisāhi catūhi sahito lokanāyakoMahoragassa bhavane nisīdi paramāsane Annaṃ pānaṃ khādaniyaṃ bhojaniyaṃ mahārahaṃVaraṃ varañca pādāsi nāgarājā mahāyaso Bhuñjitvāna sambuddho pattaṃ dhoviya yonisoAnumodaniyaṃkāsi nāgarañño mahiddhino Sabbaññuṃ phullitaṃ disvā nāgakaññā mahāyasāPasannā satthuno cittaṃ sunibaddhañca mānasaṃ Mamañca ñcittamaññāya jalajuttamanāyakoTasmiṃ khāṇe mahāvīro bhikkhunīṃ dassayiddhiyā Iddhi anekā dasessi bhikkhunī sā visāradāPameditā vedajātā sathoraṃ idamabraviṃ Addasāhaṃ imaṃ iddhiṃ sumanāyitarāyapiKathaṃ ahosi sā vīra iddhiyā suvisāradā Orasā mukhato jātā dhītā mama mahiddhikāMamānusāsanikarā iddhiyā suvisāradā Buddhassa vacanaṃ sutvā evaṃ patthesahaṃ tadāAmpi tādisā homi iddhiyā suvisāradā  Pameditāhaṃ sumanā pattauttamamānasāAnāgatamhi addhāne īdisā homi nāyaka Maṇimayamhi pallaṅke maṇḍapasmiṃ pabhaṅkareAnnapānena tappetvā sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ Parisāhi ca catūhi  machasaṃ parisāhi ca tasesāhi   Parivuto  machasaṃpharito syā pareto   Bhojanañca  machasaṃ  Mahāyasaṃ  machasaṃ  Dhovitvā machasaṃ  Nāgakaññā mahiddhikā  machasaṃ  syā  Sabbañakaduphullitaṃ simu  Sahāyasaṃ machasaṃ  Pasannaṃ  machasaṃ  Idamabravi  machasaṃ Sumanaṃ itarāyapi  machasaṃ  Tuṭeṭhā evaṃ avocahaṃ  syā  Patte uttama mānasā machasaṃ  Nāgānaṃ pavaraṃ pupphaṃ aruṇaṃ nāma uppalaṃVaṇaṇaṃ me īdisaṃ hota pujesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ Tato cutāhaṃ manuje upapannā sayambhunoUppalehi paṭicchannaṃ piṇḍapātamadāhaṃ Ekanavute ito kappe vipassī nāma nāyakoUppajji cāru nayano sabbadhammesu cakkhumā Seṭṭhi dhītā tadā hutvā bārāṇasipuruttameNimantetvāna sambuddhaṃ sasaṅghaṃ lonāyakaṃ Mahādānaṃ daditvāna uppalehi vināyakaṃPujayitvā cetasāva vaṇṇasohaṃ apatthayaṃ Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyasoKassapo nāma gottena uppajji vacataṃ varo Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaroKāsirājā kikī nāma bārāṇasipuruttame Tassāsiṃ dutiyā dhītā samaṇaguttasamavhayāDhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ Anujāni na no tāto agāreva tadā mayaṃVisaṃ vassasahassāni vicarimbha atanditā Komāribuhmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukhedhitāBuddhupaṭṭhānaniratā muditā sattadhitaro Samaṇi samaṇaguttā ca bhikkhunī bhikkhudāsikāDhammā ceva sudhammā ca sattami saṅghadāsikā Ahaṃ khemā ca sappaññā paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalāKisāgotami dhammadinnā visākhā hoti tassamī Ca tebheva  syā  Nāmena  simu  Dāyikā  machasaṃ    Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ Tato cutā manusessu upapannā mahākulePītamaṭṭhaṃ varaṃ dusasaṃ adaṃ arahato ahaṃ Tato cutāriṭṭhapure jātā vippakule ahaṃDhitā tiriṭavacchassa ummādanti manoharā Tato cutā janapade kule aññatare ahaṃPasutā nātiphitambhi sāliṃ gopemahaṃ tadā Disvā paccekasambuddhaṃ pañcalājāsatānahaṃDatvā padumachantāni pañcaputtasatānipi Patthesiṃ tepi patthesuṃ madhuṃ datvā sayambhunoTato cutā araññehaṃ ajāyiṃ padumodare Kāsirañño mahesihaṃ hutvā sakkatapujitāAjaniṃ rājaputtānaṃ anunaṃ satapañcakaṃ Yadā te yobbatappattā kiḷantā jalakiḷitaṃDisvā opattapadumaṃ āsuṃ paccekanāyakā Sāhaṃ tehi vinābhūtā sutavarehi sokiniCutā isigilipasse gāmakambhi ajāyisaṃ Yadā cuddhā sutamati sutānaṃ bhattunopi caYāgumādāya gacchanti aṭṭhapaccekanāyake Bhikkhāya gāmaṃ gacchante disvā putte anussariṃDhiradhārā viniggacchi tadā me puttapemasā Tato tesaṃ adaṃ yāguṃ pasannā sehi pāṇihiTo vutāhaṃ tidase nandanaṃ upapajjahaṃ Anubhotvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ saṃsaritvā bhavābhaveTavatthāya mahāvīra pariccattañca jīvitaṃ  Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ sampatti ca bahubbidhāPacchime bhave sampatte jātā sāvatthiyaṃ pure Pitaṃ maṭṭhaṃ  machasaṃ  Tiriṭivacchassa  machasaṃ  Ummādenti  simu  Mahādhane seṭṭhikule sukhite sajjite tathāNānāratanapajjote sabbakāmesamiddhiti Sakkatā pujitā āsiṃ mānitāpacitā tathāRūpasobhaggasampannā kulesu abhisammatā Ativa patthitā cāsiṃ rūpabhoga sirihi caPatthitā seṭṭhiputtehi anekehi satehi ca Agāraṃ pajahitvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃAḍḍhamāse asampatte arahattamapāpuṇiṃ Iddhiyā abhinimmitvā caturassarathaṃ ahaṃBuddhassa pade vandissa lokanāthassa sirimato Supupphitaggaṃ upagamma bhikkhunī ekā tuvaṃ tiṭṭhasi sālamuleNa catthi te dutiyā vaṇṇadhātu bale na tvaṃ bhāyasi dhuttakānaṃ Sataṃ sahassānapi dhuttakānaṃ idhāgatā tādisakā bhaveyyuṃLomaṃ na icajāmi na santasāmi na māra bhāyāmi Phasā antaradhāyāmi kucchiṃ vā pavisāmi tePakhumantarikāyempi tiṭṭhantiṃ maṃ na dakkhasi Vittasmiṃ vasibhūtambhi iddhipādā subhāvitāSabbabandhanamuttāmbhi na taṃ bhāyāmi āvuso Sattisulupamā kāmā khandhāsaṃ adhikuṭṭanāYaṃ tvaṃ kāmaratiṃ brūsi aratidāni sā mama  Sabbattha vihatā nandi tamondho padāḷitoEvaṃ jānāhi pāpima nihato tvamasi antaka  Jino tamhi guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃAggā iddhimatinanti parisāsu vināyako Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃOhito garuko bhāro bhavanetti samuhatā Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasmānagāriyaṃSo me attho anuppatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo Civaraṃ piṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃKhaṇena upanāmenti sahassāni samantato Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ uppalavaṇṇā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti Uppalavaṇṇā theriyāpadānaṃ navamaṃ Paṭācārāpadānaṃ Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāraguIto satasahassambhi kappe uppajji nāyako Tadāhaṃ saṃsavatiyaṃ jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃNānāratanapajjote mahāsukhasamappitā Upevo taṃ mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃTato jātappasādāhaṃ upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ Tato vinayadhārinaṃ aggaṃ vaṇeṇasi nāyakoBhikkhunīṃ lajjaniṃ tādiṃ kappākappavisāradaṃ Tadā muditacittāhaṃ taṃ ṭhānamabhikaṅkhiniNimantetvā dasabalaṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ Bhojayitvāna sattāhaṃ daditvā ca ticivaraṃNipacaca sirasā pade idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Daditvāna ticivaraṃ  machasaṃ daditvā pattacivaraṃ  syā  Yā tayā vaṇṇitā vīra ito aṭṭhamakehaniTādisāhaṃ bhavissāmi yadi sijjhati nāyaka  Tadā avoca maṃ satthā bhadde mā bhāyi assasaAnāgatambhi addhāne lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ Satasahasse ito kappe okakākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma gotattena satthā loke bhavissati Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitāPaṭācārāti nāmana hessisa satthusāvākā Tadāhaṃ muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tato jinaṃMenannacittā paricaraṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatisaṃ agacchahaṃ Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe gantvā sāmi sappena mārito Tadā vijātadukkhena anāthā kapaṇā ahaṃKunnadiṃ puritaṃ disvā gacchanti sakulālayaṃ Bālaṃ ādāya atariṃ parakule ca ekakaṃSāyetvā bālakaṃ puttaṃ itaraṃ tāraṇāyahaṃ Nivattā ukkusohāsi taruṇaṃ vilapantakaṃItarañca vahī soto sāhaṃ sokasamappitā Sāvathinegaraṃ gantvā assosiṃ sajane mateTadā avocaṃ sokaṭṭā mahāsokasamappitā Ubho puttā kālakatā panthe mayhaṃ pati matoMātā pitā ca hātā ca ekacitakasmiṃ ḍayhara Tadā kisā ca paṇḍu ca anāthā dinamānasāIto tato hamantihaṃ addasaṃ narasārathiṃ Sārapatiṃ  machasaṃ  Okkhāmi  machasaṃ  icchāmi  syā  Nārocesiṃ patiṃ machasaṃ syā  Gacchanatihaṃ  syā  Tato avoca maṃ satthā putto mā soci assasaAttānaṃ tvaṃ gavesassu kiṃ niratthaṃ vihaññasi Na satti puttā tāṇāya na pitā napi bandhavāAntakenādhipannassa natthi ñātisu tāṇatā Taṃ vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ paṭācārā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti Paṭācārātheriyāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ Te  sabbattha   Kuṇḍalakesāpadānaṃ machasaṃkhaliṃpaccārahaṃ  syā mālapacchāhataṃ        Tadāhaṃ paṇamitvāna bhattukaṃ sukatañjaliRakkhanti attano pāṇaṃ idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ Idaṃ suvaṇṇaṃ keyuraṃ muttā veḷuriyā bahuSabbaṃ harassu bhaddante mañca dāsiti sāvaya Oropayassu kalyāṇi mā bāḷhaṃ paridevasiNa cāhaṃ abhijānāmi ahanatvā dhanamābhataṃ Yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato pattasmi viññataṃNa cāhaṃ abhijānāmi aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā Ehi taṃ upaguhissaṃ kassañca taṃ padakkhiṇaṃNa vadāni puno atthi mama tuyhañca saṅgamo Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu puriso hoti paṇḍitoItthipi paṇḍitā hoti tattha tattha vivakkhaṇā Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu puriso hoti paṇḍitoItthipi paṇḍitā hoti lahuṃ atthavicintakā  Lahuñca vata khippañca nikiṭṭhesamacetayiṃMigamuṇaṇā yathā evaṃ tadāhaṃ sattukaṃ vadhiṃ Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ na khippamanukhujjhatiSo bhaññate mandamati corova girigabbhare Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ khippameva nibodhatiMuccate sattusambadhā tadāhaṃ sattukā yathā Tadā taṃ pātayitvāna giriduggamhi sattukaṃSattikaṃ setavatthānaṃ upetvā pabbajiṃ ahaṃ Saṇḍāsena ca kese me luñcitvā sabbaso tadāPabbājetvā sasamayaṃ ācikkhiṃsu nirantaraṃ Katvāna  sīmu machasaṃ  Taṃ vadāmi puna natthi  syā  So  mano  Muhutatamapicintaye  mano  Nikaṭṭhe  si anujānetvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃNa cireneva kālena arahattamapāpuṇiṃ Tadā upāsako so maṃ upagantvā apucchathaGambhire nipuṇe paññe te sabbe vyākariṃ ahaṃ Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi
