bhāro bhavanettisamuhatā Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasamānagāriyaṃSo me attho anupapatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo Anujāni no  machasaṃ  Samidadhine  machasaṃ  Sabbakāmisamiddhane  Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyāParacittāni jānāmi satthu sāsanakārikā Pubbanivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃKhepetvā āsave sabbe visuddhāmhi sunimmalā Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ dhammadinnā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti Dhammadinnātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ  Sakulāpadānaṃ Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāraguIto satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako Hitāya sabbasattānaṃ sukhāya vadataṃ varoAtthāya purisājañño paṭipanno sadevake  Yasaggappatto simā vaṇṇakittibhattājinoPujito sabbalokassa disā sabbāsu vissuto Uttiṇṇavicikiccho so vitivattakathaṃkathoSampuṇaṇamanasaṅkappo patto sambodhimuttamaṃ Anuppantassa maggassa uppādetā naruttamoAnakkhātañca akkhāsi asasañajātañca sañajati Maggañcu ca maggavidu maggakkhāyi nanarāsabhoMaggassa kusalo satthā sārathinaṃ varuttamo Mahākaruṇiko satthā dhammaṃ desesi nāyakoNimugge kāmapaṅkambhi samuddharati pāṇino Kittivaṇaṇagato  machasaṃ  Tadā mahākāruṇiko  simu  Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātā khattinandanāSurūpā sadhanā cāsiṃ dayitā ca sirimati Ānandassa mahārañño dhītā paramasobhanāVemātubhagini cāpi padumuttaranāmino Rājakaññāhi sahitā sabbabharaṇabhusitāUpagamma mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ Tadā hi so lokagaru bhikkhunīṃ dibbacakkhukaṃKittayaṃ parisāmajjhe aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi taṃ Suṇitvā tamahaṃ haṭṭhā dānaṃ datvāna santhunoPujetvāna ca sambuddhaṃ dibbacakkhuṃ apatthayiṃ Tato avoca maṃ satthā nande lacchasi patthitaṃPadipadhammadānānaṃ phalametaṃ sunicchitaṃ Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitāSakulā nāma hessasi satthusāvikā  Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyasoKassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo Paribbājakini āsiṃ tadāhaṃ ekacāriniBhikkhāya vicaritvāna alabhiṃ telamattakaṃ Tena dīpaṃ padipetvā upaṭṭhiṃ sabbasaṃvariṃCetiyaṃ dipadaggassa vippasannena cetasā Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ Vemātā  machasaṃ  Upāgamma  machasaṃ  Catuparisāya majjhe  syā Pujitvāna  machasaṃ  Tadā  simu  Sakulāti ca  syā  Davipadagagasasa  machasaṃ  Yattha yatthupapajjāmi tassa kammassa vāhasāPajjalanti mahādipā tattha tattha gatāya me Tirokuḍḍaṃ tiroselaṃ samatiggayha pabbataṃPassāmahaṃ yadiccāmi dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Visuddhanayanā homi yasasā ca jalāmahaṃSaddhāpaññāvati ceva dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ Paccime ca havedāni jātā vippakule ahaṃPahutadhanadhaññamhi mudite rājapujite Ahuṃ sabbaṅgasampannā sabbābharaṇabhusitāPurappavese sugataṃ vātapāne ṭhitā ahaṃ Disvā jalantaṃ yasasā devamānusa sakkataṃAnubyañajana sampannaṃ lakkhaṇehi vibhusitaṃ Udaggacittā sumanā pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃNa cireneva kālena arahattamapāpuṇiṃ Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyāParacittāni jānāmi satthusāsanakārikā Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃKhepetvā āsave sabbe visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā Pariciṇṇo mahā satthā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃOhito garukobhāro bhavanetti samuhatā  Yassatthāya pabbajitā agārasmānagāriyaṃSo me attho anuppatto tibbasaṃyojanakkhayo Tato mahākāruṇino etadagge ṭhapesi maṃDibbacakkhukinaṃ aggā sakulāti naruttamo Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatāNāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santikeTisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhimeChaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃItthaṃ sudaṃ sakulā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti Sakulātheriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ  Saṃjalanti  syā saṃvaranti   Pasāyāmihaṃ  simu  Ahaṃ  machasaṃ Devamanusasa  machasaṃ  Anuvyañajana  simu  Nandājanapadakalyāṇi apadānaṃ Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāraguIto satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako Ovādako viññāpako kārako sabbajāṇinaṃDesanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ Anukampako kāruṇiko hitesi sabbapāṇinaṃSampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasile patiṭṭhahi Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññakaṃ titthiyehi caVicinnaṃ arahantehi vasibhutehi tādihi Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuniKañcanagghiyasaṅkāso khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvadeTāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃNānāratatapajjota mahāsukhasamappite Upetvā taṃ mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃAmataṃ paramassādaṃ paramatthanivedakaṃ Tadā nimantayitvāna sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃDatvā tassa mahādānaṃ pasantā sehi pāṇihi  Jhāyininaṃ bhikkhunīnaṃ aggaṭṭhānaṃ apatthayiṃNipacca sirasā viraṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ Tadā adantadamako tilokasaraṇo pabhuVyākāsi narasaddulo lacchase taṃ pasupatthitaṃ Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavoGotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati Tibhavatatagaṃ   Byākāsi narasārathi  machasaṃ  sārathi Piṭuva  Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitāNandāti nāma hessasi satthusāvikā Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃMettacittā paricariṃ paccayehi vināyakaṃ Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi caJahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ Tato cutā yāmamagaṃ tatohaṃ tusitaṃ agaṃTato ca nimmāṇaratiṃ vasavattipuraṃ tato Yattha yatthupapajjāmi tassa kammassa vāhasāTattha tattheva rājānaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ Tato cutā manussatte rājānaṃ cakkavattinaṃMaṇḍalinañca rājānaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna devesu manujesu caSabbattha sukhitā hutvā nekakappesu saṃsariṃ Pacchime bhave sampatte purambhi kapilavhayeRañño suddhodanassāhaṃ dhītā āsiṃ aninditā Siriṃva rūpiniṃ disvā nanditaṃ āsi taṃ kulaṃTena nandati me nāmaṃ sundaropapadaṃ ahu Yuvatinañca sabbāsaṃ kalyāṇiti ca vissutāTasmimpi nagare ramme ṭhapetvā ca yasodharā Jeṭṭho hātā tilokaggo pacchimo arahā tathāEkānini gahaṭṭhāhaṃ mātarā paricoditā  Sākiyamhi kule jātā putte buddhānujā tuvaṃNandenapi vinā bhūtā agāre kinnu vacchasi Gatā  machasaṃ  Gatā  syā  Suramme  simu machasaṃ  Siriyā machasaṃ Sundaraṃ pavaraṃ  machasaṃ  sundarā pavarā  syā kāmalālasaṃNibbindanatheṃ rūpasmiṃ mama cakkhupathe jino Sakena anubhāvena itthiṃ māpesi sobhaniṃDassaniyaṃ suruciraṃ mamatopi surūpiniṃ Tamahaṃ vimhitā disvā ativimhitadehiniṃCittahayiṃ saphalaṃ meti parikkhittā avataṃsā sunimmitāUssitāni paṭākāni ratanāni virocare Surattaṃ sukataṃ cetaṃ cetiyaṃ ratanāmayaṃAtirocati vaṇeṇana sasañejhāva divākare Jotayitvā so  simu thea  Veneyyaṃ  machasaṃ  Cātiyo  syā  Jotante  syā Pujanatthāya  machasaṃ pujāya  syā  Avaṭaṃsā  machasaṃ  Vitakaṃ  machasaṃ Sasañjhāva  syā   Thupassa vediyo tisso haritālena purayiEkaṃ manosilāyekaṃ añajanena ca ekikaṃ ca no sabbaṃ pariccatataṃ mahāmune Sadevake  simu  Sabbā patibhonti   Bhāvanaṃ ca subhāvitaṃ   Mayaṃ   Gandhaṃ vilepanaṃ mālaṃ dipaṃ ca ratanāmayaṃYaṃ kiñci patthitaṃ sabbaṃ pariccattaṃ mahāmune Aññaṃ nāyakoUppajjitvā mahāñāṇi tadāpi ca tathevahaṃ Pabbajitvā dhammadharā jotayiṃ jinasāsanaṃGantvā marupuraṃ rammaṃ anubhosiṃ mahāsukhaṃ Imamhi bhaddake kappe kakusandho jinuttamoUppajji narasaddulo
